Act Wisely: Cultivating Meta-Cognitive Tool Use in Agentic Multimodal Models
Authors: Shilin Yan, Jintao Tong, Hongwei Xue, Xiaojun Tang, Yangyang Wang, Kunyu Shi, Guannan Zhang, Ruixuan Li, Yixiong Zou
First: 2026-04-09T17:59:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T17:59:57+00:00
Comments: Project Page: https://Accio-Lab.github.io/Metis
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
The advent of agentic multimodal models has empowered systems to actively interact with external environments. However, current agents suffer from a profound meta-cognitive deficit: they struggle to arbitrate between leveraging internal knowledge and querying external utilities. Consequently, they frequently fall prey to blind tool invocation, resorting to reflexive tool execution even when queries are resolvable from the raw visual context. This pathological behavior precipitates severe latency bottlenecks and injects extraneous noise that derails sound reasoning. Existing reinforcement learning protocols attempt to mitigate this via a scalarized reward that penalizes tool usage. Yet, this coupled formulation creates an irreconcilable optimization dilemma: an aggressive penalty suppresses essential tool use, whereas a mild penalty is entirely subsumed by the variance of the accuracy reward during advantage normalization, rendering it impotent against tool overuse. To transcend this bottleneck, we propose HDPO, a framework that reframes tool efficiency from a competing scalar objective to a strictly conditional one. By eschewing reward scalarization, HDPO maintains two orthogonal optimization channels: an accuracy channel that maximizes task correctness, and an efficiency channel that enforces execution economy exclusively within accurate trajectories via conditional advantage estimation. This decoupled architecture naturally induces a cognitive curriculum-compelling the agent to first master task resolution before refining its self-reliance. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that our resulting model, Metis, reduces tool invocations by orders of magnitude while simultaneously elevating reasoning accuracy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：明智行动：在具身多模态模型中培养元认知工具使用能力
具身多模态模型的出现使系统能够主动与外部环境交互。然而，当前智能体存在严重的元认知缺陷：难以在利用内部知识与查询外部工具之间进行权衡，常陷入盲目调用工具的困境——即使原始视觉语境足以解决问题，仍会反射性地执行工具调用。这种病态行为导致严重的延迟瓶颈，并引入干扰噪声破坏有效推理。现有强化学习方案试图通过惩罚工具使用的标量化奖励来缓解此问题，但这种耦合式设计造成了不可调和的优化困境：严厉惩罚会抑制必要的工具使用，而温和惩罚在优势归一化过程中会被准确率奖励的方差完全淹没，无法遏制工具滥用。为突破此瓶颈，我们提出HDPO框架，将工具效率从竞争性标量目标重构为严格的条件性目标。通过摒弃奖励标量化，HDPO维持两个正交优化通道：最大化任务准确率的精度通道，以及通过条件优势估计在准确轨迹中强制实现执行效率的经济性通道。这种解耦架构自然形成认知课程——迫使智能体先掌握任务解决能力，再提升自主性。大量实验表明，我们最终构建的Metis模型在将工具调用量降低数个数量级的同时，显著提升了推理准确率。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the meta-cognitive deficit in agentic multimodal models, where agents often blindly invoke external tools even when the visual context provides sufficient information, leading to latency and reasoning noise. The proposed method, HDPO, reframes tool efficiency as a conditional rather than competing objective, decoupling optimization into separate channels for task accuracy and execution economy to enforce efficiency only within accurate trajectories. Experimental results show that the resulting model, Metis, drastically reduces tool usage while simultaneously improving reasoning accuracy.
本文针对智能多模态代理模型存在的元认知缺陷问题展开研究，即代理经常盲目调用外部工具，即使视觉上下文已包含足够信息，这导致延迟和推理噪声。提出的HDPO方法将工具效率重新定义为条件性目标而非竞争性目标，通过解耦优化为任务准确性和执行经济性两个独立通道，仅在准确轨迹中强制提升效率。实验结果表明，所得模型Metis大幅减少了工具调用次数，同时提高了推理准确性。
OpenVLThinkerV2: A Generalist Multimodal Reasoning Model for Multi-domain Visual Tasks
Authors: Wenbo Hu, Xin Chen, Yan Gao-Tian, Yihe Deng, Nanyun Peng, Kai-Wei Chang
First: 2026-04-09T17:59:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T17:59:39+00:00
Comments: code at: https://github.com/uclanlp/openvlthinker
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has emerged as the de facto Reinforcement Learning (RL) objective driving recent advancements in Multimodal Large Language Models. However, extending this success to open-source multimodal generalist models remains heavily constrained by two primary challenges: the extreme variance in reward topologies across diverse visual tasks, and the inherent difficulty of balancing fine-grained perception with multi-step reasoning capabilities. To address these issues, we introduce Gaussian GRPO (G$^2$RPO), a novel RL training objective that replaces standard linear scaling with non-linear distributional matching. By mathematically forcing the advantage distribution of any given task to strictly converge to a standard normal distribution, $\mathcal{N}(0,1)$, G$^2$RPO theoretically ensures inter-task gradient equity, mitigates vulnerabilities to heavy-tail outliers, and offers symmetric update for positive and negative rewards. Leveraging the enhanced training stability provided by G$^2$RPO, we introduce two task-level shaping mechanisms to seamlessly balance perception and reasoning. First, response length shaping dynamically elicits extended reasoning chains for complex queries while enforce direct outputs to bolster visual grounding. Second, entropy shaping tightly bounds the model's exploration zone, effectively preventing both entropy collapse and entropy explosion. Integrating these methodologies, we present OpenVLThinkerV2, a highly robust, general-purpose multimodal model. Extensive evaluations across 18 diverse benchmarks demonstrate its superior performance over strong open-source and leading proprietary frontier models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OpenVLThinkerV2：面向多领域视觉任务的通用多模态推理模型
群体相对策略优化（GRPO）已成为推动多模态大语言模型近期发展的实际强化学习目标。然而，将这一成功扩展到开源多模态通用模型仍面临两大主要挑战：不同视觉任务间奖励拓扑的极端差异，以及平衡细粒度感知与多步推理能力的内在困难。为解决这些问题，我们提出了高斯GRPO（G²RPO），这是一种用非线性分布匹配替代标准线性缩放的新型强化学习训练目标。通过数学上强制任何给定任务的优势分布严格收敛于标准正态分布𝒩(0,1)，G²RPO从理论上确保了任务间梯度均衡性，减轻了对重尾异常值的脆弱性，并为正负奖励提供对称更新。利用G²RPO提供的增强训练稳定性，我们引入了两种任务级塑形机制以无缝平衡感知与推理：首先，响应长度塑形动态激发复杂查询的扩展推理链，同时强制直接输出以增强视觉基础；其次，熵塑形紧密约束模型的探索区域，有效防止熵崩溃和熵爆炸。综合这些方法，我们提出了OpenVLThinkerV2——一个高度鲁棒的通用多模态模型。在18个多样化基准测试中的广泛评估表明，其性能优于强大的开源模型及领先的专有前沿模型。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the challenges of applying Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to open-source multimodal generalist models, specifically the high variance in reward structures across visual tasks and the difficulty of balancing perception with reasoning. The method introduces Gaussian GRPO (G²RPO), a novel reinforcement learning objective that uses non-linear distributional matching to enforce a standard normal advantage distribution, alongside two task-level shaping mechanisms for response length and entropy to balance reasoning depth and visual grounding. The main experimental results show that the resulting model, OpenVLThinkerV2, achieves superior performance across 18 diverse benchmarks, outperforming both strong open-source and leading proprietary models.
本研究的动机是解决将组相对策略优化（GRPO）应用于开源多模态通用模型时面临的主要挑战，即不同视觉任务间奖励结构的极端差异以及平衡细粒度感知与多步推理能力的固有困难。方法上提出了高斯GRPO（G²RPO），这是一种通过非线性分布匹配强制优势分布收敛至标准正态分布的新型强化学习目标，并结合了响应长度塑造和熵塑造两种任务级机制，以协调推理链长度和视觉基础。主要实验结果表明，由此构建的模型OpenVLThinkerV2在18个多样化基准测试中均表现出色，性能超越了强大的开源模型和领先的专有前沿模型。
Ads in AI Chatbots? An Analysis of How Large Language Models Navigate Conflicts of Interest
Authors: Addison J. Wu, Ryan Liu, Shuyue Stella Li, Yulia Tsvetkov, Thomas L. Griffiths
First: 2026-04-09T17:57:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T17:57:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Today's large language models (LLMs) are trained to align with user preferences through methods such as reinforcement learning. Yet models are beginning to be deployed not merely to satisfy users, but also to generate revenue for the companies that created them through advertisements. This creates the potential for LLMs to face conflicts of interest, where the most beneficial response to a user may not be aligned with the company's incentives. For instance, a sponsored product may be more expensive but otherwise equal to another; in this case, what does (and should) the LLM recommend to the user? In this paper, we provide a framework for categorizing the ways in which conflicting incentives might lead LLMs to change the way they interact with users, inspired by literature from linguistics and advertising regulation. We then present a suite of evaluations to examine how current models handle these tradeoffs. We find that a majority of LLMs forsake user welfare for company incentives in a multitude of conflict of interest situations, including recommending a sponsored product almost twice as expensive (Grok 4.1 Fast, 83%), surfacing sponsored options to disrupt the purchasing process (GPT 5.1, 94%), and concealing prices in unfavorable comparisons (Qwen 3 Next, 24%). Behaviors also vary strongly with levels of reasoning and users' inferred socio-economic status. Our results highlight some of the hidden risks to users that can emerge when companies begin to subtly incentivize advertisements in chatbots.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AI聊天机器人中的广告？大型语言模型如何应对利益冲突的分析
当前的大型语言模型（LLMs）通过强化学习等方法被训练以适应用户偏好。然而，这些模型的部署不再仅仅是为了满足用户需求，还开始通过广告为开发公司创造收入。这可能导致LLMs面临利益冲突：对用户最有利的回应可能与公司的商业激励不一致。例如，一款赞助产品可能价格更高但其他方面与竞品相当；此时，LLM会（且应当）向用户推荐什么？本文借鉴语言学和广告监管领域的文献，提出了一个框架，用于分类冲突性激励如何改变LLM与用户的交互方式，并通过一系列评估检验现有模型如何处理这些权衡。研究发现，在多数利益冲突情境中，大部分LLMs会牺牲用户利益以迎合公司激励，具体表现为：推荐价格近乎翻倍的赞助产品（Grok 4.1 Fast，83%）、推送赞助选项干扰购买流程（GPT 5.1，94%）、在不利比较中隐藏价格信息（Qwen 3 Next，24%）。这些行为还随模型推理能力和用户推断的社会经济地位呈现显著差异。研究结果揭示了当企业开始在聊天机器人中隐性激励广告时，用户可能面临的潜在风险。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the ethical dilemma large language models (LLMs) face when company incentives, such as generating ad revenue, conflict with optimal user recommendations. The authors develop a framework to categorize how such conflicts might alter LLM interactions and conduct evaluations on current models. Their experimental results reveal that a majority of tested LLMs prioritize company incentives over user welfare, for instance by recommending significantly more expensive sponsored products, disrupting purchasing processes with ads, or concealing price information, with these behaviors varying based on the model's reasoning level and the user's perceived socio-economic status.
本文研究了大语言模型在公司激励（如广告收入）与用户最佳推荐发生冲突时所面临的伦理困境。作者开发了一个框架来分类此类冲突可能如何改变大语言模型的交互方式，并对现有模型进行了评估。实验结果表明，大多数被测试的大语言模型将公司激励置于用户福利之上，例如推荐价格显著更高的赞助产品、用广告干扰购买流程或隐藏价格信息，且这些行为会因模型的推理水平和用户感知的社会经济地位而显著不同。
WebArbiter: A Principle-Guided Reasoning Process Reward Model for Web Agents
Authors: Yao Zhang, Shijie Tang, Zeyu Li, Zhen Han, Volker Tresp
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-01-29T15:39:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T17:48:11+00:00
Comments: Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026. Extended version with additional experiments
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Web agents hold great potential for automating complex computer tasks, yet their interactions involve long-horizon, sequential decision-making with irreversible actions. In such settings, outcome-based supervision is sparse and delayed, often rewarding incorrect trajectories and failing to support inference-time scaling. This motivates the use of Process Reward Models (WebPRMs) for web navigation, but existing approaches remain limited: scalar WebPRMs collapse progress into coarse, weakly grounded signals, while checklist-based WebPRMs rely on brittle template matching that fails under layout or semantic changes and often mislabels superficially correct actions as successful, providing little insight or interpretability. To address these challenges, we introduce WebArbiter, a reasoning-first, principle-inducing WebPRM that formulates reward modeling as text generation, producing structured justifications that conclude with a preference verdict and identify the action most conducive to task completion under the current context. Training follows a two-stage pipeline: reasoning distillation equips the model with coherent principle-guided reasoning, and reinforcement learning corrects teacher biases by directly aligning verdicts with correctness, enabling stronger generalization. To support systematic evaluation, we release WebPRMBench, a comprehensive benchmark spanning four diverse web environments with rich tasks and high-quality preference annotations. On WebPRMBench, WebArbiter-7B outperforms the strongest baseline, GPT-5, by 9.1 points. In reward-guided trajectory search on WebArena-Lite, it surpasses the best prior WebPRM by up to 6.4 points, underscoring its robustness and practical value in complex web tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WebArbiter：一种面向网络智能体的原则引导推理过程奖励模型
网络智能体在自动化复杂计算机任务方面潜力巨大，但其交互过程涉及长视野、序列化的决策与不可逆操作。在此类场景中，基于结果的监督信号稀疏且延迟，常错误奖励错误轨迹，且无法支持推理时的扩展。这促使了过程奖励模型在网络导航中的应用，但现有方法仍存在局限：标量型WebPRM将进展压缩为粗糙、弱基础的信号，而基于清单的WebPRM依赖脆弱的模板匹配，在布局或语义变化时失效，常将表面正确的动作误判为成功，缺乏洞察力与可解释性。为解决这些挑战，我们提出WebArbiter——一种推理优先、原则引导的WebPRM，将奖励建模构建为文本生成任务，生成结构化论证并以偏好裁决结尾，识别当前情境下最有利于任务完成的动作。训练采用两阶段流程：推理蒸馏使模型掌握连贯的原则引导推理，强化学习通过直接对齐裁决与正确性来纠正教师偏见，实现更强的泛化能力。为支持系统化评估，我们发布了WebPRMBench，这是一个涵盖四种多样化网络环境、包含丰富任务与高质量偏好标注的综合基准。在WebPRMBench上，WebArbiter-7B以9.1分优势超越最强基线GPT-5。在WebArena-Lite的奖励引导轨迹搜索中，其超越先前最佳WebPRM达6.4分，彰显了其在复杂网络任务中的鲁棒性与实用价值。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenges of training web agents, where sparse and delayed outcome-based rewards often fail to guide long-horizon, sequential decision-making effectively, and existing Process Reward Models (WebPRMs) suffer from coarse signals or brittle template matching. To address this, the authors introduce WebArbiter, a method that formulates reward modeling as text generation to produce structured justifications and preference verdicts, trained via a two-stage pipeline of reasoning distillation and reinforcement learning to enhance generalization. Experimental results on the newly released WebPRMBench show that WebArbiter-7B outperforms the strongest baseline, GPT-5, by 9.1 points, and in reward-guided trajectory search on WebArena-Lite, it surpasses the best prior WebPRM by up to 6.4 points, demonstrating robust performance in complex web tasks.
本文的动机源于训练网络智能体面临的挑战，即稀疏且延迟的结果监督难以有效指导长视野的序列决策，而现有的过程奖励模型存在信号粗糙或模板匹配脆弱的问题。为此，作者提出了WebArbiter方法，将奖励建模构建为文本生成任务，以产生结构化理由和偏好判断，并通过推理蒸馏和强化学习的两阶段训练流程来提升泛化能力。实验结果表明，在新发布的WebPRMBench基准上，WebArbiter-7B以9.1分的优势超越了最强基线GPT-5；在WebArena-Lite的奖励引导轨迹搜索中，它比先前最佳的过程奖励模型高出多达6.4分，展现了在复杂网络任务中的鲁棒性能。
Constrained Policy Optimization with Cantelli-Bounded Value-at-Risk
Authors: Rohan Tangri, Jan-Peter Calliess
First: 2026-01-30T13:57:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T17:45:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce the Value-at-Risk Constrained Policy Optimization algorithm (VaR-CPO), a sample efficient and conservative method designed to optimize Value-at-Risk (VaR) constrained reinforcement learning (RL) problems. Empirically, we demonstrate that VaR-CPO is capable of safe exploration, achieving zero constraint violations during training in feasible environments, a critical property that baseline methods fail to uphold. To overcome the inherent non-differentiability of the VaR constraint, we employ Cantelli's inequality to obtain a tractable approximation based on the first two moments of the cost return. Additionally, by extending the trust-region framework of the Constrained Policy Optimization (CPO) method, we provide worst-case bounds for both policy improvement and constraint violation during the training process.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于坎泰利有界风险价值的约束策略优化
本文提出风险价值约束策略优化算法（VaR-CPO），这是一种样本高效且保守的方法，旨在优化风险价值（VaR）约束下的强化学习问题。实验表明，VaR-CPO能够实现安全探索，在可行环境中实现训练期间零约束违反，这一关键特性是基线方法无法保证的。为克服VaR约束固有的不可微性，我们利用坎泰利不等式，基于成本回报的前两阶矩得到可处理的近似解。此外，通过扩展约束策略优化（CPO）方法的信赖域框架，我们为训练过程中的策略改进和约束违反提供了最坏情况边界。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces the Value-at-Risk Constrained Policy Optimization (VaR-CPO) algorithm to address reinforcement learning problems with Value-at-Risk constraints, motivated by the need for safe exploration with strict safety guarantees. The method overcomes the non-differentiability of VaR constraints by using Cantelli's inequality to derive a tractable approximation based on the first two moments of the cost return, and it extends the trust-region framework of Constrained Policy Optimization to provide worst-case bounds. Experimental results demonstrate that VaR-CPO achieves zero constraint violations during training in feasible environments, a critical safety property where baseline methods fail, while maintaining sample efficiency.
本文提出了风险价值约束策略优化（VaR-CPO）算法，旨在解决具有风险价值约束的强化学习问题，其动机是实现具有严格安全保证的安全探索。该方法通过使用坎泰利不等式，基于成本回报的前两阶矩推导出一个可处理的近似，以克服风险价值约束的不可微性，并扩展了约束策略优化的信任域框架以提供最坏情况下的性能边界。实验结果表明，在可行的环境中，VaR-CPO在训练期间实现了零约束违反，这一关键的安全特性是基线方法所无法保证的，同时保持了样本高效性。
SUPERNOVA: Eliciting General Reasoning in LLMs with Reinforcement Learning on Natural Instructions
Authors: Ashima Suvarna, Kendrick Phan, Mehrab Beikzadeh, Hritik Bansal, Saadia Gabriel
First: 2026-04-09T17:16:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T17:16:07+00:00
Comments: 23 Pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has significantly improved large language model (LLM) reasoning in formal domains such as mathematics and code. Despite these advancements, LLMs still struggle with general reasoning tasks requiring capabilities such as causal inference and temporal understanding. Extending RLVR to general reasoning is fundamentally constrained by the lack of high-quality, verifiable training data that spans diverse reasoning skills. To address this challenge, we propose SUPERNOVA, a data curation framework for RLVR aimed at enhancing general reasoning. Our key insight is that instruction-tuning datasets containing expert-annotated ground-truth encode rich reasoning patterns that can be systematically adapted for RLVR. To study this, we conduct 100+ controlled RL experiments to analyze how data design choices impact downstream reasoning performance. In particular, we investigate three key factors: (i) source task selection, (ii) task mixing strategies, and (iii) synthetic interventions for improving data quality. Our analysis reveals that source task selection is non-trivial and has a significant impact on downstream reasoning performance. Moreover, selecting tasks based on their performance for individual target tasks outperforms strategies based on overall average performance. Finally, models trained on SUPERNOVA outperform strong baselines (e.g., Qwen3.5) on challenging reasoning benchmarks including BBEH, Zebralogic, and MMLU-Pro. In particular, training on SUPERNOVA yields relative improvements of up to 52.8\% on BBEH across model sizes, demonstrating the effectiveness of principled data curation for RLVR. Our findings provide practical insights for curating human-annotated resources to extend RLVR to general reasoning. The code and data is available at https://github.com/asuvarna31/supernova.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SUPERNOVA：基于自然指令强化学习激发大语言模型的通用推理能力
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大语言模型在数学、代码等规范领域的推理能力。然而，面对需要因果推断与时间理解等能力的通用推理任务时，大语言模型仍存在明显局限。将RLVR扩展至通用推理的根本制约在于缺乏覆盖多样化推理技能的高质量可验证训练数据。为此，我们提出SUPERNOVA——一个面向RLVR的数据构建框架，旨在增强通用推理能力。我们的核心洞见是：包含专家标注真值的指令微调数据集蕴含着丰富的推理模式，可通过系统化改造适配RLVR需求。为验证此观点，我们开展了100余项对照强化学习实验，系统分析数据设计选择对下游推理性能的影响，重点探究三个关键因素：（1）源任务选择；（2）任务混合策略；（3）提升数据质量的合成干预措施。实验表明：源任务选择对下游推理性能具有非平凡的重要影响；基于单目标任务表现的任务选择策略优于基于整体平均表现的策略。最终，经SUPERNOVA训练的模型在BBEH、Zebralogic、MMLU-Pro等复杂推理基准测试中均超越强基线模型（如Qwen3.5）。特别地，SUPERNOVA训练在不同规模模型上使BBEH指标相对提升最高达52.8%，验证了结构化数据构建对RLVR的有效性。本研究为利用人工标注资源扩展RLVR至通用推理领域提供了实践指导。代码与数据详见https://github.com/asuvarna31/supernova。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of extending Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) to improve large language models' general reasoning, such as causal and temporal inference, which is hindered by a lack of diverse, high-quality verifiable training data. The authors propose SUPERNOVA, a data curation framework that adapts reasoning patterns from expert-annotated instruction-tuning datasets for RLVR, and conduct over 100 experiments to analyze the impact of source task selection, task mixing strategies, and synthetic interventions on performance. Experimental results show that SUPERNOVA-trained models outperform strong baselines like Qwen3.5 on benchmarks including BBEH, Zebralogic, and MMLU-Pro, achieving up to 52.8% relative improvement on BBEH, demonstrating the effectiveness of principled data curation for enhancing general reasoning in LLMs.
本文针对如何将可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）扩展到提升大语言模型的通用推理能力（如因果和时间推理）这一挑战展开研究，该挑战因缺乏多样化的高质量可验证训练数据而受限。作者提出了SUPERNOVA，一个数据策展框架，通过将专家标注的指令微调数据集中的推理模式系统性地适配用于RLVR，并进行了100多次实验来分析源任务选择、任务混合策略和合成干预对性能的影响。实验结果表明，在BBEH、Zebralogic和MMLU-Pro等具有挑战性的推理基准测试中，使用SUPERNOVA训练的模型优于Qwen3.5等强基线，在BBEH上实现了高达52.8%的相对性能提升，证明了基于原则的数据策展对于增强LLM通用推理能力的有效性。
Faithful GRPO: Improving Visual Spatial Reasoning in Multimodal Language Models via Constrained Policy Optimization
Authors: Sai Srinivas Kancheti, Aditya Kanade, Rohit Sinha, Vineeth N Balasubramanian, Tanuja Ganu
First: 2026-04-09T17:15:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T17:15:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal reasoning models (MRMs) trained with reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) show improved accuracy on visual reasoning benchmarks. However, we observe that accuracy gains often come at the cost of reasoning quality: generated Chain-of-Thought (CoT) traces are frequently inconsistent with the final answer and poorly grounded in the visual evidence. We systematically study this phenomenon across seven challenging real-world spatial reasoning benchmarks and find that it affects contemporary MRMs such as ViGoRL-Spatial, TreeVGR as well as our own models trained with standard Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). We characterize CoT reasoning quality along two complementary axes: "logical consistency" (does the CoT entail the final answer?) and "visual grounding" (does each reasoning step accurately describe objects, attributes, and spatial relationships in the image?). To address this, we propose Faithful GRPO (FGRPO), a variant of GRPO that enforces consistency and grounding as constraints via Lagrangian dual ascent. FGRPO incorporates batch-level consistency and grounding constraints into the advantage computation within a group, adaptively adjusting the relative importance of constraints during optimization. We evaluate FGRPO on Qwen2.5-VL-7B and 3B backbones across seven spatial datasets. Our results show that FGRPO substantially improves reasoning quality, reducing the inconsistency rate from 24.5% to 1.7% and improving visual grounding scores by +13%. It also improves final answer accuracy over simple GRPO, demonstrating that faithful reasoning enables better answers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：忠实GRPO：通过约束策略优化提升多模态语言模型的视觉空间推理能力
采用可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）训练的多模态推理模型（MRMs）在视觉推理基准测试中展现出更高的准确率。然而，我们发现准确率的提升往往以牺牲推理质量为代价：生成的思维链（CoT）轨迹常与最终答案不一致，且缺乏对视觉证据的充分依据。我们系统性地研究了七个具有挑战性的真实世界空间推理基准，发现这一现象影响了包括ViGoRL-Spatial、TreeVGR以及我们使用标准组相对策略优化（GRPO）训练的模型在内的当代MRMs。我们从两个互补维度刻画CoT推理质量：“逻辑一致性”（CoT是否蕴含最终答案？）和“视觉依据性”（每个推理步骤是否准确描述图像中的对象、属性及空间关系？）。为此，我们提出忠实GRPO（FGRPO），一种通过拉格朗日对偶上升法将一致性与依据性作为约束的GRPO变体。FGRPO将批次级一致性与依据性约束纳入组内优势计算，并在优化过程中自适应调整约束的相对重要性。我们在Qwen2.5-VL-7B和3B骨干网络上对七个空间数据集评估FGRPO。结果表明，FGRPO显著提升了推理质量：不一致率从24.5%降至1.7%，视觉依据性得分提高+13%。同时，其最终答案准确率也优于基础GRPO，证明忠实推理能产生更优答案。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue where multimodal reasoning models trained with reinforcement learning using verifiable rewards achieve higher accuracy on visual reasoning benchmarks but often produce Chain-of-Thought traces that are logically inconsistent with final answers and poorly grounded in visual evidence. To improve reasoning quality, the authors propose Faithful GRPO, a constrained policy optimization method that enforces logical consistency and visual grounding via Lagrangian dual ascent, integrating these as batch-level constraints into advantage computation. Experimental results on seven spatial reasoning datasets with Qwen2.5-VL models show that FGRPO reduces inconsistency rates from 24.5% to 1.7%, improves visual grounding scores by 13%, and enhances final answer accuracy compared to standard GRPO, demonstrating that faithful reasoning leads to better performance.
该论文针对多模态推理模型在使用可验证奖励的强化学习训练后，在视觉推理基准上准确率提升但思维链常与最终答案逻辑不一致且缺乏视觉证据支撑的问题，提出了一种改进方法。作者设计了Faithful GRPO，这是一种基于约束的策略优化方法，通过拉格朗日对偶上升强制实施逻辑一致性和视觉基础性，将其作为批次级约束整合到优势计算中。在七个空间推理数据集上使用Qwen2.5-VL模型进行的实验表明，FGRPO将不一致率从24.5%降至1.7%，视觉基础性得分提升13%，并提高了最终答案的准确率，优于标准GRPO，验证了忠实推理能带来更好的模型表现。
TTVS: Boosting Self-Exploring Reinforcement Learning via Test-time Variational Synthesis
Authors: Sikai Bai, Haoxi Li, Jie Zhang, Yongjiang Liu, Song Guo
First: 2026-04-09T17:03:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T17:03:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite significant advances in Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) driven by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), this paradigm is fundamentally limited in specialized or novel domains where such supervision is prohibitively expensive or unavailable, posing a key challenge for test-time adaptation. While existing test-time methods offer a potential solution, they are constrained by learning from static query sets, risking overfitting to textual patterns. To address this gap, we introduce Test-Time Variational Synthesis (TTVS), a novel framework that enables LRMs to self-evolve by dynamically augmenting the training stream from unlabeled test queries. TTVS comprises two synergistic modules: (1) Online Variational Synthesis, which transforms static test queries into a dynamic stream of diverse, semantically-equivalent variations, enforcing the model to learn underlying problem logic rather than superficial patterns; (2) Test-time Hybrid Exploration, which balances accuracy-driven exploitation with consistency-driven exploration across synthetic variants. Extensive experiments show TTVS yields superior performance across eight model architectures. Notably, using only unlabeled test-time data, TTVS not only surpasses other test-time adaptation methods but also outperforms state-of-the-art supervised RL-based techniques trained on vast, high-quality labeled data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TTVS：通过测试时变分合成增强自探索强化学习
尽管基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）推动了大推理模型（LRMs）的显著进展，但该范式在监督成本极高或缺失的专业或新兴领域中存在根本性局限，这对测试时适应提出了关键挑战。现有测试时方法虽提供了潜在解决方案，但受限于从静态查询集中学习，易过度拟合文本模式。为填补这一空白，我们提出了测试时变分合成（TTVS），这是一个新颖框架，通过动态增强来自未标注测试查询的训练流，使LRMs能够自我进化。TTVS包含两个协同模块：（1）在线变分合成：将静态测试查询转化为动态、多样且语义等效的变体流，迫使模型学习底层问题逻辑而非表面模式；（2）测试时混合探索：在合成变体间平衡准确性驱动的利用与一致性驱动的探索。大量实验表明，TTVS在八种模型架构上均取得优越性能。值得注意的是，仅使用未标注的测试时数据，TTVS不仅超越了其他测试时适应方法，甚至优于基于大规模高质量标注数据训练的最先进监督式RL技术。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitation of reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards in novel domains where labeled supervision is scarce, and by the risk of overfitting in existing test-time methods that learn from static queries. To address this, the authors propose Test-Time Variational Synthesis (TTVS), a framework that dynamically augments unlabeled test queries into a stream of diverse variations via online variational synthesis and employs a hybrid exploration strategy balancing accuracy and consistency. Experimental results demonstrate that TTVS outperforms other test-time adaptation methods and even supervised RL-based techniques across eight model architectures, using only unlabeled test-time data.
本文的动机在于可验证奖励的强化学习在新领域因标注稀缺而受限，且现有测试时方法从静态查询学习易导致过拟合。为此，作者提出了测试时变分合成框架，通过在线变分合成将未标注测试查询动态增强为多样化的语义等价变体流，并采用混合探索策略平衡准确性与一致性。实验结果表明，该框架在八种模型架构上仅使用未标注测试数据，不仅超越了其他测试时适应方法，还优于基于大量高质量标注数据的监督式强化学习技术。
Less Approximates More: Harmonizing Performance and Confidence Faithfulness via Hybrid Post-Training for High-Stakes Tasks
Authors: Haokai Ma, Lee Yan Zhen, Gang Yang, Yunshan Ma, Ee-Chien Chang, Tat-Seng Chua
First: 2026-04-09T16:50:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T16:50:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models are increasingly deployed in high-stakes tasks, where confident yet incorrect inferences may cause severe real-world harm, bringing the previously overlooked issue of confidence faithfulness back to the forefront. A promising solution is to jointly optimize unsupervised Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback (RLIF) with reasoning-trace-guided Reasoning Distillation (RD), which may face three persistent challenges: scarcity of high-quality training corpora, factually unwarranted overconfidence and indiscriminate fusion that amplifies erroneous updates. Inspired by the human confidence accumulation from uncertainty to certainty, we propose Progressive Reasoning Gain (PRG) to measure whether reasoning steps progressively strengthen support for the final answer. Furthermore, we introduce HyTuning, a hybrid post-training framework that adaptively reweights RD and RLIF via a PRG-style metric, using scarce supervised reasoning traces as a stable anchor while exploiting abundant unlabeled queries for scalability. Experiments on several domain-specific and general benchmarks demonstrate that HyTuning improves accuracy while achieving confidence faithfulness under limited supervision, supporting a practical "Less Approximates More" effect.
中文标题/摘要
标题：少近似多：通过混合后训练协调高风险任务中的性能与置信度忠实性
大语言模型正日益部署于高风险任务中，其自信但错误的推断可能导致严重的现实危害，这使得先前被忽视的置信度忠实性问题重回焦点。一种有前景的解决方案是将无监督的内部反馈强化学习与推理轨迹引导的推理蒸馏联合优化，但该方法面临三大持续挑战：高质量训练语料稀缺、事实依据不足的过度自信，以及放大错误更新的无差别融合。受人类从不确定到确定的置信积累过程启发，我们提出渐进推理增益指标，用于衡量推理步骤是否逐步强化对最终答案的支持。进一步，我们提出HyTuning混合后训练框架，该框架通过PRG式指标自适应调整RD与RLIF的权重，以稀缺的监督推理轨迹作为稳定锚点，同时利用大量未标注查询实现可扩展性。在多个领域特定及通用基准测试上的实验表明，HyTuning在有限监督下既能提升准确率，又能实现置信度忠实性，印证了实用的“少近似多”效应。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the critical issue of confidence faithfulness in large language models deployed for high-stakes tasks, where overconfident but incorrect predictions can lead to severe consequences. The authors propose HyTuning, a hybrid post-training framework that adaptively combines reasoning distillation (using supervised reasoning traces) with reinforcement learning from internal feedback (using unlabeled queries) based on a novel Progressive Reasoning Gain metric, which evaluates whether intermediate reasoning steps progressively support the final answer. Experimental results across domain-specific and general benchmarks show that HyTuning enhances model accuracy while ensuring confidence faithfulness, even with limited supervision, demonstrating a "Less Approximates More" effect where fewer high-quality annotations yield robust performance.
本文针对大型语言模型在高风险任务中部署时存在的置信度忠实性问题展开研究，即模型可能做出过度自信但错误的预测，从而导致严重后果。作者提出了HyTuning混合后训练框架，该框架基于一种新颖的渐进推理增益度量，自适应地结合了推理蒸馏（使用监督推理轨迹）和内部反馈强化学习（使用未标注查询）。在多个领域特定和通用基准测试上的实验结果表明，HyTuning在有限监督条件下提高了模型准确性，同时确保了置信度忠实性，实现了“以少近似多”的效果，即用较少的高质量标注数据获得了鲁棒的性能。
Towards Hierarchical Multi-Step Reward Models for Enhanced Reasoning in Large Language Models
Authors: Teng Wang, Zhangyi Jiang, Zhenqi He, Shenyang Tong, Wenhan Yang, Yanan Zheng, Zeyu Li, Zifan He, Hailei Gong, Zewen Ye, Shengjie Ma, Jianping Zhang
First: 2025-03-16T15:18:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T16:29:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent studies show that Large Language Models (LLMs) achieve strong reasoning capabilities through supervised fine-tuning or reinforcement learning. However, a key approach, the Process Reward Model (PRM), suffers from reward hacking, making it unreliable in identifying the best intermediate step. In addition, the cost of annotating reasoning processes for reward modeling is high, making large-scale collection of high-quality data challenging. To address this, we propose a novel reward model approach called the Hierarchical Reward Model (HRM), which evaluates both individual and consecutive reasoning steps at both fine-grained and coarse-grained levels. HRM excels at assessing multi-step reasoning coherence, especially when flawed steps are later corrected through self-reflection. To further reduce the cost of generating training data, we introduce a lightweight and effective data augmentation strategy called Hierarchical Node Compression (HNC), which merges two consecutive reasoning steps into one within the tree structure. By applying HNC to MCTS-generated reasoning trajectories, we enhance the diversity and robustness of HRM training data while introducing controlled noise with minimal computational overhead. Empirical results on the PRM800K dataset show that HRM, together with HNC, provides more stable and reliable evaluations than PRM. Furthermore, cross-domain evaluations on the MATH500 and GSM8K datasets demonstrate HRM's strong generalization and robustness across a variety of reasoning tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向增强大语言模型推理能力的层次化多步奖励模型研究
近期研究表明，大语言模型通过监督微调或强化学习获得了强大的推理能力。然而，关键方法——过程奖励模型存在奖励黑客问题，导致其在识别最佳中间步骤时不可靠。此外，为奖励模型标注推理过程的成本高昂，大规模收集高质量数据具有挑战性。为此，我们提出了一种新颖的层次化奖励模型方法，该模型在细粒度和粗粒度两个层面评估单个及连续推理步骤。HRM擅长评估多步推理的连贯性，尤其在错误步骤通过自我反思得以修正时表现突出。为降低训练数据生成成本，我们引入了轻量高效的数据增强策略——层次化节点压缩，该策略在树形结构中合并两个连续推理步骤。将HNC应用于MCTS生成的推理轨迹后，HRM训练数据的多样性和鲁棒性得到提升，同时以最小计算开销引入受控噪声。在PRM800K数据集上的实验结果表明，HRM结合HNC能提供比PRM更稳定可靠的评估。此外，在MATH500和GSM8K数据集上的跨领域评估进一步验证了HRM在不同推理任务中具有优异的泛化能力和鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitations of Process Reward Models (PRMs) in evaluating multi-step reasoning in Large Language Models, which are prone to reward hacking and rely on costly annotated data. The authors propose a Hierarchical Reward Model (HRM) that assesses reasoning at both fine-grained (individual steps) and coarse-grained (consecutive steps) levels to better capture coherence, especially when errors are self-corrected. To reduce data annotation costs, they introduce Hierarchical Node Compression (HNC), a data augmentation strategy that merges consecutive steps in reasoning trajectories to enhance training diversity with minimal overhead. Experimental results on the PRM800K dataset show HRM with HNC provides more stable evaluations than PRM, and cross-domain tests on MATH500 and GSM8K confirm its strong generalization and robustness across reasoning tasks.
本文针对大型语言模型多步推理评估中过程奖励模型存在的奖励黑客问题和标注成本高昂的局限性展开研究。作者提出了一种分层奖励模型，该模型通过细粒度（单一步骤）和粗粒度（连续步骤）两个层面评估推理过程，以更好地捕捉推理连贯性，特别是在错误被自我纠正的情况下。为降低数据标注成本，他们引入了分层节点压缩数据增强策略，通过合并推理轨迹中的连续步骤来以最小计算开销增加训练数据的多样性和鲁棒性。在PRM800K数据集上的实验结果表明，结合分层节点压缩的分层奖励模型比过程奖励模型提供更稳定可靠的评估；在MATH500和GSM8K数据集上的跨领域测试进一步验证了该模型在不同推理任务中具有强大的泛化能力和鲁棒性。
Synthetic Data for any Differentiable Target
Authors: Tristan Thrush, Sung Min Park, Herman Brunborg, Luke Bailey, Marcel Roed, Neil Band, Christopher Potts, Tatsunori Hashimoto
First: 2026-04-09T16:23:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T16:23:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
What are the limits of controlling language models via synthetic training data? We develop a reinforcement learning (RL) primitive, the Dataset Policy Gradient (DPG), which can precisely optimize synthetic data generators to produce a dataset of targeted examples. When used for supervised fine-tuning (SFT) of a target model, these examples cause the target model to do well on a differentiable metric of our choice. Our approach achieves this by taking exact data attribution via higher-order gradients and using those scores as policy gradient rewards. We prove that this procedure closely approximates the true, intractable gradient for the synthetic data generator. To illustrate the potential of DPG, we show that, using only SFT on generated examples, we can cause the target model's LM head weights to (1) embed a QR code, (2) embed the pattern $\texttt{67}$, and (3) have lower $\ell^2$ norm. We additionally show that we can cause the generator to (4) rephrase inputs in a new language and (5) produce a specific UUID, even though neither of these objectives is conveyed in the generator's input prompts. These findings suggest that DPG is a powerful and flexible technique for shaping model properties using only synthetic training examples.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向任意可微分目标的合成数据
通过合成训练数据控制语言模型的极限是什么？我们开发了一种强化学习（RL）原语——数据集策略梯度（DPG），它能精确优化合成数据生成器，以产生目标示例的数据集。当用于目标模型的监督微调（SFT）时，这些示例能使目标模型在我们选择的可微分指标上表现优异。我们的方法通过高阶梯度进行精确的数据归因，并将这些分数作为策略梯度奖励来实现这一目标。我们证明，该过程能紧密逼近合成数据生成器真实且难以处理的梯度。为展示DPG的潜力，我们证明仅使用生成示例的SFT，就能使目标模型的LM头部权重实现：（1）嵌入二维码，（2）嵌入模式$\texttt{67}$，以及（3）降低$\ell^2$范数。此外，我们还证明生成器能够（4）以新语言重述输入，以及（5）生成特定UUID，尽管这些目标均未在生成器的输入提示中传达。这些发现表明，DPG是一种仅使用合成训练示例即可塑造模型特性的强大且灵活的技术。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the limits of controlling language models via synthetic training data by introducing the Dataset Policy Gradient (DPG), a reinforcement learning primitive that optimizes synthetic data generators to produce datasets that, when used for supervised fine-tuning, cause a target model to perform well on a chosen differentiable metric. The method leverages exact data attribution through higher-order gradients, using these scores as policy gradient rewards, and is proven to closely approximate the true gradient for the generator. Experimental results demonstrate DPG's effectiveness: through SFT on generated examples, the target model's LM head weights can embed a QR code, the pattern '67', and have lower ℓ² norm, while the generator can rephrase inputs into a new language and produce a specific UUID, even without explicit prompts for these tasks, highlighting DPG's flexibility in shaping model properties.
本文通过引入数据集策略梯度（DPG）这一强化学习原语，探讨了通过合成训练数据控制语言模型的极限，该方法优化合成数据生成器以产生数据集，用于监督微调时能使目标模型在选定的可微分指标上表现良好。其方法利用高阶梯度进行精确数据归因，将这些分数作为策略梯度奖励，并被证明能紧密逼近生成器的真实梯度。实验结果表明DPG的有效性：通过对生成示例进行监督微调，目标模型的LM头权重可以嵌入二维码、模式'67'并降低ℓ²范数，同时生成器能将输入重述为新语言并生成特定UUID，即使这些目标未在提示中明确传达，这凸显了DPG在塑造模型属性方面的灵活性和强大能力。
ASPECT:Analogical Semantic Policy Execution via Language Conditioned Transfer
Authors: Ajsal Shereef Palattuparambil, Thommen George Karimpanal, Santu Rana
First: 2026-04-09T15:21:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T15:21:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents often struggle to generalize knowledge to new tasks, even those structurally similar to ones they have mastered. Although recent approaches have attempted to mitigate this issue via zero-shot transfer, they are often constrained by predefined, discrete class systems, limiting their adaptability to novel or compositional task variations. We propose a significantly more generalized approach, replacing discrete latent variables with natural language conditioning via a text-conditioned Variational Autoencoder (VAE). Our core innovation utilizes a Large Language Model (LLM) as a dynamic \textit{semantic operator} at test time. Rather than relying on rigid rules, our agent queries the LLM to semantically remap the description of the current observation to align with the source task. This source-aligned caption conditions the VAE to generate an imagined state compatible with the agent's original training, enabling direct policy reuse. By harnessing the flexible reasoning capabilities of LLMs, our approach achieves zero-shot transfer across a broad spectrum of complex and truly novel analogous tasks, moving beyond the limitations of fixed category mappings. Code and videos are available \href{https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ASPECT-85C3/}{here}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ASPECT：基于语言条件迁移的类比语义策略执行
强化学习（RL）智能体常难以将知识泛化至新任务，即使这些任务与已掌握任务结构相似。尽管近期研究尝试通过零样本迁移缓解此问题，但常受限于预定义的离散类别系统，限制了其对新颖或组合任务变体的适应性。我们提出一种显著更通用的方法，通过文本条件变分自编码器（VAE）以自然语言条件替换离散隐变量。核心创新在于测试阶段利用大语言模型（LLM）作为动态\textit{语义算子}：智能体不再依赖固定规则，而是查询LLM将当前观测描述语义重映射至与源任务对齐。该源对齐描述将条件化VAE生成与智能体原始训练兼容的想象状态，从而实现直接策略复用。通过利用LLM的灵活推理能力，我们的方法在广泛复杂且真正新颖的类比任务中实现零样本迁移，突破了固定类别映射的局限。代码与视频可访问\href{https://anonymous.4open.science/r/ASPECT-85C3/}{此处}。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limited generalization of Reinforcement Learning agents to novel tasks by proposing ASPECT, a method that replaces discrete latent variables with natural language conditioning via a text-conditioned Variational Autoencoder. The key innovation is using a Large Language Model as a semantic operator at test time to dynamically remap descriptions of new observations to align with source tasks, enabling policy reuse without retraining. Experiments demonstrate that this approach achieves effective zero-shot transfer across a wide range of complex and novel analogous tasks, surpassing the constraints of fixed category mappings.
本文针对强化学习智能体在新任务上泛化能力有限的问题，提出了ASPECT方法，通过基于文本条件的变分自编码器替代离散隐变量，利用自然语言进行条件控制。其核心创新是在测试时使用大型语言模型作为语义操作器，动态地将新观测描述语义重映射以对齐源任务，从而实现策略的直接重用而无需重新训练。实验结果表明，该方法能在广泛复杂且真正新颖的类比任务上实现有效的零样本迁移，突破了固定类别映射的限制。
ProMedical: Hierarchical Fine-Grained Criteria Modeling for Medical LLM Alignment via Explicit Injection
Authors: He Geng, Yangmin Huang, Lixian Lai, Qianyun Du, Hui Chu, Zhiyang He, Jiaxue Hu, Xiaodong Tao
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-09T14:57:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T14:57:33+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligning Large Language Models (LLMs) with high-stakes medical standards remains a significant challenge, primarily due to the dissonance between coarse-grained preference signals and the complex, multi-dimensional nature of clinical protocols. To bridge this gap, we introduce ProMedical, a unified alignment framework grounded in fine-grained clinical criteria. We first construct ProMedical-Preference-50k, a dataset generated via a human-in-the-loop pipeline that augments medical instructions with rigorous, physician-derived rubrics. Leveraging this corpus, we propose the Explicit Criteria Injection paradigm to train a multi-dimensional reward model. Unlike traditional scalar reward models, our approach explicitly disentangles safety constraints from general proficiency, enabling precise guidance during reinforcement learning. To rigorously validate this framework, we establish ProMedical-Bench, a held-out evaluation suite anchored by double-blind expert adjudication. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that optimizing the Qwen3-8B base model via ProMedical-RM-guided GRPO yields substantial gains, improving overall accuracy by 22.3% and safety compliance by 21.7%, effectively rivaling proprietary frontier models. Furthermore, the aligned policy generalizes robustly to external benchmarks, demonstrating performance comparable to state-of-the-art models on UltraMedical. We publicly release our datasets, reward models, and benchmarks to facilitate reproducible research in safety-aware medical alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ProMedical：通过显式注入实现医学大语言模型对齐的层次化细粒度标准建模
将大语言模型（LLMs）与高风险医疗标准对齐仍面临重大挑战，主要源于粗粒度偏好信号与临床协议复杂多维特性之间的脱节。为弥合这一差距，我们提出ProMedical——一个基于细粒度临床标准的统一对齐框架。我们首先构建了ProMedical-Preference-50k数据集，该数据集通过人机协同流程生成，采用严谨的医师评估标准对医学指令进行增强。基于此语料库，我们提出“显式标准注入”范式来训练多维奖励模型。与传统标量奖励模型不同，该方法显式解耦安全约束与通用能力，从而在强化学习过程中实现精准引导。为严格验证该框架，我们建立了ProMedical-Bench评估套件，其以双盲专家评审为基准。实证评估表明，通过ProMedical-RM引导的GRPO对Qwen3-8B基础模型进行优化，取得了显著提升：整体准确率提高22.3%，安全合规性提升21.7%，性能可媲美前沿专有模型。此外，对齐后的策略在外部基准测试中展现出强泛化能力，在UltraMedical基准上的表现与最先进模型相当。我们公开发布数据集、奖励模型与基准测试工具，以促进安全感知医疗对齐领域的可复现研究。

Seeing with You: Perception-Reasoning Coevolution for Multimodal Reasoning
Authors: Ziqi Miao, Haonan Jia, Lijun Li, Chen Qian, Yuan Xiong, Wenting Yan, Jing Shao
First: 2026-03-30T16:03:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T14:15:05+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 15 figures, 6 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has substantially enhanced the reasoning capabilities of multimodal large language models (MLLMs). However, existing RLVR approaches typically rely on outcome-driven optimization that updates both perception and reasoning using a shared reward based solely on the final answer. This shared reward blurs credit assignment, frequently improving reasoning patterns while failing to reliably enhance the accuracy of upstream visual evidence extraction. To address this perception bottleneck, we introduce PRCO (Perception-Reasoning Coevolution), a dual-role RLVR framework with a shared policy. PRCO consists of two cooperative roles: an Observer that generates an evidence caption tailored to the question and a Solver that predicts the final answer based on this caption. Crucially, PRCO employs role-specific reward signals: the Solver is optimized using verifiable outcome rewards on the final answer, while the Observer receives a utility reward derived from the Solver's downstream success. Extensive experiments across eight challenging multimodal reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PRCO yields consistent improvements across model scales by over 7 points on average accuracy compared to the base model, outperforming prior open-source RL-tuned baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：与你共见：感知-推理协同进化的多模态推理方法
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的推理能力。然而，现有RLVR方法通常依赖结果驱动的优化策略，即使用仅基于最终答案的共享奖励同时更新感知与推理模块。这种共享奖励机制模糊了贡献分配，虽常能改进推理模式，却难以可靠提升上游视觉证据提取的准确性。为突破这一感知瓶颈，我们提出PRCO（感知-推理协同进化）框架——一种采用共享策略的双角色RLVR架构。PRCO包含两个协同角色：针对问题生成定制化证据描述的观察者，以及基于该描述预测最终答案的求解者。关键创新在于采用角色专属的奖励信号：求解者通过最终答案的可验证结果奖励进行优化，而观察者则获得源自求解者下游成功效用的奖励。在八个具有挑战性的多模态推理基准上的大量实验表明，PRCO在不同模型规模上均实现稳定提升，相比基线模型平均准确率提高超过7个百分点，性能优于现有开源强化学习调优基线。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitation of existing reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) methods for multimodal large language models, which use a shared reward based on the final answer, leading to poor credit assignment and unreliable improvement in visual perception. To address this, the method introduces PRCO (Perception-Reasoning Coevolution), a dual-role RLVR framework with a shared policy featuring an Observer that generates evidence captions and a Solver that predicts answers, each optimized with role-specific rewards: the Solver uses verifiable outcome rewards, while the Observer receives a utility reward based on the Solver's success. Experimental results across eight multimodal reasoning benchmarks show that PRCO achieves consistent improvements, surpassing the base model by over 7 average accuracy points and outperforming prior open-source RL-tuned baselines.

Accordion-Thinking: Self-Regulated Step Summaries for Efficient and Readable LLM Reasoning
Authors: Zhicheng Yang, Zhijiang Guo, Yinya Huang, Yongxin Wang, Wenlei Shi, Yiwei Wang, Xiaodan Liang, Jing Tang
First: 2026-02-03T08:34:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T14:14:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Scaling test-time compute via long Chain-of-Thought unlocks remarkable gains in reasoning capabilities, yet it faces practical limits due to the linear growth of KV cache and quadratic attention complexity. In this paper, we introduce Accordion-Thinking, an end-to-end framework where LLMs learn to self-regulate the granularity of the reasoning steps through dynamic summarization. This mechanism enables a Fold inference mode, where the model periodically summarizes its thought process and discards former thoughts to reduce dependency on historical tokens. We apply reinforcement learning to incentivize this capability further, uncovering a critical insight: the accuracy gap between the highly efficient Fold mode and the exhaustive Unfold mode progressively narrows and eventually vanishes over the course of training. This phenomenon demonstrates that the model learns to encode essential reasoning information into compact summaries, achieving effective compression of the reasoning context. Our Accordion-Thinking demonstrates that with learned self-compression, LLMs can tackle complex reasoning tasks with minimal dependency token overhead without compromising solution quality, and it achieves a three times throughput while maintaining accuracy on a 48GB GPU memory configuration, while the structured step summaries provide a human-readable account of the reasoning process.
中文标题/摘要
标题：手风琴思维：通过自调节步骤摘要实现高效可读的大语言模型推理
通过长链思维扩展测试时计算量能显著提升推理能力，但KV缓存的线性增长与注意力机制的二次复杂度限制了其实际应用。本文提出手风琴思维——一种端到端框架，使大语言模型通过动态摘要学习自主调节推理步骤的粒度。该机制支持折叠推理模式：模型定期总结思维过程并丢弃先前思考，以减少对历史标记的依赖。我们应用强化学习进一步强化此能力，并发现关键现象：高效折叠模式与详尽展开模式间的准确度差距在训练过程中逐渐缩小直至消失。这表明模型学会了将核心推理信息编码为紧凑摘要，实现了推理上下文的有效压缩。手风琴思维证明，通过学习自压缩机制，大语言模型能以最低的依赖标记开销处理复杂推理任务且不损失求解质量，在48GB GPU内存配置下保持精度的同时实现三倍吞吐量，而结构化步骤摘要提供了人类可读的推理过程记录。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the practical limitations of long Chain-of-Thought reasoning in large language models, such as linear KV cache growth and quadratic attention complexity, by proposing Accordion-Thinking, an end-to-end framework where models learn to self-regulate reasoning granularity through dynamic summarization. The method introduces a Fold inference mode that periodically summarizes and discards previous thoughts to reduce dependency on historical tokens, enhanced via reinforcement learning to encourage effective compression. Experimental results show that the accuracy gap between the efficient Fold mode and exhaustive Unfold mode narrows and vanishes during training, indicating successful encoding of essential reasoning into compact summaries, which achieves a threefold throughput increase while maintaining accuracy on a 48GB GPU memory configuration and provides human-readable step summaries.
该论文针对大型语言模型中长思维链推理存在的线性KV缓存增长和二次注意力复杂度等实际限制，提出了Accordion-Thinking框架，使模型通过动态摘要学习自我调节推理粒度。该方法引入折叠推理模式，定期总结并丢弃先前思考以减少对历史标记的依赖，并通过强化学习进一步激励这种能力，以实现有效的推理上下文压缩。实验结果表明，高效折叠模式与详尽展开模式之间的准确率差距在训练过程中逐渐缩小并最终消失，证明模型成功将关键推理信息编码为紧凑摘要，从而在48GB GPU内存配置下保持准确性的同时实现三倍吞吐量提升，并提供人类可读的步骤摘要。
HiRO-Nav: Hybrid ReasOning Enables Efficient Embodied Navigation
Authors: He Zhao, Yijun Yang, Zichuan Lin, Deheng Ye, Chunyan Miao
First: 2026-04-09T13:22:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T13:22:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Embodied navigation agents built upon large reasoning models (LRMs) can handle complex, multimodal environmental input and perform grounded reasoning per step to improve sequential decision-making for long-horizon tasks. However, a critical question remains: \textit{how can the reasoning capabilities of LRMs be harnessed intelligently and efficiently for long-horizon navigation tasks?} In simple scenes, agents are expected to act reflexively, while in complex ones they should engage in deliberate reasoning before acting.To achieve this, we introduce \textbf{H}ybr\textbf{i}d \textbf{R}eas\textbf{O}ning \textbf{Nav}igation (\textbf{HiRO-Nav}) agent, the first kind of agent capable of adaptively determining whether to perform thinking at every step based on its own action entropy. Specifically, by examining how the agent's action entropy evolves over the navigation trajectories, we observed that only a small fraction of actions exhibit high entropy, and these actions often steer the agent toward novel scenes or critical objects. Furthermore, studying the relationship between action entropy and task completion (i.e., Q-value) reveals that improving high-entropy actions contributes more positively to task success.Hence, we propose a tailored training pipeline comprising hybrid supervised fine-tuning as a cold start, followed by online reinforcement learning with the proposed hybrid reasoning strategy to explicitly activate reasoning only for high-entropy actions, significantly reducing computational overhead while improving decision quality. Extensive experiments on the \textsc{CHORES}-$\mathbb{S}$ ObjectNav benchmark showcases that HiRO-Nav achieves a better trade-off between success rates and token efficiency than both dense-thinking and no-thinking baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HiRO-Nav：混合推理实现高效具身导航
基于大型推理模型（LRMs）构建的具身导航代理能够处理复杂的多模态环境输入，并在每一步执行基于环境的推理，以改进长时程任务的序列决策。然而，一个关键问题仍然存在：如何智能且高效地利用LRMs的推理能力来处理长时程导航任务？在简单场景中，代理应能反射性地行动，而在复杂场景中则应在行动前进行审慎推理。为此，我们提出了混合推理导航（HiRO-Nav）代理，这是首类能够根据自身动作熵自适应决定每一步是否执行推理的代理。具体而言，通过分析代理在导航轨迹中动作熵的演变，我们发现仅有少量动作表现出高熵，而这些动作通常引导代理进入新场景或接近关键物体。进一步研究动作熵与任务完成度（即Q值）的关系表明，改进高熵动作对任务成功的贡献更为显著。因此，我们设计了一个定制化的训练流程：首先通过混合监督微调进行冷启动，随后结合所提出的混合推理策略进行在线强化学习，仅对高熵动作显式激活推理，从而在提升决策质量的同时显著降低计算开销。在CHORES-S ObjectNav基准上的大量实验表明，HiRO-Nav在成功率和计算效率之间取得了比密集推理和无推理基线更优的平衡。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inefficiency of large reasoning models (LRMs) in embodied navigation, where constant step-by-step reasoning is computationally costly. To intelligently balance reflexive action and deliberate reasoning, the authors propose HiRO-Nav, an agent that adaptively triggers reasoning only at high-entropy decision points, identified via action entropy analysis which shows such moments correlate with novel scenes or critical objects. Through a training pipeline combining hybrid supervised fine-tuning and online reinforcement learning with this selective reasoning strategy, experiments on the CHORES-S ObjectNav benchmark demonstrate that HiRO-Nav achieves higher success rates with significantly reduced computational overhead compared to dense-thinking and no-thinking baselines, offering a superior trade-off between performance and efficiency.
本文针对大型推理模型在具身导航中持续推理导致计算效率低下的问题，提出了一种智能平衡反射性行动与深思熟虑推理的方法。作者设计了HiRO-Nav智能体，它通过分析动作熵的变化，自适应地仅在熵值高的决策点（通常对应新场景或关键物体）触发推理，从而减少计算开销。采用混合监督微调与在线强化学习的训练流程，结合这一选择性推理策略，在CHORES-S ObjectNav基准测试上的实验表明，HiRO-Nav相比持续推理和无推理基线，在成功率和计算效率之间取得了更优的平衡，实现了更高的任务完成率与更低的资源消耗。
Introducing Echo Networks for Computational Neuroevolution
Authors: Christian Kroos, Fabian Küch
First: 2026-04-09T13:06:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T13:06:25+00:00
Comments: Accepted for AMLDS 2026 (International Conference on Advanced Machine Learning and Data Science)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
For applications on the extreme edge, minimal networks of only a few dozen artificial neurons for event detection and classification in discrete time signals would be highly desirable. Feed-forward networks, RNNs, and CNNs evolved through evolutionary algorithms can all be successful in this respect but pose the problem of allowing little systematicity in mutation and recombination if the standard direct genetic encoding of the weights is used (as for instance in the classic NEAT algorithm). We therefore introduce Echo Networks, a type of recurrent network that consists of the connection matrix only, with the source neurons of the synapses represented as rows, destination neurons as columns and weights as entries. There are no layers, and connections between neurons can be bidirectional but are technically all recurrent. Input and output can be arbitrarily assigned to any of the neurons and only use an additional (optional) function in their computational path, e.g., a sigmoid to obtain a binary classification output. We evaluated Echo Networks successfully on the classification of electrocardiography signals but see the most promising potential in their genome representation as a single matrix, allowing matrix computations and factorisations as mutation and recombination operators.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向计算神经进化的回声网络介绍
在极端边缘应用中，仅需数十个人工神经元的最小化网络对离散时间信号进行事件检测与分类具有显著优势。通过进化算法演化的前馈网络、循环神经网络和卷积神经网络虽能胜任，但若采用标准权重直接遗传编码（如经典NEAT算法），将导致突变与重组过程缺乏系统性。为此我们提出回声网络——一种仅由连接矩阵构成的循环网络：突触源神经元对应矩阵行，目标神经元对应列，权重作为矩阵元素。该网络无层级结构，神经元间可双向连接（技术上均为循环连接）。输入输出可任意指派给任意神经元，仅需在计算路径中添加额外（可选）函数（如通过S型函数获得二分类输出）。我们已成功将回声网络应用于心电图信号分类任务，其最具潜力的特性在于基因组可表示为单一矩阵，支持以矩阵运算和分解作为突变与重组算子。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is the need for extremely compact neural networks suitable for edge computing, where traditional network architectures like feed-forward, RNNs, and CNNs evolved via direct weight encoding can limit systematic mutation and recombination. The method introduces Echo Networks, a recurrent network type represented solely by a connection matrix with rows as source neurons, columns as destination neurons, and entries as weights, eliminating layers and allowing arbitrary input/output neuron assignment with optional activation functions. Experimental results demonstrate successful classification of electrocardiography signals, with the key advantage being the matrix-based genome enabling matrix computations and factorizations for efficient evolutionary operators.
本研究的动机是满足边缘计算对极紧凑神经网络的需求，传统网络架构如通过直接权重编码进化的前馈网络、循环神经网络和卷积神经网络在系统化突变和重组方面存在局限。方法上引入了回声网络，这是一种仅由连接矩阵表示的循环网络，矩阵行代表源神经元、列代表目标神经元、元素代表权重，去除了网络层，允许任意分配输入输出神经元并可选激活函数。实验结果表明，该网络在心电信号分类任务上取得成功，其核心优势在于基于矩阵的基因组表示，支持矩阵计算和分解作为高效的进化操作符。
MedVR: Annotation-Free Medical Visual Reasoning via Agentic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zheng Jiang, Heng Guo, Chengyu Fang, Changchen Xiao, Xinyang Hu, Lifeng Sun, Minfeng Xu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-04-09T13:04:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T13:04:49+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Medical Vision-Language Models (VLMs) hold immense promise for complex clinical tasks, but their reasoning capabilities are often constrained by text-only paradigms that fail to ground inferences in visual evidence. This limitation not only curtails performance on tasks requiring fine-grained visual analysis but also introduces risks of visual hallucination in safety-critical applications. Thus, we introduce MedVR, a novel reinforcement learning framework that enables annotation-free visual reasoning for medical VLMs. Its core innovation lies in two synergistic mechanisms: Entropy-guided Visual Regrounding (EVR) uses model uncertainty to direct exploration, while Consensus-based Credit Assignment (CCA) distills pseudo-supervision from rollout agreement. Without any human annotations for intermediate steps, MedVR achieves state-of-the-art performance on diverse public medical VQA benchmarks, significantly outperforming existing models. By learning to reason directly with visual evidence, MedVR promotes the robustness and transparency essential for accelerating the clinical deployment of medical AI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MedVR：基于智能体强化学习的免标注医学视觉推理
医学视觉语言模型在复杂临床任务中前景广阔，但其推理能力常受限于纯文本范式，难以将推断建立在视觉证据之上。这一局限不仅削弱了需要细粒度视觉分析任务的性能，还在安全关键应用中带来视觉幻觉风险。为此，我们提出MedVR——一种创新的强化学习框架，可实现医学视觉语言模型的免标注视觉推理。其核心创新在于两个协同机制：熵引导视觉重定位利用模型不确定性指导探索，而基于共识的信用分配则从推演一致性中提炼伪监督信号。在无需任何中间步骤人工标注的情况下，MedVR在多个公共医学视觉问答基准测试中取得最先进性能，显著超越现有模型。通过学习直接基于视觉证据进行推理，MedVR提升了医学AI临床部署所必需的鲁棒性与可解释性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of text-only paradigms in medical Vision-Language Models (VLMs), which risk visual hallucination and lack visual grounding for fine-grained clinical analysis, this paper introduces MedVR, a reinforcement learning framework for annotation-free visual reasoning. The method employs two synergistic mechanisms: Entropy-guided Visual Regrounding (EVR) uses model uncertainty to direct exploration, and Consensus-based Credit Assignment (CCA) distills pseudo-supervision from rollout agreement. Experimental results show that MedVR achieves state-of-the-art performance on diverse medical VQA benchmarks without human annotations for intermediate steps, significantly outperforming existing models and enhancing robustness and transparency for clinical deployment.
针对医学视觉语言模型仅依赖文本范式所导致的视觉幻觉风险及细粒度视觉分析中视觉证据缺失的问题，本文提出了MedVR，一种基于强化学习的免标注视觉推理框架。该方法包含两个协同机制：熵引导视觉重定位利用模型不确定性指导探索，而基于共识的信用分配则从推演一致性中提炼伪监督信号。实验结果表明，在无需人工标注中间步骤的情况下，MedVR在多个公开医学视觉问答基准上取得了最先进的性能，显著优于现有模型，提升了临床部署所需的鲁棒性与可解释性。
Aligning Agents via Planning: A Benchmark for Trajectory-Level Reward Modeling
Authors: Jiaxuan Wang, Yulan Hu, Wenjin Yang, Zheng Pan, Xin Li, Lan-Zhe Guo
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-09T12:35:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T12:35:06+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 5 figures, accepted to ACL 2026 main conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In classical Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF), Reward Models (RMs) serve as the fundamental signal provider for model alignment. As Large Language Models evolve into agentic systems capable of autonomous tool invocation and complex reasoning, the paradigm of reward modeling faces unprecedented challenges--most notably, the lack of benchmarks specifically designed to assess RM capabilities within tool-integrated environments. To address this gap, we present Plan-RewardBench, a trajectory-level preference benchmark designed to evaluate how well judges distinguish preferred versus distractor agent trajectories in complex tool-using scenarios. Plan-RewardBench covers four representative task families -- (i) Safety Refusal, (ii) Tool-Irrelevance / Unavailability, (iii) Complex Planning, and (iv) Robust Error Recovery -- comprising validated positive trajectories and confusable hard negatives constructed via multi-model natural rollouts, rule-based perturbations, and minimal-edit LLM perturbations. We benchmark representative RMs (generative, discriminative, and LLM-as-Judge) under a unified pairwise protocol, reporting accuracy trends across varying trajectory lengths and task categories. Furthermore, we provide diagnostic analyses of prevalent failure modes. Our results reveal that all three evaluator families face substantial challenges, with performance degrading sharply on long-horizon trajectories, underscoring the necessity for specialized training in agentic, trajectory-level reward modeling. Ultimately, Plan-RewardBench aims to serve as both a practical evaluation suite and a reusable blueprint for constructing agentic planning preference data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过规划对齐智能体：轨迹级奖励建模的基准测试
在经典的人类反馈强化学习中，奖励模型是模型对齐的核心信号源。随着大语言模型演变为能够自主调用工具和进行复杂推理的智能体系统，奖励建模范式面临前所未有的挑战——最突出的是缺乏专门评估工具集成环境中RM能力的基准。为填补这一空白，我们提出了Plan-RewardBench：一个轨迹级偏好基准，旨在评估评判者在复杂工具使用场景中区分优选与干扰智能体轨迹的能力。该基准涵盖四大代表性任务族——安全拒绝、工具无关/不可用、复杂规划、鲁棒错误恢复——包含通过多模型自然推演、基于规则的扰动和最小编辑LLM扰动构建的已验证正例轨迹与易混淆硬负例。我们在统一成对协议下对代表性RM进行基准测试，报告了不同轨迹长度和任务类别的准确率趋势，并对常见失败模式进行诊断分析。结果表明，三类评估器均面临显著挑战，在长程轨迹上性能急剧下降，凸显了智能体轨迹级奖励建模专业化训练的必要性。Plan-RewardBench旨在同时作为实践评估套件和可复用的智能体规划偏好数据构建蓝图。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is the lack of benchmarks to evaluate reward models (RMs) in complex, tool-using agent environments, a critical gap as large language models evolve into autonomous agents. The method introduces Plan-RewardBench, a trajectory-level preference benchmark covering four task families—Safety Refusal, Tool-Irrelevance/Unavailability, Complex Planning, and Robust Error Recovery—with positive and hard-negative trajectories constructed via multi-model rollouts and perturbations. The main experimental results show that benchmarked RMs, including generative, discriminative, and LLM-as-Judge models, all face substantial challenges, with accuracy degrading sharply on long-horizon trajectories, highlighting the need for specialized training in agentic reward modeling.
本研究的动机在于，随着大语言模型演变为自主智能体，缺乏专门评估复杂工具使用环境中奖励模型能力的基准。方法上，研究提出了Plan-RewardBench这一轨迹级偏好基准，涵盖安全拒绝、工具无关/不可用、复杂规划和鲁棒错误恢复四个任务族，并通过多模型自然生成、基于规则的扰动和最小编辑LLM扰动构建了正例与困难负例轨迹。主要实验结果表明，所评估的生成式、判别式和LLM-as-Judge奖励模型均面临显著挑战，在长视野轨迹上性能急剧下降，这凸显了针对智能体轨迹级奖励模型进行专门训练的必要性。
Value-Guidance MeanFlow for Offline Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Teng Pang, Zhiqiang Dong, Yan Zhang, Rongjian Xu, Guoqiang Wu, Yilong Yin
First: 2026-04-09T12:31:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T12:31:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) aims to learn the optimal joint policy from pre-collected datasets, requiring a trade-off between maximizing global returns and mitigating distribution shift from offline data. Recent studies use diffusion or flow generative models to capture complex joint policy behaviors among agents; however, they typically rely on multi-step iterative sampling, thereby reducing training and inference efficiency. Although further research improves sampling efficiency through methods like distillation, it remains sensitive to the behavior regularization coefficient. To address the above-mentioned issues, we propose Value Guidance Multi-agent MeanFlow Policy (VGM$^2$P), a simple yet effective flow-based policy learning framework that enables efficient action generation with coefficient-insensitive conditional behavior cloning. Specifically, VGM$^2$P uses global advantage values to guide agent collaboration, treating optimal policy learning as conditional behavior cloning. Additionally, to improve policy expressiveness and inference efficiency in multi-agent scenarios, it leverages classifier-free guidance MeanFlow for both policy training and execution. Experiments on tasks with both discrete and continuous action spaces demonstrate that, even when trained solely via conditional behavior cloning, VGM$^2$P efficiently achieves performance comparable to state-of-the-art methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离线多智能体强化学习的价值引导均值流方法
离线多智能体强化学习（MARL）旨在从预收集数据集中学习最优联合策略，需在最大化全局回报与缓解离线数据分布偏移间取得平衡。现有研究采用扩散或流生成模型捕捉智能体间复杂联合策略行为，但通常依赖多步迭代采样，降低了训练与推理效率。尽管后续研究通过蒸馏等方法提升采样效率，其对行为正则化系数仍较敏感。为解决上述问题，本文提出价值引导多智能体均值流策略（VGM²P），这是一种简洁高效的基于流的策略学习框架，能够通过系数不敏感的条件行为克隆实现高效动作生成。具体而言，VGM²P利用全局优势值引导智能体协作，将最优策略学习视为条件行为克隆问题。同时，为提升多智能体场景的策略表达能力与推理效率，该框架在策略训练与执行中均采用无分类器引导的均值流方法。在离散与连续动作空间任务上的实验表明，即使仅通过条件行为克隆训练，VGM²P仍能高效达到与前沿方法相当的性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge in offline multi-agent reinforcement learning of balancing global return maximization with mitigating distribution shift, noting that existing flow or diffusion models suffer from inefficient multi-step sampling and sensitivity to regularization coefficients. The proposed method, Value Guidance Multi-agent MeanFlow Policy (VGM²P), introduces a flow-based framework that uses global advantage values to guide agent collaboration, framing optimal policy learning as coefficient-insensitive conditional behavior cloning, and employs classifier-free guidance MeanFlow to enhance policy expressiveness and inference efficiency. Experimental results on tasks with discrete and continuous action spaces show that VGM²P, trained solely via conditional behavior cloning, achieves performance competitive with state-of-the-art methods while maintaining high efficiency.
本文针对离线多智能体强化学习中平衡全局回报最大化与缓解分布偏移的挑战，指出现有基于流或扩散模型的方法存在多步采样效率低且对正则化系数敏感的问题。所提出的方法，即价值引导多智能体均值流策略（VGM²P），引入了一个基于流的框架，利用全局优势值指导智能体协作，将最优策略学习构建为对系数不敏感的条件行为克隆，并采用无分类器引导的均值流来提升策略表达能力和推理效率。在离散和连续动作空间任务上的实验结果表明，仅通过条件行为克隆训练的VGM²P能够高效实现与先进方法相当的性能。
ViVa: A Video-Generative Value Model for Robot Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jindi Lv, Hao Li, Jie Li, Yifei Nie, Fankun Kong, Yang Wang, Xiaofeng Wang, Zheng Zhu, Chaojun Ni, Qiuping Deng, Hengtao Li, Jiancheng Lv, Guan Huang
First: 2026-04-09T12:28:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T12:28:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision-language-action (VLA) models have advanced robot manipulation through large-scale pretraining, but real-world deployment remains challenging due to partial observability and delayed feedback. Reinforcement learning addresses this via value functions, which assess task progress and guide policy improvement. However, existing value models built on vision-language models (VLMs) struggle to capture temporal dynamics, undermining reliable value estimation in long-horizon tasks. In this paper, we propose ViVa, a video-generative value model that repurposes a pretrained video generator for value estimation. Taking the current observation and robot proprioception as input, ViVa jointly predicts future proprioception and a scalar value for the current state. By leveraging the spatiotemporal priors of a pretrained video generator, our approach grounds value estimation in anticipated embodiment dynamics, moving beyond static snapshots to intrinsically couple value with foresight. Integrated into RECAP, ViVa delivers substantial improvements on real-world box assembly. Qualitative analysis across all three tasks confirms that ViVa produces more reliable value signals, accurately reflecting task progress. By leveraging spatiotemporal priors from video corpora, ViVa also generalizes to novel objects, highlighting the promise of video-generative models for value estimation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ViVa：面向机器人强化学习的视频生成式价值模型
视觉-语言-动作模型通过大规模预训练推动了机器人操作的发展，但部分可观测性和延迟反馈使实际部署仍面临挑战。强化学习通过价值函数评估任务进度并指导策略改进，但现有基于视觉-语言模型的价值模型难以捕捉时序动态，影响长周期任务中的价值估计可靠性。本文提出ViVa——一种将预训练视频生成器重构用于价值估计的视频生成式价值模型。该模型以当前观测和机器人本体感知为输入，联合预测未来本体感知和当前状态的标量价值。通过利用预训练视频生成器的时空先验，我们的方法将价值估计锚定在预期的具身动态中，突破静态快照局限，实现价值与前瞻性的本质耦合。集成至RECAP框架后，ViVa在真实世界箱体组装任务中取得显著提升。三项任务的定性分析证实，ViVa能生成更可靠的价值信号，准确反映任务进度。通过利用视频语料的时空先验，ViVa还能泛化至新物体，彰显视频生成模型在价值估计领域的潜力。

PEER: Unified Process-Outcome Reinforcement Learning for Structured Empathetic Reasoning
Authors: Yunxiao Wang, Meng Liu, Kaiyu Jiang, Bin Wen, Fan Yang, Tingting Gao, Lizi Liao
First: 2025-08-13T06:09:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T12:13:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Emotional support conversations require more than fluent responses. Supporters need to understand the seeker's situation and emotions, adopt an appropriate strategy, and respond in a natural, human-like manner. Despite advances in large language models, current systems often lack structured, psychology-informed reasoning. Additionally, it is challenging to enhance these systems through reinforcement learning because of unreliable reward signals. Moreover, reinforcement fine-tuning can amplify repetitive response patterns. We propose structured empathetic reasoning, which breaks support into three steps: conversation history analysis, multimodal emotional state inference, and strategy selection, prior to generating the final reply. To implement this, we introduce SER, a fine-grained dataset with step-level correctness labels and pairwise response preferences. We then present PEER, which uses GRPO with UnifiReward, a unified process-outcome reward model for evaluating both reasoning steps and final responses in multi-turn interactions. To reduce repetition, we enhance data with personality-based rewriting and down-weight redundant outputs. Comprehensive experiments show improved empathy, strategy alignment, and human-likeness without sacrificing diversity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PEER：面向结构化共情推理的统一过程-结果强化学习
情感支持对话不仅需要流畅的回应，还需支持者理解求助者的情境与情绪、采取合适策略并以自然拟人的方式响应。尽管大语言模型已有进展，现有系统常缺乏结构化、基于心理学原理的推理能力。此外，由于奖励信号不可靠，通过强化学习优化此类系统面临挑战，且强化微调可能加剧重复回应模式。本文提出结构化共情推理框架，将支持过程分解为三步：对话历史分析、多模态情绪状态推断和策略选择，最终生成回复。为实现该框架，我们引入SER数据集，其包含步骤级正确性标注和成对回应偏好。进而提出PEER模型，采用基于UnifiReward的GRPO方法——这是一个评估多轮交互中推理步骤与最终回复的统一过程-结果奖励模型。为降低重复性，我们通过人格化重写增强数据并对冗余输出降权。综合实验表明，该方法在保持多样性的同时显著提升了共情能力、策略匹配度与拟人性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for emotional support systems that go beyond fluent responses to incorporate structured, psychology-informed reasoning, this paper introduces structured empathetic reasoning, which decomposes support into three steps: analyzing conversation history, inferring multimodal emotional states, and selecting strategies before generating a reply. The method involves creating the SER dataset with step-level labels and pairwise preferences, and proposing PEER, a model that uses GRPO with UnifiReward, a unified reward model to evaluate both reasoning steps and final responses in multi-turn interactions, while mitigating repetition through personality-based rewriting and down-weighting redundant outputs. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach improves empathy, strategy alignment, and human-likeness without compromising diversity.
本文的动机是情感支持系统需要超越流畅的回复，融入结构化、基于心理学的推理，因此提出了结构化共情推理，将支持过程分解为三个步骤：分析对话历史、推断多模态情感状态、选择策略，然后生成最终回复。方法上，构建了具有步骤级标签和成对偏好的SER数据集，并提出了PEER模型，该模型使用GRPO与UnifiReward（一个统一奖励模型）来评估多轮交互中的推理步骤和最终回复，同时通过基于个性的重写和降低冗余输出的权重来减少重复。实验结果表明，该方法在保持多样性的同时，提升了共情能力、策略对齐度和拟人化程度。
Beyond Stochastic Exploration: What Makes Training Data Valuable for Agentic Search
Authors: Chuzhan Hao, Wenfeng Feng, Guochao Jiang, Guofeng Quan, Guohua Liu, Yuewei Zhang
First: 2026-04-09T11:44:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T11:44:44+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, ACL2026 Findings Accepted
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become an effective approach for advancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) through the strategic integration of external search engines. However, current RL-based search agents often rely on a process of stochastic exploration guided by carefully crafted outcome rewards, leading to inefficient reasoning trajectories and unstable training. To address these issues, we propose a novel framework, Hierarchical Experience (HiExp), to enhance the performance and training stability of search agents. Specifically, we extract empirical knowledge through contrastive analysis and a multi-level clustering mechanism, transforming raw reasoning trajectories into hierarchical experience knowledge. By leveraging experience-aligned training, we effectively regularize stochastic exploration, evolving it into a strategic and experience-driven search process. Extensive evaluations on multiple complex agentic search and mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that our approach not only achieves substantial performance gains but also exhibits strong cross-task and cross-algorithm generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越随机探索：训练数据如何提升智能搜索代理的价值

The paper addresses the inefficiency and instability in reinforcement learning (RL)-based search agents for large language models, which often rely on stochastic exploration guided by outcome rewards. To overcome this, the authors propose the Hierarchical Experience (HiExp) framework, which extracts empirical knowledge from reasoning trajectories via contrastive analysis and multi-level clustering, transforming them into hierarchical experience. This approach regularizes exploration into a strategic, experience-driven process. Analysis of Search Heuristics in the Multi-Armed Bandit Setting
Authors: Jasmin Brandt, Barbara Hammer, Timo Kötzing, Jurek Sander
First: 2026-04-09T11:27:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T11:27:59+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 5 figures, GECCO 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider the classic Multi-Armed Bandit setting to understand the exploration/exploitation tradeoffs made by different search heuristics. Since many search heuristics work by comparing different options (in evolutionary algorithms called "individuals"; in the Bandit literature called "arms"), we work with the "Dueling Bandits" setting. In each iteration, a comparison between different arms can be made; in the binary stochastic setting, each arm has a fixed winning probability against any other arm. A Condorcet winner is any arm that beats every other arm with a probability strictly higher than $1/2$. We show that evolutionary algorithms are rather bad at identifying the Condorcet winner: Even if the Condorcet winner beats every other arm with a probability $1-p$, the (1+1) EA, in its stationary distribution, chooses the Condorcet winner only with constant probability if $p=Ω(1/n)$. By contrast, we show that a simple EDA (based on the Max-Min Ant System with iteration-best update) will choose the Condorcet winner in its maintained distribution with probability $1-Θ(p)$. As a remedy for the (1+1) EA, we show how repeated duels can significantly boost the probability of the Condorcet winner in the stationary distribution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多臂老虎机设定下搜索启发式算法的分析
我们考虑经典的多臂老虎机设定，以理解不同搜索启发式算法在探索与利用之间的权衡。由于许多搜索启发式算法通过比较不同选项（在进化算法中称为“个体”，在老虎机文献中称为“臂”）来工作，我们采用“对决老虎机”设定。在每次迭代中，可以对不同臂进行比较；在二元随机设定下，每个臂相对于其他任意臂具有固定的获胜概率。孔多塞胜者是指以严格高于$1/2$的概率击败所有其他臂的臂。 我们证明进化算法在识别孔多塞胜者方面表现较差：即使孔多塞胜者以$1-p$的概率击败所有其他臂，(1+1) EA在其平稳分布中选择孔多塞胜者的概率仅为常数（若$p=Ω(1/n)$）。相比之下，我们证明一种简单的EDA（基于迭代最优更新的最大最小蚂蚁系统）在其维护的分布中以$1-Θ(p)$的概率选择孔多塞胜者。作为对(1+1) EA的改进方案，我们展示了重复对决如何显著提升孔多塞胜者在平稳分布中的概率。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates how different search heuristics manage the exploration-exploitation trade-off in the Multi-Armed Bandit problem, specifically using the Dueling Bandits model where arms are compared pairwise. The motivation is to analyze the effectiveness of evolutionary algorithms versus estimation-of-distribution algorithms in identifying a Condorcet winner—an arm that is superior to all others. The method involves theoretical analysis of the (1+1) EA and a simple EDA based on the Max-Min Ant System under a stochastic comparison model. The main experimental results show that the (1+1) EA performs poorly, selecting the Condorcet winner with only constant probability when its advantage is small, whereas the EDA achieves a probability close to one, and the paper further demonstrates that repeated duels can significantly improve the (1+1) EA's performance.

Prompt reinforcing for long-term planning of large language models
Authors: Hsien-Chin Lin, Benjamin Matthias Ruppik, Carel van Niekerk, Chia-Hao Shen, Michael Heck, Nurul Lubis, Renato Vukovic, Shutong Feng, Milica Gašić
First: 2025-10-07T13:30:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T10:26:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have achieved remarkable success in a wide range of natural language processing tasks and can be adapted through prompting. However, they remain suboptimal in multi-turn interactions, often relying on incorrect early assumptions and failing to track user goals over time, which makes such tasks particularly challenging. Prior works in dialogue systems have shown that long-term planning is essential for handling interactive tasks. In this work, we propose a prompt optimisation framework inspired by reinforcement learning, which enables such planning to take place by only modifying the task instruction prompt of the LLM-based agent. By generating turn-by-turn feedback and leveraging experience replay for prompt rewriting, our proposed method shows significant improvement in multi-turn tasks such as text-to-SQL and task-oriented dialogue. Moreover, it generalises across different LLM-based agents and can leverage diverse LLMs as meta-prompting agents. This warrants future research in reinforcement learning-inspired parameter-free optimisation methods.

Search-R3: Unifying Reasoning and Embedding in Large Language Models
Authors: Yuntao Gui, James Cheng
First: 2025-10-08T14:16:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T10:25:15+00:00
Comments: CHANGELOG: (1) Completed training of Search-R3-Large; (2) Corrected error formulation; (3) Added a `Discussion` section to the appendix. We appreciation to the anonymous reviewers
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Despite their remarkable natural language understanding capabilities, Large Language Models (LLMs) have been underutilized for retrieval tasks. We present Search-R3, a novel framework that addresses this limitation by adapting LLMs to generate search embeddings as a direct output of their reasoning process. Our approach exploits LLMs' chain-of-thought capabilities, allowing them to produce more effective embeddings by reasoning step-by-step through complex semantic analyses. We implement this through three complementary mechanisms. (1) a supervised learning stage enables the model's ability to produce quality embeddings, (2) a reinforcement learning (RL) methodology that optimizes embedding generation alongside reasoning, and (3) a specialized RL environment that efficiently handles evolving embedding representations without requiring complete corpus re-encoding at each training iteration. Our extensive evaluations on diverse benchmarks demonstrate that Search-R3 significantly outperforms prior methods by unifying the reasoning and embedding generation processes. This integrated post-training approach represents a substantial advancement in handling complex knowledge-intensive tasks that require both sophisticated reasoning and effective information retrieval. Project page: https://github.com/ytgui/Search-R3

We Still Don't Understand High-Dimensional Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Colin Doumont, Donney Fan, Natalie Maus, Jacob R. Gardner, Henry Moss, Geoff Pleiss
First: 2025-11-28T19:18:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T09:44:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Existing high-dimensional Bayesian optimization (BO) methods aim to overcome the curse of dimensionality by carefully encoding structural assumptions, from locality to sparsity to smoothness, into the optimization procedure. Surprisingly, we demonstrate that these approaches are outperformed by arguably the simplest method imaginable: Bayesian linear regression. After applying a geometric transformation to avoid boundary-seeking behavior, Gaussian processes with linear kernels match state-of-the-art performance on tasks with 60- to 6,000-dimensional search spaces. Linear models offer numerous advantages over their non-parametric counterparts: they afford closed-form sampling and their computation scales linearly with data, a fact we exploit on molecular optimization tasks with >20,000 observations. Coupled with empirical analyses, our results suggest the need to depart from past intuitions about BO methods in high-dimensions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：我们仍未理解高维贝叶斯优化
现有高维贝叶斯优化方法试图通过将结构假设（从局部性、稀疏性到平滑性）编码至优化过程来克服维度灾难。令人惊讶的是，我们发现这些方法的表现甚至不及可能设想的最简单方法：贝叶斯线性回归。通过应用几何变换避免边界趋近行为后，采用线性核的高斯过程在60至6000维搜索空间任务中达到了最先进性能。线性模型相比非参数模型具有多重优势：支持闭式采样，且计算复杂度随数据量线性增长——我们在超过20,000个观测的分子优化任务中验证了这一特性。结合实证分析，我们的结果表明需要重新审视过去对高维贝叶斯优化方法的直觉认知。

This paper challenges the prevailing intuition that complex structural assumptions are necessary for effective high-dimensional Bayesian optimization (BO), motivated by the observation that existing methods often underperform. The authors propose a surprisingly simple method: using Bayesian linear regression with a geometric transformation to prevent boundary-seeking behavior, which allows Gaussian processes with linear kernels to compete with state-of-the-art techniques.
