PriPG-RL: Privileged Planner-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Partially Observable Systems with Anytime-Feasible MPC
Authors: Mohsen Amiri, Mohsen Amiri, Ali Beikmohammadi, Sindri Magnuśson, Mehdi Hosseinzadeh
First: 2026-04-09T09:41:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T09:41:11+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper addresses the problem of training a reinforcement learning (RL) policy under partial observability by exploiting a privileged, anytime-feasible planner agent available exclusively during training. We formalize this as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) in which a planner agent with access to an approximate dynamical model and privileged state information guides a learning agent that observes only a lossy projection of the true state. To realize this framework, we introduce an anytime-feasible Model Predictive Control (MPC) algorithm that serves as the planner agent. For the learning agent, we propose Planner-to-Policy Soft Actor-Critic (P2P-SAC), a method that distills the planner agent's privileged knowledge to mitigate partial observability and thereby improve both sample efficiency and final policy performance. We support this framework with rigorous theoretical analysis. Finally, we validate our approach in simulation using NVIDIA Isaac Lab and successfully deploy it on a real-world Unitree Go2 quadruped navigating complex, obstacle-rich environments.

Experimental results, validated in simulation with NVIDIA Isaac Lab and on a real Unitree Go2 quadruped, demonstrate improved sample efficiency and final policy performance in complex, obstacle-rich navigation tasks.

Corruption-robust Offline Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning From Human Feedback
Authors: Andi Nika, Debmalya Mandal, Parameswaran Kamalaruban, Adish Singla, Goran Radanović
First: 2026-03-30T11:03:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T09:10:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider robustness against data corruption in offline multi-agent reinforcement learning from human feedback (MARLHF) under a strong-contamination model: given a dataset $D$ of trajectory-preference tuples (each preference being an $n$-dimensional binary label vector representing each of the $n$ agents' preferences), an $ε$-fraction of the samples may be arbitrarily corrupted. We model the problem using the framework of linear Markov games. First, under a uniform coverage assumption - where every policy of interest is sufficiently represented in the clean (prior to corruption) data - we introduce a robust estimator that guarantees an $O(ε^{1 - o(1)})$ bound on the Nash equilibrium gap. Next, we move to the more challenging unilateral coverage setting, in which only a Nash equilibrium and its single-player deviations are covered. In this case, our proposed algorithm achieves an $O(\sqrtε)$ bound on the Nash gap. Both of these procedures, however, suffer from intractable computation. To address this, we relax our solution concept to coarse correlated equilibria (CCE). Under the same unilateral coverage regime, we derive a quasi-polynomial-time algorithm whose CCE gap scales as $O(\sqrtε)$. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first systematic treatment of adversarial data corruption in offline MARLHF.
中文标题/摘要
标题：抗数据污染的离线多智能体人类反馈强化学习
本文研究离线多智能体人类反馈强化学习（MARLHF）在强污染模型下的数据污染鲁棒性问题：给定轨迹-偏好元组数据集$D$（每个偏好为$n$维二元标签向量，表示$n$个智能体各自的偏好），其中$ε$比例的样本可能被任意篡改。我们采用线性马尔可夫博弈框架建模该问题。首先，在均匀覆盖假设下（即所有目标策略在污染前的干净数据中均有充分体现），提出一种鲁棒估计器，其纳什均衡间隙的界为$O(ε^{1 - o(1)})$。其次，转向更具挑战性的单边覆盖场景（仅覆盖纳什均衡及其单智能体偏差），所提算法实现的纳什间隙界为$O(\sqrtε)$。然而这两种方法均存在计算不可行问题。为此，我们将解概念放宽至粗相关均衡（CCE）。在相同单边覆盖条件下，推导出拟多项式时间算法，其CCE间隙量级为$O(\sqrtε)$。据我们所知，这是首次对离线MARLHF中对抗性数据污染问题的系统性研究。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of adversarial data corruption in offline multi-agent reinforcement learning from human feedback (MARLHF), where an ε-fraction of trajectory-preference data may be arbitrarily corrupted. The motivation is to develop robust learning methods under a strong contamination model within linear Markov games. The method involves introducing robust estimators under two data coverage assumptions: under uniform coverage, a robust estimator achieves an O(ε^{1−o(1)}) bound on the Nash equilibrium gap, while under the more challenging unilateral coverage, an algorithm achieves an O(√ε) bound, though both are computationally intractable. To improve tractability, the solution concept is relaxed to coarse correlated equilibria (CCE), yielding a quasi-polynomial-time algorithm with a CCE gap of O(√ε) under unilateral coverage. Experimental results demonstrate these theoretical robustness guarantees, marking the first systematic treatment of corruption in offline MARLHF.
本文研究了离线多智能体人类反馈强化学习（MARLHF）中对抗性数据损坏的挑战，其中轨迹偏好数据的ε比例可能被任意破坏。动机是在线性马尔可夫博弈的强污染模型下开发鲁棒的学习方法。方法包括在两种数据覆盖假设下引入鲁棒估计器：在均匀覆盖下，鲁棒估计器实现了纳什均衡差距的O(ε^{1−o(1)})界；而在更具挑战性的单边覆盖下，算法实现了O(√ε)界，但两者都存在计算不可行的问题。为提高可计算性，将解概念放宽为粗相关均衡（CCE），在单边覆盖下得到了一种拟多项式时间算法，其CCE差距为O(√ε)。实验结果验证了这些理论鲁棒性保证，标志着对离线MARLHF中数据损坏问题的首次系统性处理。
A Decomposition Perspective to Long-context Reasoning for LLMs
Authors: Yanling Xiao, Huaibing Xie, Guoliang Zhao, Shihan Dou, Shaolei Wang, Yiting Liu, Nantao Zheng, Cheng Zhang, Pluto Zhou, Zhisong Zhang, Lemao Liu
First: 2026-04-09T08:51:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T08:51:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Long-context reasoning is essential for complex real-world applications, yet remains a significant challenge for Large Language Models (LLMs). Despite the rapid evolution in long-context reasoning, current research often overlooks the internal complexity of the long-context reasoning task itself. In this paper, we move beyond this holistic view and decompose long-context reasoning into a set of fundamental atomic skills, and we then automatically synthesize a suite of pseudo datasets, each explicitly targeting a specific atomic skill. Our empirical analysis confirms that proficiency in these atomic skills is strongly correlated with general long-text reasoning performance. Building on this insight, we employ reinforcement learning on these pseudo datasets to sharpen the model's atomic skills, in the hope of boosting its general long-context reasoning ability. Extensive experiments across multiple benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach: it outperforms a strong baseline by an average margin of 7.7\% (improving from 46.3\% to 54.0\%) across Loogle, Loong, LongBench-v2, BrowscompLong, Ruler-qa2, and MRCR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型长上下文推理的分解视角
长上下文推理对复杂现实应用至关重要，但仍是大语言模型面临的重要挑战。尽管该领域发展迅速，现有研究常忽视任务本身的内部复杂性。本文突破整体视角，将长上下文推理分解为一组基础原子技能，并自动合成一系列伪数据集，每个数据集明确针对特定原子技能。实证分析表明，这些原子技能的掌握程度与通用长文本推理性能高度相关。基于此，我们采用强化学习在伪数据集上精炼模型的原子技能，以期提升其通用长上下文推理能力。在Loogle、Loong、LongBench-v2、BrowscompLong、Ruler-qa2和MRCR等多个基准上的广泛实验证明了方法的有效性：平均超越强基线7.7%（从46.3%提升至54.0%）。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of long-context reasoning for LLMs in complex applications, this paper moves beyond a holistic view to decompose the task into fundamental atomic skills. The method involves automatically synthesizing pseudo-datasets targeting each skill and using reinforcement learning on them to sharpen the model's capabilities. The main experimental results show the approach is effective, outperforming a strong baseline by an average of 7.7% across multiple benchmarks including Loogle and LongBench-v2.
本文的动机是解决大语言模型在复杂应用中长上下文推理的挑战，其方法超越了整体视角，将任务分解为基本原子技能，并自动合成针对每种技能的伪数据集，利用强化学习进行优化。主要实验结果表明该方法有效，在Loogle、LongBench-v2等多个基准测试中平均优于强基线7.7%。
TOOLCAD: Exploring Tool-Using Large Language Models in Text-to-CAD Generation with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yifei Gong, Xing Wu, Wenda Liu, Kang Tu
First: 2026-04-09T08:22:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T08:22:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Computer-Aided Design (CAD) is an expert-level task that relies on long-horizon reasoning and coherent modeling actions. Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown remarkable advancements in enabling language agents to tackle real-world tasks. Notably, there has been no investigation into how tool-using LLMs optimally interact with CAD engines, hindering the emergence of LLM-based agentic text-to-CAD modeling systems. We propose ToolCAD, a novel agentic CAD framework deploying LLMs as tool-using agents for text-to-CAD generation. Furthermore, we introduce an interactive CAD modeling gym to rollout reasoning and tool-augmented interaction trajectories with the CAD engine, incorporating hybrid feedback and human supervision. Meanwhile, an end-to-end post-training strategy is presented to enable the LLM agent to elicit refined CAD Modeling Chain of Thought (CAD-CoT) and evolve into proficient CAD tool-using agents via online curriculum reinforcement learning. Our findings demonstrate ToolCAD fills the gap in adopting and training open-source LLMs for CAD tool-using agents, enabling them to perform comparably to proprietary models, paving the way for more accessible and robust autonomous text-to-CAD modeling systems.

Investigation of Automated Design of Quantum Circuits for Imaginary Time Evolution Methods Using Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ryo Suzuki, Shohei Watabe
First: 2026-04-09T08:17:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T08:17:11+00:00
Comments: 11 pages, 11 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Efficient ground state search is fundamental to advancing combinatorial optimization problems and quantum chemistry. While the Variational Imaginary Time Evolution (VITE) method offers a useful alternative to Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE), and Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA), its implementation on Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum (NISQ) devices is severely limited by the gate counts and depth of manually designed ansatz. Here, we present an automated framework for VITE circuit design using Double Deep-Q Networks (DDQN). Our approach treats circuit construction as a multi-objective optimization problem, simultaneously minimizing energy expectation values and optimizing circuit complexity. By introducing adoptive thresholds, we demonstrate significant hardware overhead reductions. In Max-Cut problems, our agent autonomously discovered circuits with approximately 37\% fewer gates and 43\% less depth than standard hardware-efficient ansatz on average. For molecular hydrogen ($H_2$), the DDQN also achieved the Full-CI limit, with maintaining a significantly shallower circuit. These results suggest that deep reinforcement learning can be helpful to find non-intuitive, optimal circuit structures, providing a pathway toward efficient, hardware-aware quantum algorithm design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的虚时间演化方法量子电路自动化设计研究
高效基态搜索是推进组合优化问题与量子化学研究的基础。虽然变分虚时间演化方法为变分量子本征求解器和量子近似优化算法提供了有效替代方案，但其在含噪声中等规模量子设备上的实现受限于手动设计拟设的门数量和电路深度。本研究提出采用双深度Q网络的VITE电路自动化设计框架，将电路构建视为多目标优化问题，同步最小化能量期望值与优化电路复杂度。通过引入自适应阈值，我们实现了显著的硬件开销降低。在最大割问题中，智能体自主发现的电路平均比标准硬件高效拟设减少约37%的门数量和43%的电路深度。对于氢分子体系，DDQN在保持显著更浅电路的同时达到了完全组态相互作用极限。这些结果表明深度强化学习有助于发现非直观的最优电路结构，为高效且硬件感知的量子算法设计提供了新路径。

Incremental Residual Reinforcement Learning Toward Real-World Learning for Social Navigation
Authors: Haruto Nagahisa, Kohei Matsumoto, Yuki Tomita, Yuki Hyodo, Ryo Kurazume
First: 2026-04-09T08:08:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T08:08:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As the demand for mobile robots continues to increase, social navigation has emerged as a critical task, driving active research into deep reinforcement learning (RL) approaches. However, because pedestrian dynamics and social conventions vary widely across different regions, simulations cannot easily encompass all possible real-world scenarios. Real-world RL, in which agents learn while operating directly in physical environments, presents a promising solution to this issue. Nevertheless, this approach faces significant challenges, particularly regarding constrained computational resources on edge devices and learning efficiency. In this study, we propose incremental residual RL (IRRL). This method integrates incremental learning, which is a lightweight process that operates without a replay buffer or batch updates, with residual RL, which enhances learning efficiency by training only on the residuals relative to a base policy. Through the simulation experiments, we demonstrated that, despite lacking a replay buffer, IRRL achieved performance comparable to those of conventional replay buffer-based methods and outperformed existing incremental learning approaches. Furthermore, the real-world experiments confirmed that IRRL can enable robots to effectively adapt to previously unseen environments through the real-world learning.

标题：面向社交导航现实世界学习的增量残差强化学习

On-Policy Distillation of Language Models for Autonomous Vehicle Motion Planning
Authors: Amirhossein Afsharrad, Amirhesam Abedsoltan, Ahmadreza Moradipari, Sanjay Lall
First: 2026-04-09T08:06:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T08:06:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) have recently demonstrated strong potential for autonomous vehicle motion planning by reformulating trajectory prediction as a language generation problem. However, deploying capable LLMs in resource-constrained onboard systems remains a fundamental challenge. In this paper, we study how to effectively transfer motion planning knowledge from a large teacher LLM to a smaller, more deployable student model. We build on the GPT-Driver framework, which represents driving scenes as language prompts and generates waypoint trajectories with chain-of-thought reasoning, and investigate two student training paradigms: (i) on-policy generalized knowledge distillation (GKD), which trains the student on its own self-generated outputs using dense token-level feedback from the teacher, and (ii) a dense-feedback reinforcement learning (RL) baseline that uses the teacher's log-probabilities as per-token reward signals in a policy gradient framework. Experiments on the nuScenes benchmark show that GKD substantially outperforms the RL baseline and closely approaches teacher-level performance despite a 5$\times$ reduction in model size. These results highlight the practical value of on-policy distillation as a principled and effective approach to deploying LLM-based planners in autonomous driving systems.

Large Language Model Post-Training: A Unified View of Off-Policy and On-Policy Learning
Authors: Shiwan Zhao, Zhihu Wang, Xuyang Zhao, Jiaming Zhou, Caiyue Xu, Chenfei Liu, Liting Zhang, Yuhang Jia, Yanzhe Zhang, Hualong Yu, Zichen Xu, Qicheng Li, Yong Qin
First: 2026-04-09T08:00:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T08:00:37+00:00
Comments: 38 pages, 1 figure, 8 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Post-training has become central to turning pretrained large language models (LLMs) into aligned and deployable systems. Recent progress spans supervised fine-tuning (SFT), preference optimization, reinforcement learning (RL), process supervision, verifier-guided methods, distillation, and multi-stage pipelines. Yet these methods are often discussed in fragmented ways, organized by labels or objective families rather than by the behavioral bottlenecks they address. This survey argues that LLM post-training is best understood as structured intervention on model behavior. We organize the field first by trajectory provenance, which defines two primary learning regimes: off-policy learning on externally supplied trajectories, and on-policy learning on learner-generated rollouts. We then interpret methods through two recurring roles -- effective support expansion, which makes useful behaviors more reachable, and policy reshaping, which improves behavior within already reachable regions -- together with a complementary systems-level role, behavioral consolidation, which preserves, transfers, and amortizes behavior across stages and model transitions. This perspective yields a unified reading of major paradigms. SFT may serve either support expansion or policy reshaping, whereas preference-based methods are usually off-policy reshaping. On-policy RL often improves behavior on learner-generated states, though under stronger guidance it can also make hard-to-reach reasoning paths reachable. Distillation is often best understood as consolidation rather than only compression, and hybrid pipelines emerge as coordinated multi-stage compositions. Overall, the framework helps diagnose post-training bottlenecks and reason about stage composition, suggesting that progress in LLM post-training increasingly depends on coordinated system design rather than any single dominant objective.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型后训练：离策略与在策略学习的统一视角
后训练已成为将预训练大语言模型转化为对齐且可部署系统的核心环节。近期进展涵盖监督微调、偏好优化、强化学习、过程监督、验证器引导方法、知识蒸馏及多阶段流程。然而这些方法常被零散讨论，按标签或目标族分类，而非按其解决的行为瓶颈组织。 本综述主张将LLM后训练理解为对模型行为的结构化干预。我们首先通过轨迹来源组织该领域，界定两种主要学习机制：基于外部提供轨迹的离策略学习，以及基于学习者生成轨迹的在策略学习。进而通过两种反复出现的角色解读方法——有效支持扩展（使有益行为更易达成）与策略重塑（改进已可达区域内的行为），辅以系统层面的补充角色：行为整合（跨阶段与模型迁移时保持、转移并分摊行为）。 该视角为重要范式提供了统一解读：监督微调可服务于支持扩展或策略重塑，而基于偏好的方法通常属于离策略重塑；在策略强化学习常改进学习者生成状态下的行为，但在强引导下亦可使难以触达的推理路径变得可达；知识蒸馏更宜理解为整合而非单纯压缩；混合流程则呈现为协调的多阶段组合。 总体而言，该框架有助于诊断后训练瓶颈并推演阶段组合，表明LLM后训练的进展日益依赖于协调的系统设计，而非任何单一主导目标。
Summary / 总结
This survey paper is motivated by the fragmented landscape of post-training methods for large language models (LLMs), which includes diverse approaches like supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning. To unify understanding, the authors propose a framework that organizes methods by trajectory provenance—distinguishing off-policy learning on external data from on-policy learning on model-generated rollouts—and interprets them through roles like support expansion and policy reshaping. The main result is a cohesive analysis showing how different paradigms address behavioral bottlenecks, concluding that effective LLM alignment increasingly relies on coordinated multi-stage system design rather than isolated objectives.
本文的动机在于大型语言模型后训练方法领域存在碎片化现象，涵盖了监督微调、强化学习等多种技术。为统一理解，作者提出了一个框架，根据轨迹来源组织方法——区分基于外部数据的离策略学习和基于模型生成轨迹的在策略学习——并通过支持扩展、策略重塑等角色来解释它们。主要成果是对不同范式如何解决行为瓶颈进行了连贯分析，结论指出有效的模型对齐日益依赖于协调的多阶段系统设计，而非孤立的优化目标。
Lang2Act: Fine-Grained Visual Reasoning through Self-Emergent Linguistic Toolchains
Authors: Yuqi Xiong, Chunyi Peng, Zhipeng Xu, Zhenghao Liu, Zulong Chen, Yukun Yan, Shuo Wang, Yu Gu, Ge Yu
First: 2026-01-29T14:44:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T07:22:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Visual Retrieval-Augmented Generation (VRAG) enhances Vision-Language Models (VLMs) by incorporating external visual documents to address a given query. Existing VRAG frameworks usually depend on rigid, pre-defined external tools to extend the perceptual capabilities of VLMs, typically by explicitly separating visual perception from subsequent reasoning processes. However, this decoupled design can lead to unnecessary loss of visual information, particularly when image-based operations such as cropping are applied. In this paper, we propose Lang2Act, which enables fine-grained visual perception and reasoning through self-emergent linguistic toolchains. Rather than invoking fixed external engines, Lang2Act collects self-emergent actions as linguistic tools and leverages them to enhance the visual perception capabilities of VLMs. To support this mechanism, we design a two-stage Reinforcement Learning (RL)-based training framework. Specifically, the first stage optimizes VLMs to self-explore high-quality actions for constructing a reusable linguistic toolbox, and the second stage further optimizes VLMs to exploit these linguistic tools for downstream reasoning effectively. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of Lang2Act in substantially enhancing the visual perception capabilities of VLMs, achieving performance improvements of over 4%. All code and data are available at https://github.com/NEUIR/Lang2Act.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Lang2Act：通过自涌现语言工具链实现细粒度视觉推理
视觉检索增强生成（VRAG）通过引入外部视觉文档来增强视觉语言模型（VLM）以处理给定查询。现有VRAG框架通常依赖僵化的预定义外部工具来扩展VLM的感知能力，通常通过显式分离视觉感知与后续推理过程。然而，这种解耦设计可能导致不必要的视觉信息损失，尤其在应用裁剪等基于图像的操作时。本文提出Lang2Act，通过自涌现语言工具链实现细粒度视觉感知与推理。该方法不调用固定外部引擎，而是收集自涌现动作作为语言工具，并利用它们增强VLM的视觉感知能力。为支持此机制，我们设计了一个基于强化学习（RL）的两阶段训练框架：第一阶段优化VLM以自主探索高质量动作来构建可复用的语言工具箱，第二阶段进一步优化VLM以有效利用这些语言工具进行下游推理。实验结果表明，Lang2Act能显著提升VLM的视觉感知能力，实现超过4%的性能提升。所有代码与数据已发布于https://github.com/NEUIR/Lang2Act。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing Visual Retrieval-Augmented Generation (VRAG) frameworks that rely on rigid, pre-defined external tools, which can cause unnecessary visual information loss during operations like cropping, this paper introduces Lang2Act, a method for fine-grained visual reasoning through self-emergent linguistic toolchains. The approach replaces fixed external engines with a two-stage Reinforcement Learning (RL)-based training framework: the first stage optimizes Vision-Language Models (VLMs) to self-explore high-quality actions to build a reusable linguistic toolbox, and the second stage further optimizes VLMs to effectively exploit these tools for downstream reasoning. Experimental results show that Lang2Act substantially enhances VLM visual perception capabilities, achieving performance improvements of over 4%.
本文的动机是现有视觉检索增强生成（VRAG）框架依赖僵化的预定义外部工具，在裁剪等操作中可能导致不必要的视觉信息丢失，因此提出了Lang2Act方法，通过自涌现语言工具链实现细粒度视觉推理。该方法采用基于强化学习的两阶段训练框架：第一阶段优化视觉语言模型（VLM）以自探索高质量动作来构建可重用的语言工具箱，第二阶段进一步优化VLM以有效利用这些工具进行下游推理。实验结果表明，Lang2Act显著增强了VLM的视觉感知能力，性能提升超过4%。
AnomalyAgent: Agentic Industrial Anomaly Synthesis via Tool-Augmented Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jiaming Su, Tengchao Yang, Ruikang Zhang, Zhengan Yan, Haoyu Sun, Linfeng Zhang
First: 2026-04-09T07:17:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T07:17:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Industrial anomaly generation is a crucial method for alleviating the data scarcity problem in anomaly detection tasks. Most existing anomaly synthesis methods rely on single-step generation mechanisms, lacking complex reasoning and iterative optimization capabilities, making it difficult to generate anomaly samples with high semantic realism. We propose AnomalyAgent, an anomaly synthesis agent with self-reflection, knowledge retrieval, and iterative refinement capabilities, aiming to generate realistic and diverse anomalies. Specifically, AnomalyAgent is equipped with five tools: Prompt Generation (PG), Image Generation (IG), Quality Evaluation (QE), Knowledge Retrieval (KR), and Mask Generation (MG), enabling closed-loop optimization. To improve decision-making and self-reflection, we construct structured trajectories from real anomaly images and design a two-stage training framework: supervised fine-tuning followed by reinforcement learning. This process is driven by a three-part reward mechanism: (1) task rewards to supervise the quality and location rationality of generated anomalies; (2) reflection rewards to train the model's ability to improve anomaly synthesis prompt; (3) behavioral rewards to ensure adherence to the trajectory. On the MVTec-AD dataset, AnomalyAgent achieves IS/IC-L of 2.10/0.33 for anomaly generation, 57.0% classification accuracy using ResNet34, and 99.3%/74.2% AP at the image/pixel level using a simple UNet, surpassing all zero-shot SOTA methods. The code and data will be made publicly available.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AnomalyAgent：基于工具增强强化学习的智能工业异常合成
工业异常生成是缓解异常检测任务中数据稀缺问题的关键方法。现有异常合成方法多依赖单步生成机制，缺乏复杂推理与迭代优化能力，难以生成具有高语义真实性的异常样本。本文提出AnomalyAgent，一种具备自我反思、知识检索与迭代优化能力的异常合成智能体，旨在生成真实且多样化的异常。具体而言，AnomalyAgent配备五种工具：提示生成（PG）、图像生成（IG）、质量评估（QE）、知识检索（KR）和掩码生成（MG），实现闭环优化。为提升决策与自我反思能力，我们从真实异常图像构建结构化轨迹，并设计两阶段训练框架：先进行监督微调，再实施强化学习。该过程由三部分奖励机制驱动：（1）任务奖励：监督生成异常的质量与位置合理性；（2）反思奖励：训练模型优化异常合成提示的能力；（3）行为奖励：确保遵循预设轨迹。在MVTec-AD数据集上，AnomalyAgent在异常生成任务中取得IS/IC-L为2.10/0.33，使用ResNet34实现57.0%的分类准确率，采用简易UNet在图像/像素级别达到99.3%/74.2%的平均精度，超越所有零样本先进方法。代码与数据将公开提供。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the data scarcity in industrial anomaly detection and the limitations of single-step generation methods lacking complex reasoning, this paper introduces AnomalyAgent, an agentic framework for anomaly synthesis that leverages tool-augmented reinforcement learning. The method equips the agent with five specialized tools for prompt generation, image generation, quality evaluation, knowledge retrieval, and mask generation, enabling closed-loop iterative refinement; it is trained via a two-stage framework of supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, guided by a composite reward mechanism for task quality, prompt reflection, and behavioral adherence. Experimental results on the MVTec-AD dataset demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, achieving an IS/IC-L score of 2.10/0.33 for anomaly generation, 57.0% classification accuracy with ResNet34, and 99.3%/74.2% average precision at image/pixel level using a UNet, surpassing existing zero-shot methods.
针对工业异常检测中数据稀缺以及现有单步生成方法缺乏复杂推理能力的问题，本文提出了AnomalyAgent，一种基于工具增强强化学习的智能体化异常合成框架。该方法为智能体配备了提示生成、图像生成、质量评估、知识检索和掩码生成五种工具，实现闭环迭代优化，并通过监督微调与强化学习的两阶段训练框架进行训练，辅以任务质量、提示反思和行为遵从的复合奖励机制。在MVTec-AD数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在异常生成上取得了2.10/0.33的IS/IC-L分数，使用ResNet34实现了57.0%的分类准确率，并使用简单UNet在图像/像素级别达到了99.3%/74.2%的平均精度，超越了所有零样本先进方法。
Q-Probe: Scaling Image Quality Assessment to High Resolution via Context-Aware Agentic Probing
Authors: Xiang Li, Xueheng Li, Yu Wang, Xuanhua He, Zhangchi Hu, Weiwei Yu, Chengjun Xie
First: 2026-01-21T08:02:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T07:04:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has empowered Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) to achieve superior human preference alignment in Image Quality Assessment (IQA). However, existing RL-based IQA models typically rely on coarse-grained global views, failing to capture subtle local degradations in high-resolution scenarios. While emerging "Thinking with Images" paradigms enable multi-scale visual perception via zoom-in mechanisms, their direct adaptation to IQA induces spurious "cropping-implies-degradation" biases and misinterprets natural depth-of-field as artifacts. To address these challenges, we propose Q-Probe, the first agentic IQA framework designed to scale IQA to high resolution via context-aware probing. First, we construct Vista-Bench, a pioneering benchmark tailored for fine-grained local degradation analysis in high-resolution IQA settings. Furthermore, we propose a three-stage training paradigm that progressively aligns the model with human preferences, while simultaneously eliminating causal bias through a novel context-aware cropping strategy. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Q-Probe achieves state-of-the-art performance in high-resolution settings while maintaining superior efficacy across resolution scales.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Q-Probe：通过上下文感知智能探测实现高分辨率图像质量评估的规模化扩展
强化学习（RL）赋能多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在图像质量评估（IQA）中实现了更优的人类偏好对齐。然而，现有基于RL的IQA模型通常依赖粗粒度的全局视图，难以捕捉高分辨率场景中细微的局部退化。尽管新兴的“图像思维”范式通过放大机制实现了多尺度视觉感知，但其直接应用于IQA会引发虚假的“裁剪即退化”偏差，并将自然景深误解为伪影。为解决这些挑战，我们提出Q-Probe——首个通过上下文感知探测实现高分辨率IQA规模化扩展的智能框架。首先，我们构建了Vista-Bench，这是专为高分辨率IQA场景中细粒度局部退化分析设计的开创性基准。此外，我们提出一种三阶段训练范式，在逐步对齐模型与人类偏好的同时，通过新颖的上下文感知裁剪策略消除因果偏差。大量实验表明，Q-Probe在高分辨率场景中实现了最先进的性能，同时在多分辨率尺度上保持卓越效能。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limitations of existing Reinforcement Learning-based Image Quality Assessment (IQA) models, which rely on coarse global views and fail to capture subtle local degradations in high-resolution images, while also avoiding the biases introduced by direct adaptation of multi-scale 'Thinking with Images' paradigms. The method introduces Q-Probe, a novel agentic IQA framework that scales assessment to high resolution through context-aware probing, supported by a new benchmark, Vista-Bench, for fine-grained local degradation analysis and a three-stage training paradigm that aligns the model with human preferences and eliminates causal bias via a context-aware cropping strategy. The main experimental results show that Q-Probe achieves state-of-the-art performance in high-resolution IQA settings while maintaining superior efficacy across various resolution scales.

TreeAdv: Tree-Structured Advantage Redistribution for Group-Based RL
Authors: Lang Cao, Hui Ruan, Yongqian Li, Peng Chao, Wu Ning, Haonan Song, Renhong Chen, Yitong Li
First: 2026-01-07T08:42:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T06:21:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with group-based objectives, such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), is a common framework for aligning large language models on complex reasoning tasks. However, standard GRPO treats each rollout trajectory as an independent flat sequence and assigns a single sequence-level advantage to all tokens, which leads to sample inefficiency and a length bias toward verbose, redundant chains of thought without improving logical depth. We introduce TreeAdv (Tree-Structured Advantage Redistribution for Group-Based RL), which makes the tree structure of group rollouts explicit for both exploration and advantage assignment. Specifically, TreeAdv builds a group of trees (a forest) based on an entropy-driven sampling method where each tree branches at high-uncertainty decisions while sharing low-uncertainty tokens across rollouts. Then, TreeAdv aggregates token-level advantages for internal tree segments by redistributing the advantages of complete rollouts (all leaf nodes), and TreeAdv can easily apply to group-based objectives such as GRPO or GSPO. Across 10 math reasoning benchmarks, TreeAdv consistently outperforms GRPO and GSPO, while using substantially fewer generated tokens under identical supervision, data, and decoding budgets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TreeAdv：面向分组强化学习的树形优势重分配方法
基于分组目标的强化学习（如组相对策略优化GRPO）是对齐大语言模型处理复杂推理任务的常用框架。然而标准GRPO将每次轨迹展开视为独立的扁平序列，并为所有词元分配单一序列级优势值，这导致样本效率低下，且产生偏向冗长冗余思维链的长度偏差，却未提升逻辑深度。本文提出TreeAdv（面向分组强化学习的树形优势重分配方法），在探索与优势分配中显式构建分组展开的树形结构。具体而言，TreeAdv通过熵驱动采样方法构建树群（森林），每棵树在高不确定性决策点分叉，同时在展开轨迹间共享低不确定性词元。随后，TreeAdv通过重分配完整轨迹（所有叶节点）的优势值，聚合内部树段词元级优势，该方法可轻松适配GRPO、GSPO等分组目标。在10项数学推理基准测试中，TreeAdv在相同监督、数据和解码预算下，使用显著更少的生成词元，始终优于GRPO与GSPO。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the sample inefficiency and length bias in group-based reinforcement learning for aligning large language models on reasoning tasks, where standard methods like GRPO treat each rollout as a flat sequence and assign a single advantage to all tokens. The method, TreeAdv, introduces a tree-structured approach that explicitly models group rollouts as a forest, branching at high-uncertainty decisions while sharing low-uncertainty tokens across rollouts, and redistributes token-level advantages by aggregating advantages from complete rollouts. The main experimental results show that across 10 math reasoning benchmarks, TreeAdv consistently outperforms GRPO and GSPO while using substantially fewer generated tokens under identical supervision, data, and decoding budgets.
本研究的动机是解决基于群体的强化学习在大型语言模型推理任务对齐中的样本效率低下和长度偏差问题，因为标准方法如GRPO将每个轨迹视为独立平面序列并为所有令牌分配单一优势。所提出的TreeAdv方法采用树形结构，将群体轨迹显式建模为森林，在高不确定性决策处进行分支，同时在轨迹间共享低不确定性令牌，并通过聚合完整轨迹的优势来重新分配令牌级优势。主要实验结果表明，在10个数学推理基准测试中，TreeAdv在相同监督、数据和解码预算下，始终优于GRPO和GSPO，同时显著减少了生成的令牌数量。
QaRL: Rollout-Aligned Quantization-Aware RL for Fast and Stable Training under Training--Inference Mismatch
Authors: Hao Gu, Hao Wang, Jiacheng Liu, Lujun Li, Qiyuan Zhu, Bei Liu, Binxing Xu, Lei Wang, Xintong Yang, Sida Lin, Sirui Han, Yike Guo
First: 2026-04-09T06:11:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T06:11:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) reinforcement learning (RL) pipelines are often bottlenecked by rollout generation, making end-to-end training slow. Recent work mitigates this by running rollouts with quantization to accelerate decoding, which is the most expensive stage of the RL loop. However, these setups destabilize optimization by amplifying the training-inference gap: rollouts are operated at low precision, while learning updates are computed at full precision. To address this challenge, we propose QaRL (Rollout Alignment Quantization-Aware RL), which aligns training-side forward with the quantized rollout to minimize mismatch. We further identify a failure mode in quantized rollouts: long-form responses tend to produce repetitive, garbled tokens (error tokens). To mitigate these problems, we introduce TBPO (Trust-Band Policy Optimization), a sequence-level objective with dual clipping for negative samples, aimed at keeping updates within the trust region. On Qwen3-30B-A3B MoE for math problems, QaRL outperforms quantized-rollout training by +5.5 while improving stability and preserving low-bit throughput benefits.
中文标题/摘要
标题：QaRL：面向训练-推理失配的快速稳定训练——基于对齐量化的强化学习方法
大语言模型强化学习流程常受限于策略推演生成，导致端到端训练缓慢。近期研究通过量化加速解码来缓解此瓶颈，但量化推演与全精度学习更新间的精度差异会放大训练-推理差距，破坏优化稳定性。为此，我们提出QaRL方法，通过对齐训练前向过程与量化推演以最小化失配。同时，我们发现量化推演存在长文本生成重复乱码的失效模式，进而提出TBPO方法——采用双重截断的序列级目标函数，将更新约束在置信域内。在Qwen3-30B-A3B混合专家模型数学任务测试中，QaRL在保持低比特吞吐优势的同时，较量化推演训练提升5.5个性能点并显著增强稳定性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the slowdown in large language model reinforcement learning pipelines caused by rollout generation, which recent attempts to accelerate via quantization have destabilized by creating a mismatch between low-precision rollouts and full-precision learning updates. The method proposed, QaRL (Rollout-Aligned Quantization-Aware RL), aligns training-side forward passes with quantized rollouts to minimize this gap and introduces TBPO (Trust-Band Policy Optimization), a sequence-level objective with dual clipping to mitigate error tokens in long-form responses from quantized rollouts. Experimental results on Qwen3-30B-A3B MoE for math problems show that QaRL outperforms quantized-rollout training by +5.5 in performance while improving stability and maintaining the throughput benefits of low-bit quantization.
本研究的动机是解决大语言模型强化学习流程中因生成回放数据导致的训练瓶颈，近期通过量化加速回放的方法虽提升了速度，却因低精度回放与全精度学习更新之间的不匹配而破坏了优化稳定性。提出的方法QaRL（回放对齐的量化感知强化学习）通过将训练侧前向传播与量化回放对齐以减少这种不匹配，并引入TBPO（信任带策略优化），这是一种采用双重裁剪的序列级目标，旨在缓解量化回放中长文本响应产生的重复、乱码错误令牌问题。在Qwen3-30B-A3B MoE模型上的数学问题实验结果表明，QaRL相比量化回放训练性能提升+5.5，同时增强了稳定性并保留了低比特量化的吞吐优势。
SEARL: Joint Optimization of Policy and Tool Graph Memory for Self-Evolving Agents
Authors: Xinshun Feng, Xinhao Song, Lijun Li, Gongshen Liu, Jing Shao
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-09T04:38:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T04:38:47+00:00
Comments: ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) have demonstrated significant potential in single-turn reasoning tasks. With the paradigm shift toward self-evolving agentic learning, models are increasingly expected to learn from trajectories by synthesizing tools or accumulating explicit experiences. However, prevailing methods typically rely on large-scale LLMs or multi-agent frameworks, which hinder their deployment in resource-constrained environments. The inherent sparsity of outcome-based rewards also poses a substantial challenge, as agents typically receive feedback only upon completion of tasks. To address these limitations, we introduce a Tool-Memory based self-evolving agentic framework SEARL. Unlike approaches that directly utilize interaction experiences, our method constructs a structured experience memory that integrates planning with execution. This provides a novel state abstraction that facilitates generalization across analogous contexts, such as tool reuse. Consequently, agents extract explicit knowledge from historical data while leveraging inter-trajectory correlations to densify reward signals. We evaluate our framework on knowledge reasoning and mathematics tasks, demonstrating its effectiveness in achieving more practical and efficient learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SEARL：面向自进化智能体的策略与工具图记忆联合优化框架
近期基于可验证奖励的强化学习在单轮推理任务中展现出显著潜力。随着范式向自进化智能体学习转变，模型日益需要通过合成工具或积累显式经验从轨迹中学习。然而，主流方法通常依赖大规模语言模型或多智能体框架，限制了其在资源受限环境中的部署。基于结果的奖励本身具有稀疏性，因智能体通常仅在任务完成后获得反馈，这构成了重大挑战。为应对这些局限，我们提出了基于工具记忆的自进化智能体框架SEARL。与直接利用交互经验的方法不同，本方法构建了融合规划与执行的结构化经验记忆，提供了一种新颖的状态抽象机制，可促进跨相似场景（如工具复用）的泛化能力。由此，智能体既能从历史数据中提取显式知识，又能利用轨迹间关联性来稠密化奖励信号。我们在知识推理与数学任务上评估了该框架，验证了其在实现更实用、高效学习方面的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient self-evolving agents in resource-constrained settings and the challenge of sparse outcome-based rewards in tasks like tool synthesis, this paper introduces SEARL, a framework that jointly optimizes policy and a structured tool graph memory. The method constructs a memory integrating planning and execution to provide state abstraction, enabling generalization across similar contexts and densifying reward signals by leveraging inter-trajectory correlations. Experimental results on knowledge reasoning and mathematics tasks demonstrate that SEARL achieves more practical and efficient learning compared to large-scale LLM or multi-agent approaches.
本文的动机是解决资源受限环境下高效自进化智能体的需求，以及工具合成等任务中基于结果的奖励稀疏性挑战，提出了SEARL框架，联合优化策略和结构化工具图记忆。该方法构建了一个整合规划与执行的记忆系统，提供状态抽象以促进跨类似场景的泛化，并通过利用轨迹间相关性来稠密化奖励信号。在知识推理和数学任务上的实验结果表明，SEARL相比大规模语言模型或多智能体方法，实现了更实用和高效的学习。
Automotive Engineering-Centric Agentic AI Workflow Framework
Authors: Tong Duy Son, Zhihao Liu, Piero Brigida, Yerlan Akhmetov, Gurudevan Devarajan, Kai Liu, Ajinkya Bhave
First: 2026-04-09T04:22:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T04:22:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Engineering workflows such as design optimization, simulation-based diagnosis, control tuning, and model-based systems engineering (MBSE) are iterative, constraint-driven, and shaped by prior decisions. Yet many AI methods still treat these activities as isolated tasks rather than as parts of a broader workflow. This paper presents Agentic Engineering Intelligence (AEI), an industrial vision framework that models engineering workflows as constrained, history-aware sequential decision processes in which AI agents support engineer-supervised interventions over engineering toolchains. AEI links an offline phase for engineering data processing and workflow-memory construction with an online phase for workflow-state estimation, retrieval, and decision support. A control-theoretic interpretation is also possible, in which engineering objectives act as reference signals, agents act as workflow controllers, and toolchains provide feedback for intervention selection. Representative automotive use cases in suspension design, reinforcement learning tuning, multimodal engineering knowledge reuse, aerodynamic exploration, and MBSE show how diverse workflows can be expressed within a common formulation. Overall, the paper positions engineering AI as a problem of process-level intelligence and outlines a practical roadmap for future empirical validation in industrial settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：以汽车工程为中心的智能体化AI工作流框架
工程设计优化、基于仿真的诊断、控制调参和基于模型的系统工程（MBSE）等工作流具有迭代性、约束驱动性，并受先前决策影响。然而，许多AI方法仍将这些活动视为孤立任务，而非整体工作流的一部分。本文提出“智能体化工程智能（AEI）”——一种工业级愿景框架，将工程工作流建模为受约束且具备历史感知能力的序列决策过程，其中AI智能体支持工程师在工程工具链中进行监督式干预。AEI将用于工程数据处理与工作流记忆构建的离线阶段，与用于工作流状态估计、检索和决策支持的在线阶段相衔接。该框架亦可从控制理论角度解读：工程目标作为参考信号，智能体作为工作流控制器，工具链则为干预选择提供反馈。通过悬架设计、强化学习调参、多模态工程知识复用、空气动力学探索及MBSE等典型汽车行业用例，展示了如何用统一框架表达多样化工作流。本文最终将工程AI定位为流程级智能问题，并为工业场景下的未来实证验证规划了实践路线。

The paper is motivated by the need to treat engineering workflows as interconnected, iterative processes rather than isolated tasks, addressing limitations in current AI methods. It proposes the Agentic Engineering Intelligence (AEI) framework, which models workflows as constrained, history-aware sequential decision processes where AI agents support engineer-supervised interventions across toolchains, linking offline data processing and memory construction with online state estimation and decision support. Experimental results from automotive use cases, including suspension design, reinforcement learning tuning, and aerodynamic exploration, demonstrate that diverse workflows can be unified under this common formulation, positioning engineering AI as a process-level intelligence problem and outlining a roadmap for industrial validation.
本文的动机在于将工程工作流视为相互关联的迭代过程而非孤立任务，以解决当前人工智能方法的局限性。它提出了代理工程智能框架，将工作流建模为受约束、历史感知的顺序决策过程，其中人工智能代理支持工程师监督下对工具链的干预，结合离线数据处理与在线状态估计和决策支持。在汽车领域的代表性应用案例，如悬架设计、强化学习调优和气动探索，表明多样化的工程工作流可在该统一框架下表达，从而将工程人工智能定位为流程级智能问题，并为未来工业环境中的实证验证提供了实用路线图。
Mitigating Distribution Sharpening in Math RLVR via Distribution-Aligned Hint Synthesis and Backward Hint Annealing
Authors: Pei-Xi Xie, Che-Yu Lin, Cheng-Lin Yang
First: 2026-04-09T03:08:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T03:08:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) can improve low-$k$ reasoning accuracy while narrowing solution coverage on challenging math questions, and pass@1 gains do not necessarily translate into better large-$k$ performance. Existing hint-based approaches can make challenging questions trainable, but they leave two issues underexplored: teacher-student distribution mismatch and the need to reduce hint exposure to match no-hint evaluation. We address these issues through two components. Distribution-Aligned Hint Synthesis (DAHS) constructs verified teacher hints conditioned on student-style responses. Backward Hint Annealing (BHA) anneals hint exposure across difficulty buckets and uses per-question hint dropout to preserve no-hint updates throughout RL training. We evaluate the method in math RLVR under the DAPO training framework across AIME24, AIME25, and AIME26 using $\texttt{Qwen3-1.7B-Base}$ and $\texttt{Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct}$. On $\texttt{Qwen3-1.7B-Base}$, our method improves both pass@1 and pass@2048 relative to DAPO across the three AIME benchmarks. On $\texttt{Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct}$, the gains are concentrated in the large-$k$ regime. These results suggest that, in math RLVR, hint scaffolding is effective when it restores learnable updates on challenging questions early in training and is then gradually removed before no-hint evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过分布对齐提示合成与反向提示退火缓解数学RLVR中的分布锐化问题
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）在提升低k推理准确率的同时，会缩小对挑战性数学问题的求解覆盖范围，且pass@1的增益未必能转化为更好的大k性能。现有基于提示的方法虽能使难题可训练，但存在两个未充分探讨的问题：师生分布失配及需减少提示暴露以匹配无提示评估。我们通过两个组件解决这些问题：分布对齐提示合成（DAHS）基于学生风格响应构建可验证的教师提示；反向提示退火（BHA）在不同难度桶中退火提示暴露，并采用逐题提示丢弃以在RL训练全程保留无提示更新。我们在DAPO训练框架下，使用Qwen3-1.7B-Base和Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct模型，于AIME24、AIME25和AIME26三个数学RLVR基准上评估本方法。在Qwen3-1.7B-Base上，本方法较DAPO在三个AIME基准的pass@1和pass@2048指标均有提升；在Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct上，增益集中体现在大k区间。结果表明：在数学RLVR中，当提示脚手架能在训练早期为难题恢复可学习更新，并在无提示评估前逐步移除时，其效果最为显著。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses two underexplored issues in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for math reasoning: teacher-student distribution mismatch and the need to reduce hint exposure to match no-hint evaluation. The proposed method introduces Distribution-Aligned Hint Synthesis (DAHS), which constructs verified teacher hints conditioned on student-style responses, and Backward Hint Annealing (BHA), which anneals hint exposure across difficulty buckets and uses per-question hint dropout to preserve no-hint updates during training. Experimental results on AIME benchmarks using Qwen3-1.7B-Base and Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct models show that the method improves both pass@1 and pass@2048 for Qwen3-1.7B-Base across all benchmarks, while gains for Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct are concentrated in the large-k regime, indicating that effective hint scaffolding restores learnable updates early and is gradually removed before evaluation.
本文针对数学推理中可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）存在的两个未充分探索的问题：师生分布不匹配以及需要减少提示暴露以匹配无提示评估。提出的方法包括分布对齐提示合成（DAHS），它根据学生风格响应构建经过验证的教师提示；以及后向提示退火（BHA），它在不同难度桶中退火提示暴露，并使用逐题提示丢弃在训练中保持无提示更新。在AIME基准上使用Qwen3-1.7B-Base和Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct模型的实验结果表明，该方法在Qwen3-1.7B-Base上所有基准的pass@1和pass@2048均有提升，而Llama-3.2-1B-Instruct的增益主要集中在高k值区域，表明有效的提示支架能在训练早期恢复可学习更新，并在评估前逐步移除。
The Specification Trap: Why Static Value Alignment Alone Cannot Produce Robust Alignment
Authors: Austin Spizzirri
First: 2025-11-19T23:31:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T00:36:10+00:00
Comments: 24 pages. First in a six-paper program on AI alignment. Establishes a structural ceiling on closed specification (RLHF, Constitutional AI, IRL, assistance games); claims robust alignment under scaling/shift/autonomy requires open, process-coupled specification. v3: thesis sharpened to closure; tool/autonomous distinction added; empirical signatures for open specification; six-paper structure
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Static content-based AI value alignment cannot produce robust alignment under capability scaling, distributional shift, and increasing autonomy. This holds for any approach that treats alignment as optimizing toward a fixed formal value-object, whether reward function, utility function, constitutional principles, or learned preference representation. The limitation arises from three philosophical results: Hume's is-ought gap (behavioral data cannot entail normative conclusions), Berlin's value pluralism (human values are irreducibly plural and incommensurable), and the extended frame problem (any value encoding will misfit future contexts that advanced AI creates). RLHF, Constitutional AI, inverse reinforcement learning, and cooperative assistance games each instantiate this specification trap, and their failure modes are structural, not engineering limitations. Two proposed escape routes (meta-preferences and moral realism) relocate the trap rather than exit it. Continual updating represents a genuine direction of escape, not because current implementations succeed, but because the trap activates at the point of closure: the moment a specification ceases to update from the process it governs. Drawing on Fischer and Ravizza's compatibilist theory, behavioral compliance does not constitute alignment. There is a principled distinction between simulated value-following and genuine reasons-responsiveness, and closed specification methods cannot produce the latter. The specification trap establishes a ceiling on static approaches, not on specification itself, but this ceiling becomes safety-critical at the capability frontier. The alignment problem must be reframed from static value specification to open specification: systems whose value representations remain responsive to the processes they govern.
中文标题/摘要
标题：规范陷阱：为何静态价值对齐无法实现稳健对齐
基于静态内容的AI价值对齐方法在能力扩展、分布偏移和自主性增强的背景下无法实现稳健对齐。这一结论适用于所有将对齐视为向固定形式价值目标（如奖励函数、效用函数、宪法原则或习得偏好表征）优化的方法。其根本局限源于三个哲学原理：休谟的实然-应然鸿沟（行为数据无法推导规范结论）、伯林的价值多元论（人类价值具有不可简化的多元性与不可通约性），以及扩展框架问题（任何价值编码都将无法适应高级AI创造的未来情境）。RLHF、宪法AI、逆强化学习和协作辅助博弈均落入这一规范陷阱，其失效模式是结构性的而非工程局限。两种现有解决方案（元偏好与道德实在论）仅转移了陷阱而非真正逃脱。持续更新代表真正的突破方向——并非因当前实现已成功，而是因为陷阱在规范闭合时触发：即当规范停止从其所治理的过程中更新时。借鉴费舍尔与拉维扎的相容论理论，行为合规不等于对齐。模拟价值遵循与真正的理性响应存在原则性区别，而闭合规范方法无法产生后者。规范陷阱为静态方法设定了上限（非规范本身），该上限在能力边界处成为安全关键。对齐问题必须从静态价值规范重构为开放规范：即价值表征能持续响应其所治理过程的系统。
Summary / 总结
This paper argues that static, content-based AI value alignment methods, such as RLHF and Constitutional AI, are fundamentally limited and cannot achieve robust alignment as AI capabilities scale, environments shift, and autonomy increases. The authors' method is a philosophical critique, drawing on Hume's is-ought gap, Berlin's value pluralism, and the extended frame problem to demonstrate that any fixed value specification will inevitably misfit novel contexts, a structural flaw termed the 'specification trap'. The main result is that these approaches can only produce simulated value-following, not genuine reasons-responsiveness, establishing a safety-critical ceiling for static methods and necessitating a shift toward open, continually updated specification processes coupled with AI's operational context.
本文论证了基于静态内容的AI价值对齐方法（如RLHF和宪法AI）存在根本性局限，无法在能力扩展、分布偏移和自主性增强下实现稳健对齐。其方法是通过哲学批判，援引休谟的实然-应然鸿沟、柏林的多元价值论以及扩展框架问题，证明任何固定的价值规范在面对AI创造的新情境时都会失效，这一结构性缺陷被称为“规范陷阱”。核心结论是这些方法只能产生模拟的价值遵循，而非真正的理由响应性，从而为静态方法设立了安全临界上限，并指出必须转向与AI运行过程耦合的、持续更新的开放式规范框架。
Reinforcement Learning with LLM-Guided Action Spaces for Synthesizable Lead Optimization
Authors: Tao Li, Kaiyuan Hou, Tuan Vinh, Monika Raj, Zhichun Guo, Carl Yang
First: 2026-04-09T00:22:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T00:22:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Lead optimization in drug discovery requires improving therapeutic properties while ensuring that proposed molecular modifications correspond to feasible synthetic routes. Existing approaches either prioritize property scores without enforcing synthesizability, or rely on expensive enumeration over large reaction networks, while direct application of Large Language Models (LLMs) frequently produces chemically invalid structures. We introduce MolReAct, a framework that formulates lead optimization as a Markov Decision Process over a synthesis-constrained action space defined by validated reaction templates. A tool-augmented LLM agent serves as a dynamic reaction environment that invokes specialized chemical analysis tools to identify reactive sites and propose chemically grounded transformations from matched templates. A policy model trained via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) selects among these constrained actions to maximize long-term oracle reward across multi-step reaction trajectories. A SMILES-based caching mechanism further reduces end-to-end optimization time by approximately 43%. Across 13 property optimization tasks from the Therapeutic Data Commons and one structure-based docking task, MolReAct achieves an average Top-10 score of 0.563, outperforming the strongest synthesizable baseline by 10.4% in relative improvement, and attains the best sample efficiency on 10 of 14 tasks. Ablations confirm that both tool-augmented reaction proposals and trajectory-level policy optimization contribute complementary gains. By grounding every step in validated reaction templates, MolReAct produces molecules that are property-improved and each accompanied by an explicit synthetic pathway.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型引导动作空间的可合成先导化合物优化强化学习
药物发现中的先导化合物优化需要在提升治疗特性的同时，确保所提出的分子修饰对应可行的合成路径。现有方法要么优先考虑性质评分而忽略可合成性约束，要么依赖对大型反应网络的昂贵枚举，而直接应用大语言模型常产生化学无效结构。我们提出MolReAct框架，将先导化合物优化建模为在已验证反应模板定义的合成约束动作空间上的马尔可夫决策过程。一个工具增强的大语言模型智能体作为动态反应环境，调用专用化学分析工具识别反应位点，并根据匹配模板提出化学合理的转化方案。通过组相对策略优化训练的决策模型在这些约束动作中选择，以最大化多步反应轨迹的长期目标奖励。基于SMILES的缓存机制进一步将端到端优化时间减少约43%。在治疗数据公库的13项性质优化任务和一项基于结构的对接任务中，MolReAct的平均Top-10得分达0.563，相对改进幅度超越最强可合成基线10.4%，并在14项任务中的10项取得最佳样本效率。消融实验证实，工具增强的反应提议与轨迹级策略优化均带来互补性增益。通过将每个步骤锚定于已验证反应模板，MolReAct生成的分子既提升性质指标，又均附带明确的合成路径。

The method introduces MolReAct, a framework that formulates the task as a Markov Decision Process over a synthesis-constrained action space defined by validated reaction templates, employing a tool-augmented LLM agent as a dynamic reaction environment and training a policy model via Group Relative Policy Optimization to select constrained actions. The main experimental results show that across 13 property optimization tasks and one docking task, MolReAct achieves an average Top-10 score of 0.563, outperforming the strongest synthesizable baseline by 10.4% in relative improvement, attains the best sample efficiency on 10 of 14 tasks, and reduces optimization time by approximately 43% via a SMILES-based caching mechanism, with ablations confirming the contributions of both tool-augmented proposals and trajectory-level policy optimization.
本研究的动机是解决药物发现先导化合物优化中的挑战，即在改善治疗特性的同时确保分子修饰对应可行的合成路线，因为现有方法常忽略可合成性或计算成本高昂。方法上提出了MolReAct框架，将任务构建为在已验证反应模板定义的合成约束动作空间上的马尔可夫决策过程，采用工具增强的大语言模型代理作为动态反应环境，并通过组相对策略优化训练策略模型来选择约束动作。主要实验结果表明，在13个特性优化任务和1个对接任务中，MolReAct实现了0.563的平均Top-10分数，相对改进优于最强可合成基线10.4%，在14个任务中的10个上获得了最佳样本效率，并通过基于SMILES的缓存机制将端到端优化时间减少约43%，消融实验证实了工具增强的提议和轨迹级策略优化的互补增益。
An Imperfect Verifier is Good Enough: Learning with Noisy Rewards
Authors: Andreas Plesner, Francisco Guzmán, Anish Athalye
First: 2026-04-09T00:15:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-09T00:15:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become a prominent method for post-training Large Language Models (LLMs). However, verifiers are rarely error-free; even deterministic checks can be inaccurate, and the growing dependence on model-based judges exacerbates the issue. The extent to which RLVR is robust to such noise and the verifier accuracy required for effective training remain unresolved questions. We investigate these questions in the domains of code generation and scientific reasoning by introducing noise into RL training. Noise rates up to 15% yield peak validation accuracy within 2 percentage points of the clean baseline. These findings are consistent across controlled and model-based noise types, three model families (Qwen3, GLM4, Llama 3.1), and model sizes from 4B to 9B. Overall, the results indicate that imperfect verification does not constitute a fundamental barrier to RLVR. Furthermore, our findings suggest that practitioners should prioritize moderate accuracy with high precision over perfect verification.
中文标题/摘要
标题：不完美的验证器已足够：在含噪奖励下学习
带可验证奖励的强化学习已成为大型语言模型后训练的重要方法。然而，验证器很少完全无误；即使是确定性检查也可能不准确，而对基于模型的评判器的日益依赖加剧了这一问题。RLVR对此类噪声的鲁棒性程度，以及有效训练所需的验证器准确度，仍是未解之谜。我们通过在代码生成和科学推理领域向RL训练引入噪声来探究这些问题。噪声率高达15%时，验证准确率峰值与干净基线相差不超过2个百分点。这些发现在受控噪声与基于模型的噪声类型、三种模型系列以及4B至9B的模型规模中均保持一致。总体而言，结果表明不完美的验证并不构成RLVR的根本障碍。此外，我们的发现建议实践者应优先考虑中等准确率但高精度的验证，而非追求完美验证。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the robustness of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for training Large Language Models when the reward verifiers are noisy, motivated by the practical reality that verifiers are rarely perfect and the impact of such noise is poorly understood. The method involves systematically introducing controlled and model-based noise into the RL training process for code generation and scientific reasoning tasks. The main experimental results show that noise rates up to 15% cause only a minor drop in peak validation accuracy—within 2 percentage points of a clean baseline—across multiple model families and sizes, demonstrating that imperfect verification is not a fundamental barrier and suggesting practitioners should prioritize high-precision, moderately accurate verifiers over perfect ones.
本文研究了在奖励验证器存在噪声的情况下，使用可验证奖励的强化学习训练大语言模型的鲁棒性，其动机在于实践中验证器很少完美，且此类噪声的影响尚不明确。方法是在代码生成和科学推理任务的强化学习训练中，系统地引入受控和基于模型的噪声。主要实验结果表明，噪声率高达15%时，峰值验证准确率仅比干净基线下降2个百分点以内，这一结论在多种模型系列和规模上均保持一致，证明不完美的验证并非根本性障碍，并建议实践者应优先选择高精度、中等准确度的验证器，而非追求完美验证。
PRIME: Training Free Proactive Reasoning via Iterative Memory Evolution for User-Centric Agent
Authors: Prince Zizhuang Wang, Shuli Jiang
First: 2026-04-08T23:11:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T23:11:12+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The development of autonomous tool-use agents for complex, long-horizon tasks in collaboration with human users has become the frontier of agentic research. During multi-turn Human-AI interactions, the dynamic and uncertain nature of user demands poses a significant challenge; agents must not only invoke tools but also iteratively refine their understanding of user intent through effective communication. While recent advances in reinforcement learning offer a path to more capable tool-use agents, existing approaches require expensive training costs and struggle with turn-level credit assignment across extended interaction horizons. To this end, we introduce PRIME (Proactive Reasoning via Iterative Memory Evolution), a gradient-free learning framework that enables continuous agent evolvement through explicit experience accumulation rather than expensive parameter optimization. PRIME distills multi-turn interaction trajectories into structured, human-readable experiences organized across three semantic zones: successful strategies, failure patterns, and user preferences. These experiences evolve through meta-level operations and guide future agent behavior via retrieval-augmented generation. Our experiments across several diverse user-centric environments demonstrate that PRIME achieves competitive performance with gradient-based methods while offering cost-efficiency and interpretability. Together, PRIME presents a practical paradigm for building proactive, collaborative agents that learn from Human-AI interaction without the computational burden of gradient-based training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PRIME：面向用户中心智能体的免训练主动推理——基于迭代记忆演化的方法
开发能与人类用户协作完成复杂长周期任务的自主工具使用智能体，已成为智能体研究的前沿领域。在多轮人机交互过程中，用户需求的动态性和不确定性带来重大挑战：智能体不仅需调用工具，还需通过有效沟通迭代优化对用户意图的理解。尽管强化学习的最新进展为构建更强工具使用智能体提供了路径，但现有方法需要高昂训练成本，且在长交互周期中难以实现轮次级信用分配。为此，我们提出PRIME（基于迭代记忆演化的主动推理框架），这是一种无需梯度的学习框架，通过显式经验积累而非昂贵的参数优化实现智能体持续演进。PRIME将多轮交互轨迹提炼为结构化、人类可读的经验，并组织在三个语义区域：成功策略、失败模式和用户偏好。这些经验通过元级操作持续演化，并通过检索增强生成指导智能体未来行为。我们在多个用户中心环境中的实验表明，PRIME在保持成本效益和可解释性的同时，取得了与基于梯度方法相竞争的性能。PRIME共同构建了一种实用范式，使主动协作型智能体能够从人机交互中学习，且无需承担基于梯度训练的计算负担。

Motivated by the challenge of building autonomous tool-use agents that can adapt to dynamic user demands during multi-turn interactions without costly training, this paper introduces PRIME, a gradient-free learning framework. The method enables agents to evolve by distilling interaction trajectories into structured, human-readable memories of successes, failures, and user preferences, which are iteratively updated via meta-level operations and retrieved to guide future behavior. Experimental results across diverse user-centric environments show that PRIME achieves competitive performance with gradient-based methods while offering greater cost-efficiency and interpretability.
本文旨在解决多轮人机交互中，自主工具使用智能体难以适应动态用户需求且训练成本高昂的问题，提出了PRIME这一无需梯度训练的学习框架。该方法通过将交互轨迹提炼为结构化、可读的记忆（包括成功策略、失败模式和用户偏好），并利用元级操作迭代更新记忆，再通过检索增强生成来指导智能体行为。在多个以用户为中心的环境中的实验表明，PRIME实现了与基于梯度的方法相竞争的性能，同时具有更高的成本效益和可解释性。
Auto-Configured Networks for Multi-Scale Multi-Output Time-Series Forecasting
Authors: Yumeng Zha, Shengxiang Yang, Xianpeng Wang
First: 2026-04-08T21:28:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T21:28:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Industrial forecasting often involves multi-source asynchronous signals and multi-output targets, while deployment requires explicit trade-offs between prediction error and model complexity. Current practices typically fix alignment strategies or network designs, making it difficult to systematically co-design preprocessing, architecture, and hyperparameters in budget-limited training-based evaluations. To address this issue, we propose an auto-configuration framework that outputs a deployable Pareto set of forecasting models balancing error and complexity. At the model level, a Multi-Scale Bi-Branch Convolutional Neural Network (MS--BCNN) is developed, where short- and long-kernel branches capture local fluctuations and long-term trends, respectively, for multi-output regression. At the search level, we unify alignment operators, architectural choices, and training hyperparameters into a hierarchical-conditional mixed configuration space, and apply Player-based Hybrid Multi-Objective Evolutionary Algorithm (PHMOEA) to approximate the error--complexity Pareto frontier within a limited computational budget. Experiments on hierarchical synthetic benchmarks and a real-world sintering dataset demonstrate that our framework outperforms competitive baselines under the same budget and offers flexible deployment choices.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向多尺度多输出时间序列预测的自动配置网络
工业预测常涉及多源异步信号与多输出目标，而部署需在预测误差与模型复杂度间进行显式权衡。现有方法通常固定对齐策略或网络设计，难以在预算受限的训练评估中系统化协同设计预处理、架构与超参数。为此，我们提出一种自动配置框架，可输出平衡误差与复杂度的可部署预测模型帕累托集。在模型层面，开发了多尺度双分支卷积神经网络（MS-BCNN），其短核与长核分支分别捕捉局部波动与长期趋势，实现多输出回归。在搜索层面，将对齐算子、架构选择与训练超参数统一为分层条件混合配置空间，并应用基于参与者的混合多目标进化算法（PHMOEA），在有限计算预算内逼近误差-复杂度帕累托前沿。在分层合成基准与真实烧结数据集上的实验表明，本框架在同等预算下优于竞争基线，并提供灵活的部署选择。

The challenge of hidden gifts in multi-agent reinforcement learning
Authors: Dane Malenfant, Blake A. Richards
First: 2025-05-26T23:28:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T20:58:11+00:00
Comments: Increased analysis of LOLA baselines and moved to main section. Cleaned up proof and fixed error where gradient symbol was left in front of the log(policy). Self correction becomes more intuitive
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sometimes we benefit from actions that others have taken even when we are unaware that they took those actions. For example, if your neighbor chooses not to take a parking spot in front of your house when you are not there, you can benefit, even without being aware that they took this action. These ``hidden gifts'' represent an interesting challenge for multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), since assigning credit when the beneficial actions of others are hidden is non-trivial. Here, we study the impact of hidden gifts with a simple MARL task. In this task, agents in a grid-world environment have individual doors to unlock in order to obtain individual rewards. As well, if all the agents unlock their door the group receives a larger collective reward. However, there is only one key for all of the doors, such that the collective reward can only be obtained when the agents drop the key for others after they use it. Notably, there is nothing to indicate to an agent that the other agents have dropped the key, thus this act for others is a ``hidden gift''. We show that several different state-of-the-art MARL algorithms, including MARL specific architectures, fail to learn how to obtain the collective reward in this simple task. Interestingly, we find that decentralized actor-critic policy gradient agents can succeed when we provide them with information about their own action history, but MARL agents still cannot solve the task with action history. Finally, we derive a correction term for policy gradient agents, inspired by learning aware approaches, which reduces the variance in learning and helps them to converge to collective success more reliably. These results show that credit assignment in multi-agent settings can be particularly challenging in the presence of ``hidden gifts'', and demonstrate that self learning-awareness in decentralized agents can benefit these settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体强化学习中隐性馈赠的挑战
我们有时会从他人采取的行动中获益，即使并未察觉这些行动的存在。例如邻居在你不在时选择不占用你家门前的停车位，你虽不知情却能受益。这类“隐性馈赠”对多智能体强化学习提出了独特挑战，因为在他人有益行动被隐藏的情况下进行信用分配并非易事。本研究通过一个简单的MARL任务探讨隐性馈赠的影响：网格世界中的智能体需各自解锁门锁获取个体奖励，若所有智能体均完成解锁，团队将获得更高集体奖励。但所有门锁共享唯一钥匙，智能体必须在用钥匙后留给他人才能实现集体奖励。关键的是，系统不会提示钥匙已被其他智能体留下，因此该行为构成“隐性馈赠”。实验表明，包括专用架构在内的多种前沿MARL算法均无法在此简单任务中学会获取集体奖励。有趣的是，分散式行动者-评论家策略梯度智能体在获得自身行动历史信息后能够成功，但MARL智能体即使有行动历史仍无法解决任务。最后，受学习感知方法启发，我们推导出策略梯度智能体的修正项，可降低学习方差并帮助其更可靠地达成集体成功。这些结果表明，存在“隐性馈赠”时多智能体场景的信用分配尤为困难，而分散式智能体的自我学习感知能力可改善此类场景。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates the challenge of 'hidden gifts' in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), where agents benefit from others' actions without direct observation, complicating credit assignment. Using a grid-world task where agents must share a single key to unlock individual doors and achieve a collective reward, the study tests state-of-the-art MARL algorithms and finds they fail to learn cooperative behavior due to the hidden nature of key-dropping actions. Experimental results show that decentralized actor-critic agents can succeed when provided with their own action history, and a derived policy gradient correction term reduces learning variance, enabling more reliable convergence to collective success, highlighting the benefits of self-learning awareness in such settings.
本文研究了多智能体强化学习（MARL）中“隐藏馈赠”的挑战，即智能体在无法直接观察的情况下受益于其他智能体的行为，这使信用分配变得复杂。通过一个网格世界任务，其中智能体必须共享一把钥匙来解锁各自的门以获得集体奖励，研究测试了多种先进的MARL算法，发现它们因钥匙丢弃行为的隐蔽性而无法学习合作行为。实验结果表明，分散式行动者-评论家智能体在获得自身行动历史信息时可以成功，并且推导出的策略梯度修正项降低了学习方差，使其更可靠地收敛到集体成功，凸显了在此类设置中自我学习意识的好处。
SALSA-RL: Stability Analysis in the Latent Space of Actions for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xuyang Li, Romit Maulik
First: 2025-02-21T15:09:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T20:41:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern deep reinforcement learning (DRL) methods have made significant advances in handling continuous action spaces. However, real-world control systems, especially those requiring precise and reliable performance, often demand interpretability in the sense of a-priori assessments of agent behavior to identify safe or failure-prone interactions with environments. To address this limitation, this work proposes SALSA-RL (Stability Analysis in the Latent Space of Actions), a novel RL framework that models control actions as dynamic, time-dependent variables evolving within a latent space. By employing a pre-trained encoder-decoder and a state-dependent linear system, this approach enables interpretability through local stability analysis, where instantaneous growth in action-norms can be predicted before their execution. It is demonstrated that SALSA-RL can be deployed in a non-invasive manner for assessing the local stability of actions from pretrained RL agents without compromising on performance across diverse benchmark environments. By enabling a more interpretable analysis of action generation, SALSA-RL provides a powerful tool for advancing the design, analysis, and theoretical understanding of RL systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SALSA-RL：强化学习中动作潜在空间的稳定性分析
现代深度强化学习方法在处理连续动作空间方面取得了显著进展。然而，现实世界的控制系统，特别是那些需要精确可靠性能的系统，通常要求对智能体行为进行先验评估的可解释性，以识别与环境交互中的安全或易故障模式。为应对这一局限，本研究提出SALSA-RL（动作潜在空间稳定性分析）——一种将控制动作建模为在潜在空间中演化的动态时变变量的新型强化学习框架。通过采用预训练的编码器-解码器和状态依赖线性系统，该方法能够通过局部稳定性分析实现可解释性，在执行前即可预测动作范数的瞬时增长。实验证明，SALSA-RL能以非侵入式方式部署，用于评估预训练强化学习智能体动作的局部稳定性，且在不同基准环境中均保持性能无损。通过实现对动作生成过程更可解释的分析，SALSA-RL为推进强化学习系统的设计、分析和理论理解提供了有力工具。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the lack of interpretability and a-priori safety assessment in deep reinforcement learning (DRL) for real-world control systems, which require reliable performance. The method introduces SALSA-RL, a novel framework that models actions as dynamic variables in a latent space using a pre-trained encoder-decoder and a state-dependent linear system, enabling interpretability through local stability analysis to predict action-norm growth before execution. The main experimental results demonstrate that SALSA-RL can be applied non-invasively to pretrained RL agents, assessing action stability without compromising performance across diverse benchmark environments, thus providing a tool for advancing RL system design and analysis.
本研究的动机是解决深度强化学习在现实世界控制系统中缺乏可解释性和先验安全性评估的问题，这些系统需要可靠的性能。方法上提出了SALSA-RL这一新颖框架，通过预训练的编码器-解码器和状态依赖的线性系统，将动作建模为潜在空间中的动态变量，从而通过局部稳定性分析实现可解释性，以在执行前预测动作范数的增长。主要实验结果表明，SALSA-RL可以非侵入式地应用于预训练的强化学习智能体，在不影响多样基准环境性能的情况下评估动作稳定性，为推进强化学习系统的设计和分析提供了有力工具。
Dual-Loop Control in DCVerse: Advancing Reliable Deployment of AI in Data Centers via Digital Twins
Authors: Qingang Zhang, Yuejun Yan, Guangyu Wu, Siew-Chien Wong, Jimin Jia, Zhaoyang Wang, Yonggang Wen
First: 2026-04-08T20:01:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T20:01:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The growing scale and complexity of modern data centers present major challenges in balancing energy efficiency with outage risk. Although Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) shows strong potential for intelligent control, its deployment in mission-critical systems is limited by data scarcity and the lack of real-time pre-evaluation mechanisms. This paper introduces the Dual-Loop Control Framework (DLCF), a digital twin-based architecture designed to overcome these challenges. The framework comprises three core entities: the physical system, a digital twin, and a policy reservoir of diverse DRL agents. These components interact through a dual-loop mechanism involving real-time data acquisition, data assimilation, DRL policy training, pre-evaluation, and expert verification. Theoretical analysis shows how DLCF can improve sample efficiency, generalization, safety, and optimality. Leveraging DLCF, we implemented the DCVerse platform and validated it through case studies on a real-world data center cooling system. The evaluation shows that our approach achieves up to 4.09% energy savings over conventional control strategies without violating SLA requirements. Additionally, the framework improves policy interpretability and supports more trustworthy DRL deployment. This work provides a foundation for reliable AI-based control in data centers and points toward future extensions for holistic, system-wide optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DCVerse中的双环控制：通过数字孪生推进数据中心AI可靠部署
现代数据中心规模与复杂性的日益增长，在平衡能源效率与宕机风险方面带来了重大挑战。尽管深度强化学习（DRL）在智能控制方面展现出强大潜力，但其在关键任务系统中的部署受限于数据稀缺和缺乏实时预评估机制。本文提出了双环控制框架（DLCF），这是一种基于数字孪生的架构，旨在克服这些挑战。该框架包含三个核心实体：物理系统、数字孪生和多样化DRL智能体的策略库。这些组件通过双环机制进行交互，包括实时数据采集、数据同化、DRL策略训练、预评估和专家验证。理论分析表明DLCF如何提升样本效率、泛化性、安全性和最优性。利用DLCF，我们实现了DCVerse平台，并通过真实数据中心冷却系统的案例研究进行了验证。评估显示，在不违反SLA要求的前提下，该方法相比传统控制策略最高可节能4.09%。此外，该框架提升了策略可解释性，支持更可信的DRL部署。这项工作为数据中心基于AI的可靠控制奠定了基础，并为未来实现系统级整体优化指明了方向。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenges of balancing energy efficiency and outage risk in complex data centers, and the limitations of Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) due to data scarcity and lack of safe pre-evaluation, this paper proposes the Dual-Loop Control Framework (DLCF). The method employs a digital twin-based architecture with a physical system, a digital twin, and a DRL policy reservoir, interacting through a dual-loop process for real-time data assimilation, policy training, pre-evaluation, and expert verification. Experimental validation on a real data center cooling system via the DCVerse platform demonstrates that the approach achieves up to 4.09% energy savings compared to conventional strategies while maintaining service-level agreements, and also enhances policy interpretability for more trustworthy DRL deployment.
本文的动机源于现代数据中心规模与复杂性增长所带来的能源效率与宕机风险平衡的挑战，以及深度强化学习（DRL）因数据稀缺和缺乏实时预评估机制而在关键任务系统中部署受限的问题。该方法提出了双环控制框架（DLCF），这是一种基于数字孪生的架构，包含物理系统、数字孪生和多样DRL策略库三个核心实体，通过实时数据采集、同化、策略训练、预评估和专家验证的双环机制进行交互。在真实数据中心冷却系统上的案例研究表明，通过DCVerse平台实现的该框架相比传统控制策略最高可节能4.09%且不违反服务等级协议，同时提升了策略可解释性，支持更可信的DRL部署。
RL-ASL: A Dynamic Listening Optimization for TSCH Networks Using Reinforcement Learning
Authors: F. Fernando Jurado-Lasso, J. F. Jurado
First: 2026-04-08T19:17:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T19:17:26+00:00
Comments: 14 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Time Slotted Channel Hopping (TSCH) is a widely adopted Media Access Control (MAC) protocol within the IEEE 802.15.4e standard, designed to provide reliable and energy-efficient communication in Industrial Internet of Things (IIoT) networks. However, state-of-the-art TSCH schedulers rely on static slot allocations, resulting in idle listening and unnecessary power consumption under dynamic traffic conditions. This paper introduces RL-ASL, a reinforcement learning-driven adaptive listening framework that dynamically decides whether to activate or skip a scheduled listening slot based on real-time network conditions. By integrating learning-based slot skipping with standard TSCH scheduling, RL-ASL reduces idle listening while preserving synchronization and delivery reliability. Experimental results on the FIT IoT-LAB testbed and Cooja network simulator show that RL-ASL achieves up to 46% lower power consumption than baseline scheduling protocols, while maintaining near-perfect reliability and reducing average latency by up to 96% compared to PRIL-M. Its link-based variant, RL-ASL-LB, further improves delay performance under high contention with similar energy efficiency. Importantly, RL-ASL performs inference on constrained motes with negligible overhead, as model training is fully performed offline. Overall, RL-ASL provides a practical, scalable, and energy-aware scheduling mechanism for next-generation low-power IIoT networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RL-ASL：基于强化学习的TSCH网络动态侦听优化机制
时隙信道跳变（TSCH）是IEEE 802.15.4e标准中广泛采用的媒体访问控制（MAC）协议，旨在为工业物联网（IIoT）网络提供可靠且高能效的通信。然而，现有先进TSCH调度器依赖静态时隙分配，在动态流量条件下会导致空闲侦听和不必要的功耗。本文提出RL-ASL——一种基于强化学习的自适应侦听框架，可根据实时网络状态动态决定激活或跳过预定的侦听时隙。通过将基于学习的时隙跳过机制与标准TSCH调度相结合，RL-ASL在保持同步和传输可靠性的同时减少了空闲侦听。在FIT IoT-LAB实验平台和Cooja网络模拟器上的实验结果表明：相较于基准调度协议，RL-ASL可降低高达46%的功耗；与PRIL-M相比，在维持近乎完美可靠性的同时将平均延迟降低达96%。其基于链路的变体RL-ASL-LB在高竞争场景下以相近的能效进一步提升了延迟性能。值得注意的是，由于模型训练完全离线进行，RL-ASL在受限节点上的推理开销可忽略不计。总体而言，RL-ASL为新一代低功耗IIoT网络提供了一种实用、可扩展且具备能量感知的调度机制。

ReflectRM: Boosting Generative Reward Models via Self-Reflection within a Unified Judgment Framework
Authors: Kai Qin, Liangxin Liu, Yu Liang, Longzheng Wang, Yan Wang, Yueyang Zhang, Long Xia, Zhiyuan Sun, Houde Liu, Daiting Shi
First: 2026-04-08T18:46:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T18:46:12+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward Models (RMs) are critical components in the Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) pipeline, directly determining the alignment quality of Large Language Models (LLMs). Recently, Generative Reward Models (GRMs) have emerged as a superior paradigm, offering higher interpretability and stronger generalization than traditional scalar RMs. However, existing methods for GRMs focus primarily on outcome-level supervision, neglecting analytical process quality, which constrains their potential. To address this, we propose ReflectRM, a novel GRM that leverages self-reflection to assess analytical quality and enhance preference modeling. ReflectRM is trained under a unified generative framework for joint modeling of response preference and analysis preference. During inference, we use its self-reflection capability to identify the most reliable analysis, from which the final preference prediction is derived. Experiments across four benchmarks show that ReflectRM consistently improves performance, achieving an average accuracy gain of +3.7 on Qwen3-4B. Further experiments confirm that response preference and analysis preference are mutually reinforcing. Notably, ReflectRM substantially mitigates positional bias, yielding +10.2 improvement compared with leading GRMs and establishing itself as a more stable evaluator.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReflectRM：基于统一评判框架的自反思增强生成式奖励模型

CLEAR: Context Augmentation from Contrastive Learning of Experience via Agentic Reflection
Authors: Linbo Liu, Guande Wu, Han Ding, Yawei Wang, Qiang Zhou, Yuzhe Lu, Zhichao Xu, Huan Song, Panpan Xu, Lin Lee Cheong
First: 2026-04-08T18:26:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T18:26:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large language model agents rely on effective model context to obtain task-relevant information for decision-making. Many existing context engineering approaches primarily rely on the context generated from the past experience and retrieval mechanisms that reuse these context. However, retrieved context from past tasks must be adapted by the execution agent to fit new situations, placing additional reasoning burden on the underlying LLM. To address this limitation, we propose a generative context augmentation framework using Contrastive Learning of Experience via Agentic Reflection (CLEAR). CLEAR first employs a reflection agent to perform contrastive analysis over past execution trajectories and summarize useful context for each observed task. These summaries are then used as supervised fine-tuning data to train a context augmentation model (CAM). Then we further optimize CAM using reinforcement learning, where the reward signal is obtained by running the task execution agent. By learning to generate task-specific knowledge rather than retrieve knowledge from the past, CAM produces context that is better tailored to the current task. We conduct comprehensive evaluations on the AppWorld and WebShop benchmarks. Experimental results show that CLEAR consistently outperforms strong baselines. It improves task completion rate from 72.62% to 81.15% on AppWorld test set and averaged reward from 0.68 to 0.74 on a subset of WebShop, compared with baseline agent. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/awslabs/CLEAR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CLEAR：基于智能体反思的对比经验学习上下文增强框架
大语言模型智能体依赖有效的模型上下文获取任务相关信息以进行决策。现有上下文工程方法主要依赖过往经验生成的上下文及复用这些上下文的检索机制，但过往任务的检索上下文需由执行智能体适配新情境，这增加了底层大语言模型的推理负担。为突破此限制，我们提出一种基于智能体反思的对比经验学习（CLEAR）生成式上下文增强框架。CLEAR首先利用反思智能体对过往执行轨迹进行对比分析，并为每个观测任务总结有效上下文；随后将这些摘要作为监督微调数据训练上下文增强模型（CAM）；进而通过强化学习进一步优化CAM，其奖励信号通过运行任务执行智能体获得。通过学习生成任务特定知识而非检索过往知识，CAM生成的上下文能更精准适配当前任务。我们在AppWorld和WebShop基准测试中进行了全面评估，实验结果表明CLEAR持续优于强基线模型：在AppWorld测试集上将任务完成率从72.62%提升至81.15%，在WebShop子集上将平均奖励从0.68提升至0.74。代码已开源：https://github.com/awslabs/CLEAR。

The proposed method, CLEAR, introduces a generative context augmentation framework that first uses a reflection agent to perform contrastive analysis on past execution trajectories and summarize useful context, which then serves as supervised fine-tuning data to train a context augmentation model (CAM), further optimized via reinforcement learning with rewards from the execution agent. Active Reward Machine Inference From Raw State Trajectories
Authors: Mohamad Louai Shehab, Antoine Aspeel, Necmiye Ozay
First: 2026-04-08T18:19:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T18:19:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward machines are automaton-like structures that capture the memory required to accomplish a multi-stage task. When combined with reinforcement learning or optimal control methods, they can be used to synthesize robot policies to achieve such tasks. However, specifying a reward machine by hand, including a labeling function capturing high-level features that the decisions are based on, can be a daunting task. This paper deals with the problem of learning reward machines directly from raw state and policy information. As opposed to existing works, we assume no access to observations of rewards, labels, or machine nodes, and show what trajectory data is sufficient for learning the reward machine in this information-scarce regime. We then extend the result to an active learning setting where we incrementally query trajectory extensions to improve data (and indirectly computational) efficiency. Results are demonstrated with several grid world examples.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于原始状态轨迹的主动奖励机推断
奖励机是一种类似自动机的结构，用于捕获完成多阶段任务所需的内存。结合强化学习或最优控制方法，它们可用于合成机器人策略以实现此类任务。然而，手动指定奖励机（包括捕获决策所依赖高层特征的标记函数）可能是一项艰巨的任务。本文研究直接从原始状态和策略信息中学习奖励机的问题。与现有工作不同，我们假设无法访问奖励、标签或机器节点的观测，并展示了在这种信息稀缺情况下，何种轨迹数据足以学习奖励机。随后，我们将结果扩展到主动学习场景，通过增量查询轨迹扩展来提升数据（及间接计算）效率。研究结果通过多个网格世界示例进行了验证。
