Regret-Aware Policy Optimization: Environment-Level Memory for Replay Suppression under Delayed Harm
Authors: Prakul Sunil Hiremath
First: 2026-04-08T17:45:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T17:45:45+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 3 figures. Includes theoretical analysis and experiments on graph diffusion environments
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety in reinforcement learning (RL) is typically enforced through objective shaping while keeping environment dynamics stationary with respect to observable state-action pairs. Under delayed harm, this can lead to replay: after a washout period, reintroducing the same stimulus under matched observable conditions reproduces a similar harmful cascade. We introduce the Replay Suppression Diagnostic (RSD), a controlled exposure-decay-replay protocol that isolates this failure mode under frozen-policy evaluation. We show that, under stationary observable transition kernels, replay cannot be structurally suppressed without inducing a persistent shift in replay-time action distributions. Motivated by platform-mediated systems, we propose Regret-Aware Policy Optimization (RAPO), which augments the environment with persistent harm-trace and scar fields and applies a bounded, mass-preserving transition reweighting to reduce reachability of historically harmful regions. On graph diffusion tasks (50-1000 nodes), RAPO suppresses replay, reducing re-amplification gain (RAG) from 0.98 to 0.33 on 250-node graphs while retaining 82\% of task return. Disabling transition deformation only during replay restores re-amplification (RAG 0.91), isolating environment-level deformation as the causal mechanism.
中文标题/摘要
标题：遗憾感知策略优化：面向延迟危害下重放抑制的环境级记忆机制
强化学习（RL）中的安全性通常通过目标函数重塑来保障，同时保持环境动态在可观测状态-动作对层面的平稳性。在延迟危害场景下，这可能导致重放现象：经过一段消退期后，在相同可观测条件下重新引入相同刺激会引发类似的危害级联。 我们提出了重放抑制诊断（RSD），这是一种受控的暴露-衰减-重放协议，可在冻结策略评估下隔离此类失效模式。研究表明，在平稳可观测转移核条件下，若不引发重放时刻动作分布的持续偏移，就无法从结构上抑制重放。 受平台中介系统启发，我们提出遗憾感知策略优化（RAPO），通过引入持久性危害轨迹与疤痕场来增强环境表征，并应用有界的质量守恒转移重加权方法，以降低历史危害区域的可达性。 在图扩散任务（50-1000节点）中，RAPO有效抑制重放，在250节点图上将重放放大增益（RAG）从0.98降至0.33，同时保留82%的任务回报。仅在重放期间禁用转移形变会导致重放恢复（RAG 0.91），这证实了环境级形变是因果机制。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the safety issue in reinforcement learning where delayed harmful effects can resurface after a washout period under stationary observable dynamics, a phenomenon termed 'replay'. To tackle this, the authors introduce the Replay Suppression Diagnostic (RSD) to isolate the failure mode and propose Regret-Aware Policy Optimization (RAPO), which augments the environment with persistent harm-trace fields and applies bounded transition reweighting to reduce reachability of harmful regions. Experimental results on graph diffusion tasks with 50-1000 nodes show that RAPO effectively suppresses replay, reducing re-amplification gain from 0.98 to 0.33 on 250-node graphs while maintaining 82% of task return, with ablation studies confirming environment-level deformation as the causal mechanism.
本文针对强化学习中的安全问题，即在可观测动态平稳条件下，延迟的有害效应可能在消退期后重现，这种现象称为“重放”。为解决此问题，作者提出了重放抑制诊断（RSD）来隔离该故障模式，并设计了后悔感知策略优化（RAPO），通过引入持久的伤害痕迹场和应用有界的转移重加权来减少有害区域的可达性。在50-1000个节点的图扩散任务上的实验结果表明，RAPO有效抑制了重放，在250节点图上将重放放大增益从0.98降至0.33，同时保留了82%的任务回报，消融研究证实了环境级变形是因果机制。
Replacing Tunable Parameters in Weather and Climate Models with State-Dependent Functions using Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Pritthijit Nath, Sebastian Schemm, Henry Moss, Peter Haynes, Emily Shuckburgh, Mark J. Webb
First: 2026-01-07T11:19:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T17:27:09+00:00
Comments: 77 pages, 24 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Weather and climate models rely on parametrisations to represent unresolved sub-grid processes. Traditional schemes rely on fixed coefficients that are weakly constrained and tuned offline, contributing to persistent biases that limit their ability to adapt to underlying physics. This study presents a framework that learns components of parametrisation schemes online as a function of the evolving model state using reinforcement learning (RL) and evaluates RL-driven parameter updates across idealised testbeds spanning a simple climate bias correction (SCBC), a radiative-convective equilibrium (RCE), and a zonal mean energy balance model (EBM) with single-agent and federated multi-agent settings. Across nine RL algorithms, Truncated Quantile Critics (TQC), Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG), and Twin Delayed DDPG (TD3) achieved the highest skill and stable convergence, with performance assessed against a static baseline using area-weighted RMSE, temperature and pressure-level diagnostics. For the EBM, single-agent RL outperformed static parameter tuning with the strongest gains in tropical and mid-latitude bands, while federated RL on multi-agent setups enabled specialised control and faster convergence, with a six-agent DDPG configuration using frequent aggregation yielding the lowest area-weighted RMSE across the tropics and mid-latitudes. The learnt corrections were also physically meaningful as agents modulated EBM radiative parameters to reduce meridional biases, adjusted RCE lapse rates to match vertical temperature errors, and stabilised heating increments to limit drift. Overall, results show that RL can learn skilful state-dependent parametrisation components in idealised settings, offering a scalable pathway for online learning within numerical models and a starting point for evaluation in weather and climate models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用强化学习将天气与气候模型中的可调参数替换为状态依赖函数
天气与气候模型依赖参数化方案表征未解析的次网格过程。传统方案采用离线弱约束和调优的固定系数，导致持续偏差并限制其适应底层物理过程的能力。本研究提出一种框架，利用强化学习在线学习参数化方案的组件作为模型动态状态的函数，并在理想化测试平台评估强化学习驱动的参数更新，涵盖简单气候偏差修正、辐射对流平衡模型及纬向平均能量平衡模型，采用单智能体与联邦多智能体设置。在九种强化学习算法中，截断分位数评论家、深度确定性策略梯度及双延迟深度确定性策略梯度展现出最高的技能与稳定收敛性，性能通过面积加权均方根误差、温度和气压层诊断指标与静态基线对比评估。在能量平衡模型中，单智能体强化学习优于静态参数调优，在热带和中纬度带提升最显著；而多智能体联邦强化学习实现专业化控制和更快收敛，采用频繁聚合的六智能体深度确定性策略梯度配置在热带和中纬度带获得最低面积加权均方根误差。习得的修正具有物理意义：智能体通过调节能量平衡模型辐射参数减少经向偏差，调整辐射对流平衡模型递减率以匹配垂直温度误差，并稳定加热增量以限制漂移。总体表明，强化学习可在理想化场景中学习有效的状态依赖参数化组件，为数值模型在线学习提供可扩展路径，并为天气和气候模型评估建立起点。
Summary / 总结
This study addresses the persistent biases in weather and climate models caused by traditional fixed-parameter schemes by introducing a reinforcement learning (RL) framework to learn state-dependent parametrisation components online. The method evaluates nine RL algorithms across three idealised testbeds—a simple climate bias correction, a radiative-convective equilibrium model, and a zonal mean energy balance model—using both single-agent and federated multi-agent settings. Experimental results show that algorithms like Truncated Quantile Critics, Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient, and Twin Delayed DDPG achieved the highest skill and stable convergence, with single-agent RL outperforming static tuning in reducing errors, particularly in tropical and mid-latitude bands, while federated multi-agent setups enabled specialised control and faster convergence, yielding physically meaningful corrections that reduced biases in radiative parameters, lapse rates, and heating increments.
本研究针对天气和气候模型中传统固定参数方案导致的持续偏差，提出了一个强化学习框架，以在线学习状态相关的参数化组件。方法在三个理想化测试平台（简单气候偏差校正、辐射对流平衡模型和纬向平均能量平衡模型）上评估了九种强化学习算法，并采用单智能体和联邦多智能体设置。实验结果表明，截断分位数批评、深度确定性策略梯度及双延迟深度确定性策略梯度等算法表现出最高的技能和稳定收敛性，其中单智能体强化学习在减少误差（尤其在热带和中纬度带）方面优于静态调参，而联邦多智能体设置实现了专业化控制和更快收敛，产生了物理意义明确的修正，有效减少了辐射参数、递减率和加热增量的偏差。
GIRL: Generative Imagination Reinforcement Learning via Information-Theoretic Hallucination Control
Authors: Prakul Sunil Hiremath
First: 2026-04-08T17:14:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T17:14:21+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 2 figures, 7 tables; reinforcement learning, world models
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) improves sample efficiency by optimizing policies inside imagined rollouts, but long-horizon planning degrades when model errors compound and imagined trajectories drift off the training manifold. We introduce GIRL (Generative Imagination Reinforcement Learning), a latent world-model framework that addresses this failure mode with two key components. First, a cross-modal grounding signal derived from a frozen foundation model (DINOv2) anchors the latent transition prior to a semantically consistent embedding space, penalizing inconsistent or implausible predictions. Second, an uncertainty-adaptive trust-region bottleneck interprets the KL regularizer as the Lagrange multiplier of a constrained optimization problem, restricting imagination drift within a learned region calibrated by Expected Information Gain and a Relative Performance Loss signal. We re-derive a value-gap bound using the Performance Difference Lemma and Integral Probability Metrics, yielding a bound that remains informative as the discount factor approaches one and connects the objective to real-environment regret. Experiments across three benchmark suites, including DeepMind Control, Adroit Hand Manipulation, and Meta-World with visual distractors, show that GIRL reduces latent rollout drift by 38 to 61 percent across tasks relative to DreamerV3, improves asymptotic return, and requires fewer environment interactions on long-horizon tasks. GIRL also outperforms TD-MPC2 on sparse-reward and high-contact settings under standard evaluation metrics. A distilled-prior variant reduces inference overhead and improves computational efficiency relative to the full model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GIRL：基于信息论幻觉控制的生成式想象强化学习
基于模型的强化学习（MBRL）通过在想象推演中优化策略来提高样本效率，但当模型误差累积导致想象轨迹偏离训练流形时，长时程规划性能会下降。我们提出GIRL（生成式想象强化学习）——一种潜在世界模型框架，通过两个关键组件解决此问题：首先，从冻结基础模型（DINOv2）提取的跨模态锚定信号将潜在状态转移先验约束在语义一致的嵌入空间，惩罚不一致或不可信的预测；其次，不确定性自适应信任区域瓶颈将KL正则器解释为约束优化问题的拉格朗日乘子，通过期望信息增益和相对性能损失信号校准的学习区域限制想象漂移。我们利用性能差异引理和积分概率度量重新推导值差距界，得到在折扣因子趋近于一时仍保持信息量的边界，并将目标与实际环境遗憾关联。在DeepMind Control、Adroit Hand Manipulation及含视觉干扰的Meta-World三个基准测试中，GIRL相比DreamerV3将潜在推演漂移降低38%-61%，提升渐进回报，并在长时程任务中减少环境交互需求。在标准评估指标下，GIRL在稀疏奖励和高接触场景中亦优于TD-MPC2。蒸馏先验变体在保持性能的同时降低了推理开销。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of model error compounding in long-horizon planning for model-based reinforcement learning, which causes imagined trajectories to drift from realistic data, this paper introduces GIRL, a latent world-model framework. The method employs a cross-modal grounding signal from a frozen foundation model to anchor latent transitions in a semantically consistent space and an uncertainty-adaptive trust-region bottleneck to control imagination drift via information-theoretic constraints. Experimental results across DeepMind Control, Adroit Hand Manipulation, and Meta-World benchmarks show that GIRL reduces latent rollout drift by 38–61% compared to DreamerV3, improves asymptotic return, requires fewer environment interactions in long-horizon tasks, and outperforms TD-MPC2 in sparse-reward and high-contact settings.
本文针对基于模型的强化学习中长期规划时模型误差累积导致想象轨迹偏离真实数据分布的问题，提出了GIRL这一潜在世界模型框架。方法上，它利用冻结基础模型提供的跨模态对齐信号将潜在转移锚定在语义一致的嵌入空间中，并通过不确定性自适应的信任区域瓶颈，基于信息论约束控制想象漂移。在DeepMind Control、Adroit Hand Manipulation和Meta-World等基准测试中，实验结果表明，相比DreamerV3，GIRL将潜在推演漂移降低了38%至61%，提升了渐进回报，在长时程任务中减少了环境交互需求，并在稀疏奖励和高接触场景下优于TD-MPC2。
Android Coach: Improve Online Agentic Training Efficiency with Single State Multiple Actions
Authors: Guo Gan, Yuxuan Ding, Cong Chen, Yuwei Ren, Yin Huang, Hong Zhou
First: 2026-04-08T16:40:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T16:40:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Online reinforcement learning (RL) serves as an effective method for enhancing the capabilities of Android agents. However, guiding agents to learn through online interaction is prohibitively expensive due to the high latency of emulators and the sample inefficiency of existing RL algorithms. We identify a fundamental limitation in current approaches: the Single State Single Action paradigm, which updates the policy with one-to-one state-action pairs from online one-way rollouts without fully exploring each costly emulator state. In this paper, we propose Android Coach, a novel framework that shifts the training paradigm to Single State Multiple Actions, allowing the agent to sample and utilize multiple actions for a single online state. We enable this without additional emulator overhead by learning a critic that estimates action values. To ensure the critic serves as a reliable coach, we integrate a process reward model and introduce a group-wise advantage estimator based on the averaged critic outputs. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness and efficiency of Android Coach: it achieves 7.5% and 8.3% success rate improvements on AndroidLab and AndroidWorld over UI-TARS-1.5-7B, and attains 1.4x higher training efficiency than Single State Single Action methods PPO and GRPO at matched success rates.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Android Coach：通过单状态多动作提升在线智能体训练效率
在线强化学习是提升Android智能体能力的有效方法，但模拟器的高延迟与现有算法的样本低效性使得在线交互训练成本极高。本文指出当前方法存在根本局限：单状态单动作范式仅利用在线单向推演的一对一状态-动作对更新策略，未能充分探索每个高成本的模拟器状态。为此，我们提出Android Coach框架，将训练范式转变为单状态多动作，使智能体能对单个在线状态采样并利用多个动作。我们通过学习评估动作价值的评论家模型实现这一目标，且无需额外模拟器开销。为确保评论家作为可靠指导者，我们整合了过程奖励模型，并基于评论家输出均值提出分组优势估计器。大量实验证明Android Coach的高效性：在AndroidLab和AndroidWorld上较UI-TARS-1.5-7B分别提升7.5%和8.3%成功率，在同等成功率下训练效率较PPO、GRPO等单状态单动作方法提升1.4倍。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the high cost and inefficiency of online reinforcement learning for training Android agents, primarily due to emulator latency and the limitations of the Single State Single Action paradigm, which fails to fully exploit each costly state. To address this, the authors propose Android Coach, a framework that shifts to a Single State Multiple Actions paradigm, allowing multiple actions to be sampled from a single online state without extra emulator overhead by learning a critic to estimate action values, enhanced with a process reward model and a group-wise advantage estimator. Experimental results show that Android Coach improves success rates by 7.5% on AndroidLab and 8.3% on AndroidWorld compared to UI-TARS-1.5-7B, and achieves 1.4x higher training efficiency than PPO and GRPO methods at equivalent success rates.
本文的动机在于在线强化学习训练Android智能体时成本高昂且效率低下，主要源于模拟器延迟和单状态单动作范式的局限性，该范式未能充分利用每个高成本状态。为解决此问题，作者提出了Android Coach框架，将训练范式转变为单状态多动作，通过训练一个评估动作价值的评论家，结合过程奖励模型和基于平均评论家输出的分组优势估计器，允许从单个在线状态采样多个动作而无需额外模拟器开销。实验结果表明，Android Coach在AndroidLab和AndroidWorld上相比UI-TARS-1.5-7B分别提升了7.5%和8.3%的成功率，并在相同成功率下比PPO和GRPO方法实现了1.4倍的训练效率提升。
UI-AGILE: Advancing GUI Agents with Effective Reinforcement Learning and Precise Inference-Time Grounding
Authors: Shuquan Lian, Yuhang Wu, Jia Ma, Yifan Ding, Zihan Song, Bingqi Chen, Xiawu Zheng, Hui Li, Rongrong Ji
First: 2025-07-29T17:22:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T16:03:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The emergence of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) has driven significant advances in Graphical User Interface (GUI) agent capabilities. Nevertheless, existing GUI agent training and inference techniques still suffer from a dilemma for reasoning designs, ineffective reward, and visual noise. To address these issues, we introduce UI-AGILE for enhancing GUI agents at both training and inference. For training, we propose a suite of improvements to the Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) process: 1) a continuous reward function to incentivize high-precision grounding; 2) a ``Simple Thinking'' reward to balance planning with speed and grounding accuracy; and 3) a cropping-based resampling strategy to mitigate the sparse reward problem and improve learning on complex tasks. For inference, we present decomposed grounding with selection to dramatically improve grounding accuracy on high-resolution displays by breaking the image into smaller, manageable parts. Experiments show that UI-AGILE achieves the state-of-the-art grounding performance on two benchmarks ScreenSpot-Pro and ScreenSpot-v2 while it also exhibits strong general agent capabilities. For instance, using both our training and inference enhancement methods brings 23\% grounding accuracy improvement over the best baseline on ScreenSpot-Pro. We provide the code in https://github.com/KDEGroup/UI-AGILE.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UI-AGILE：通过高效强化学习与精准推理时定位推进图形用户界面智能体
多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的出现显著推动了图形用户界面（GUI）智能体能力的发展。然而，现有GUI智能体的训练与推理技术仍面临推理设计困境、奖励机制低效及视觉噪声等问题。为解决这些挑战，我们提出UI-AGILE框架，从训练与推理两方面增强GUI智能体。在训练阶段，我们针对监督微调（SFT）过程提出三项改进：1）设计连续奖励函数以激励高精度定位；2）引入“简化思考”奖励机制，平衡规划速度与定位准确性；3）采用基于裁剪的重采样策略，缓解稀疏奖励问题并提升复杂任务的学习效果。在推理阶段，我们提出分解式选择性定位方法，通过将高分辨率显示图像分割为更小的可处理单元，大幅提升定位精度。实验表明，UI-AGILE在ScreenSpot-Pro和ScreenSpot-v2两个基准测试中实现了最先进的定位性能，同时展现出强大的通用智能体能力。例如，结合训练与推理增强方法，在ScreenSpot-Pro上相比最佳基线模型提升了23%的定位准确率。代码已开源：https://github.com/KDEGroup/UI-AGILE。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces UI-AGILE, a method to enhance GUI agents by addressing limitations in reasoning, reward design, and visual noise. The training improvements include a continuous reward for precise grounding, a 'Simple Thinking' reward to balance planning speed and accuracy, and a cropping-based resampling strategy to handle sparse rewards in complex tasks. At inference, it employs decomposed grounding with selection, breaking high-resolution screens into manageable parts to boost accuracy. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art grounding performance on ScreenSpot-Pro and ScreenSpot-v2 benchmarks, with a 23% accuracy improvement over the best baseline on ScreenSpot-Pro, alongside strong general agent capabilities.
本文提出了UI-AGILE方法，旨在通过解决推理设计、奖励机制和视觉噪声方面的不足来增强GUI智能体。在训练阶段，该方法引入了连续奖励函数以激励精确的视觉定位，采用“简单思考”奖励来平衡规划速度与定位准确性，并通过基于裁剪的重采样策略缓解稀疏奖励问题以提升复杂任务的学习效果。在推理阶段，采用分解式定位与选择技术，将高分辨率屏幕分割为更易处理的部分，从而显著提高定位精度。实验结果表明，UI-AGILE在ScreenSpot-Pro和ScreenSpot-v2基准测试中取得了最先进的定位性能，在ScreenSpot-Pro上相比最佳基线提升了23%的准确率，同时展现出强大的通用智能体能力。
Diffusion-based Evolutionary Optimization for 3D Multi-Objective Molecular Generation
Authors: Ruiqing Sun, Dawei Feng, Sen Yang, Ronghang Wang, Huaiyuan Song, Bo Ding, Yijie Wang, Huaimin Wang
First: 2025-05-16T09:32:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T15:48:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Optimizing conflicting molecular properties while strictly adhering to complex 3D structural constraints constitutes a challenging Constrained Multi-Objective Optimization Problem (CMOP). Traditional Evolutionary Algorithms (EAs) destroy chemical valency in 3D space, whereas 3D diffusion models act as rigid generators requiring costly retraining for novel objectives. To bridge this gap, we propose a progressive algorithmic suite. First, we introduce the Evolutionary-Guided Diffusion (EGD) operator, which executes crossover and mutation at an optimally calibrated noise level, leveraging a pre-trained denoising network to project chimeric states back onto the valid chemical manifold. Second, to combat the severe loss of molecular structural diversity inherent in traditional EMO frameworks, we design a Structure-Aware Environmental Selection (SAES) mechanism that explicitly enforces structural distinctiveness. Finally, synergizing EGD and SAES, we develop the Diffusion-based Evolutionary Molecular Optimization (DEMO) framework for CMOPs. To safely navigate disjoint feasible regions, DEMO employs a tri-population architecture with distinct goals: exploring novel chemical scaffolds, refining partially assembled intermediates, and fine-tuning perfectly feasible elite molecules. Extensive experiments across single-property targeting, unconstrained MOPs, multi-fragment CMOPs, and 3D protein-ligand docking demonstrate that our method comprehensively outperforms state-of-the-art baselines and traditional EMO frameworks. Operating entirely zero-shot, this suite consistently discovers highly diverse, chemically valid Pareto frontiers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于扩散的进化优化用于三维多目标分子生成
在严格遵循复杂三维结构约束的同时优化相互冲突的分子特性，构成了一个具有挑战性的约束多目标优化问题。传统进化算法在三维空间中会破坏化学价键，而三维扩散模型作为刚性生成器，需要针对新目标进行昂贵的重新训练。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了一套渐进式算法方案。首先，我们引入进化引导扩散算子，该算子在最优校准的噪声水平上执行交叉和变异，利用预训练的去噪网络将嵌合状态投影回有效的化学流形。其次，为应对传统进化多目标优化框架中固有的分子结构多样性严重损失问题，我们设计了结构感知环境选择机制，明确强制结构独特性。最后，通过协同进化引导扩散与结构感知环境选择，我们开发了用于约束多目标优化问题的基于扩散的进化分子优化框架。为安全探索不连通的可行区域，该框架采用具有不同目标的三种群架构：探索新型化学骨架、优化部分组装中间体、以及微调完全可行的精英分子。在单属性靶向、无约束多目标优化、多片段约束多目标优化和三维蛋白质-配体对接等广泛实验中，我们的方法全面超越了现有先进基线和传统进化多目标优化框架。该方案完全以零样本方式运行，能持续发现高度多样化且化学有效的帕累托前沿。
Summary / 总结
This work addresses the challenge of optimizing conflicting molecular properties under strict 3D structural constraints, a difficult Constrained Multi-Objective Optimization Problem (CMOP). The proposed method bridges the gap between traditional Evolutionary Algorithms, which break chemical valency, and rigid 3D diffusion models that require retraining. It introduces a progressive suite: an Evolutionary-Guided Diffusion operator that performs crossover and mutation at a calibrated noise level using a pre-trained denoising network, a Structure-Aware Environmental Selection mechanism to preserve structural diversity, and the integrated Diffusion-based Evolutionary Molecular Optimization (DEMO) framework with a tri-population architecture for safe exploration. Experimental results across single-property targeting, unconstrained MOPs, multi-fragment CMOPs, and 3D protein-ligand docking show that the method, operating zero-shot, comprehensively outperforms state-of-the-art baselines and traditional frameworks, consistently generating diverse, chemically valid Pareto frontiers.
本研究旨在解决在严格三维结构约束下优化冲突分子特性的挑战，这是一个困难的约束多目标优化问题。所提出的方法弥合了传统进化算法（会破坏化学价键）与需要重新训练的刚性三维扩散模型之间的差距。它引入了一个渐进式算法套件：包括在标定噪声水平下利用预训练去噪网络执行交叉和变异的进化引导扩散算子、用于保持结构多样性的结构感知环境选择机制，以及集成上述组件并采用三群体架构以安全探索的扩散进化分子优化框架。在单属性优化、无约束多目标问题、多片段约束问题及三维蛋白质-配体对接上的实验结果表明，该零样本方法全面优于现有先进基线和传统框架，能持续生成多样且化学有效的帕累托前沿。
LeLaR: The First In-Orbit Demonstration of an AI-Based Satellite Attitude Controller
Authors: Kirill Djebko, Tom Baumann, Erik Dilger, Frank Puppe, Sergio Montenegro
Venue: IEEE Access, vol. 14, pp. 49348-49367, 2026
First: 2025-12-22T17:00:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T15:38:50+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication in IEEE Access (DOI: 10.1109/ACCESS.2026.3678816). This is the author's version which has not been fully edited and content may change prior to final publication. 20 pages, 15 figures, 18 tables. The maneuver telemetry datasets are available in the GitHub repository under https://github.com/kdjebko/lelar-in-orbit-data
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Attitude control is essential for many satellite missions. Classical controllers, however, are time-consuming to design and sensitive to model uncertainties and variations in operational boundary conditions. Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) offers a promising alternative by learning adaptive control strategies through autonomous interaction with a simulation environment. Overcoming the Sim2Real gap, which involves deploying an agent trained in simulation onto the real physical satellite, remains a significant challenge. In this work, we present the first successful in-orbit demonstration of an AI-based attitude controller for inertial pointing maneuvers. The controller was trained entirely in simulation and deployed to the InnoCube 3U nanosatellite, which was developed by the Julius-Maximilians-Universität Würzburg in cooperation with the Technische Universität Berlin, and launched in January 2025. We present the AI agent design, the methodology of the training procedure, the discrepancies between the simulation and the observed behavior of the real satellite, and a comparison of the AI-based attitude controller with the classical PD controller of InnoCube. Steady-state metrics confirm the robust performance of the AI-based controller during repeated in-orbit maneuvers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LeLaR：首个基于人工智能的卫星姿态控制器在轨演示验证
姿态控制对多数卫星任务至关重要。然而，传统控制器设计耗时，且对模型不确定性与运行边界条件变化敏感。深度强化学习通过仿真环境自主交互学习自适应控制策略，提供了有前景的替代方案。克服仿真到现实的鸿沟——即将仿真训练的智能体部署至真实物理卫星——仍是重大挑战。本研究首次成功演示了基于人工智能的姿态控制器在惯性指向机动中的在轨应用。该控制器完全在仿真环境中训练，并部署于由维尔茨堡大学与柏林工业大学合作研制、于2025年1月发射的InnoCube 3U纳卫星。我们阐述了人工智能智能体设计、训练流程方法、仿真与真实卫星观测行为间的差异，以及基于人工智能的姿态控制器与InnoCube传统PD控制器的对比。稳态指标证实了该人工智能控制器在重复在轨机动中的鲁棒性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of classical satellite attitude controllers, which are time-consuming to design and sensitive to model uncertainties, this work demonstrates the first in-orbit use of a Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) based controller to enable adaptive control. The method involved training an AI agent entirely in simulation and then deploying it on the InnoCube nanosatellite to perform inertial pointing maneuvers, directly addressing the Sim2Real transfer challenge. Experimental results from orbital tests show that the AI controller achieved robust performance during repeated maneuvers, with steady-state metrics confirming its effectiveness compared to the satellite's classical PD controller.
针对传统卫星姿态控制器设计耗时且对模型不确定性敏感的问题，本研究首次在轨演示了基于深度强化学习（DRL）的自适应姿态控制方法。该方法通过在仿真环境中完全训练AI智能体，并将其部署至InnoCube立方星上执行惯性指向机动，以应对仿真到现实的迁移挑战。在轨实验结果表明，该AI控制器在重复机动中表现出稳健的性能，其稳态指标证实了相较于卫星传统PD控制器的有效性。
Smart Commander: A Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning Framework for Fleet-Level PHM Decision Optimization
Authors: Yong Si, Mingfei Lu, Jing Li, Yang Hu, Guijiang Li, Yueheng Song, Zhaokui Wang
First: 2026-04-08T15:00:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T15:00:12+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 6 figures, 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decision-making in military aviation Prognostics and Health Management (PHM) faces significant challenges due to the "curse of dimensionality" in large-scale fleet operations, combined with sparse feedback and stochastic mission profiles. To address these issues, this paper proposes Smart Commander, a novel Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning (HRL) framework designed to optimize sequential maintenance and logistics decisions. The framework decomposes the complex control problem into a two-tier hierarchy: a strategic General Commander manages fleet-level availability and cost objectives, while tactical Operation Commanders execute specific actions for sortie generation, maintenance scheduling, and resource allocation. The proposed approach is validated within a custom-built, high-fidelity discrete-event simulation environment that captures the dynamics of aircraft configuration and support logistics.By integrating layered reward shaping with planning-enhanced neural networks, the method effectively addresses the difficulty of sparse and delayed rewards. Empirical evaluations demonstrate that Smart Commander significantly outperforms conventional monolithic Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) and rule-based baselines. Notably, it achieves a substantial reduction in training time while demonstrating superior scalability and robustness in failure-prone environments. These results highlight the potential of HRL as a reliable paradigm for next-generation intelligent fleet management.

标题：智能指挥官：一种用于机队级PHM决策优化的分层强化学习框架
军事航空预测与健康管理（PHM）中的决策面临大规模机队运营中的“维度灾难”、稀疏反馈及随机任务剖面的重大挑战。为应对这些问题，本文提出智能指挥官，一种新颖的分层强化学习（HRL）框架，旨在优化顺序维护与后勤决策。该框架将复杂控制问题分解为双层结构：战略级总指挥官管理机队可用性与成本目标，战术级作战指挥官则执行具体的出动生成、维护调度与资源分配行动。所提方法在一个定制的高保真离散事件仿真环境中得到验证，该环境捕捉了飞机配置与保障后勤的动态特性。通过将分层奖励塑形与规划增强神经网络相结合，该方法有效解决了稀疏与延迟奖励的难题。实证评估表明，智能指挥官显著优于传统的单体深度强化学习（DRL）与基于规则的基线方法，尤其在训练时间大幅缩短的同时，在易故障环境中展现出卓越的可扩展性与鲁棒性。这些结果凸显了HRL作为下一代智能机队管理可靠范式的潜力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenges of decision-making in military aviation Prognostics and Health Management (PHM), such as the curse of dimensionality and sparse feedback in large-scale fleet operations, by proposing Smart Commander, a Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning (HRL) framework. The method decomposes the problem into a two-tier hierarchy with a strategic General Commander for fleet-level objectives and tactical Operation Commanders for specific actions like maintenance scheduling, using layered reward shaping and planning-enhanced neural networks to handle sparse rewards. Experimental results from a high-fidelity simulation show that Smart Commander outperforms conventional Deep Reinforcement Learning and rule-based baselines, achieving reduced training time and superior scalability and robustness in failure-prone environments.
本文针对军事航空预测与健康管理（PHM）中大规模机队运营面临的维度灾难和稀疏反馈等决策挑战，提出了Smart Commander这一分层强化学习框架。该方法将复杂控制问题分解为两层结构：战略性的总指挥官管理机队可用性和成本目标，战术性的操作指挥官执行具体的任务生成、维护调度和资源分配行动，并通过分层奖励塑造和规划增强的神经网络处理稀疏奖励。在高保真离散事件仿真环境中的实证评估表明，Smart Commander显著优于传统的单体深度强化学习和基于规则的基线方法，在减少训练时间的同时，在易故障环境中展现出卓越的可扩展性和鲁棒性。
Reason in Chains, Learn in Trees: Self-Rectification and Grafting for Multi-turn Agent Policy Optimization
Authors: Yu Li, Sizhe Tang, Tian Lan
First: 2026-04-08T14:55:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T14:55:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning for Large Language Model agents is often hindered by sparse rewards in multi-step reasoning tasks. Existing approaches like Group Relative Policy Optimization treat sampled trajectories as independent chains, assigning uniform credit to all steps in each chain and ignoring the existence of critical steps that may disproportionally impact reasoning outcome. In this paper, we propose T-STAR(Tree-structured Self-Taught Agent Rectification), a framework that recovers the latent correlated reward structure across seemingly independent trajectories. Specifically, we consolidate trajectories into a unified Cognitive Tree by identifying and merging functionally similar steps/nodes. It enables an Introspective Valuation mechanism that back-propagates trajectory-level rewards through the tree to obtain a new notion of variance-reduced relative advantage at step-level. Using the Cognitive Tree, we also develop In-Context Thought Grafting to synthesize corrective reasoning by contrasting successful and failed branches at critical divergence points/steps. Our proposed Surgical Policy Optimization then capitalizes on the rich policy gradient information concentrated at these critical points/steps through a Bradley-Terry type of surgical loss. Extensive experiments across embodied, interactive, reasoning, and planning benchmarks demonstrate that T-STAR achieves consistent improvements over strong baselines, with gains most pronounced on tasks requiring extended reasoning chains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：链中推理，树中学习：多轮智能体策略优化的自校正与嫁接方法
大语言模型智能体的强化学习常受多步推理任务中稀疏奖励的制约。现有方法（如组相对策略优化）将采样轨迹视为独立链，对每条链的所有步骤赋予均匀奖励，忽略了可能对推理结果产生不成比例影响的关键步骤。本文提出T-STAR（树状结构自教导智能体校正）框架，该框架能还原看似独立轨迹间的潜在关联奖励结构。具体而言，我们通过识别并合并功能相似的步骤/节点，将轨迹整合为统一的认知树。这实现了内省评估机制，可将轨迹级奖励沿树反向传播，从而获得步骤级方差缩减的相对优势新度量。基于认知树，我们还开发了上下文思维嫁接技术，通过对比关键分歧点/步骤的成功与失败分支来合成校正推理。随后，我们提出的精准策略优化利用集中于这些关键点/步骤的丰富策略梯度信息，通过布拉德利-特里型精准损失函数实现优化。在具身交互、推理和规划等多个基准测试上的广泛实验表明，T-STAR相较于强基线模型取得了一致性改进，在需要长链推理的任务上提升尤为显著。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of sparse rewards in reinforcement learning for multi-turn LLM agents, where existing methods fail to differentiate critical reasoning steps. It introduces T-STAR, a framework that consolidates sampled trajectories into a Cognitive Tree to uncover latent reward structures, employing Introspective Valuation for step-level advantage estimation and In-Context Thought Grafting to synthesize corrective reasoning by contrasting successful and failed branches. Experimental results across embodied, interactive, reasoning, and planning benchmarks show that T-STAR consistently outperforms strong baselines, with particularly significant gains on tasks involving long reasoning chains.
本文针对多轮大型语言模型智能体强化学习中奖励稀疏的问题，提出现有方法未能区分关键推理步骤的局限性。作者开发了T-STAR框架，通过将采样轨迹整合为认知树来揭示潜在的奖励结构，利用内省评估机制进行步骤级优势估计，并采用上下文思维嫁接技术，通过对比成功与失败分支来合成纠正性推理。在具身、交互、推理和规划等多个基准测试上的实验结果表明，T-STAR持续优于现有强基线方法，尤其在需要长推理链的任务上提升最为显著。
Dual-Rerank: Fusing Causality and Utility for Industrial Generative Reranking
Authors: Chao Zhang, Shuai Lin, ChengLei Dai, Ye Qian, Fan Mingyang, Yi Zhang, Yi Wang, Jingwei Zhuo
First: 2026-04-08T14:54:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T14:54:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Kuaishou serves over 400 million daily active users, processing hundreds of millions of search queries daily against a repository of tens of billions of short videos. As the final decision layer, the reranking stage determines user experience by optimizing whole-page utility. While traditional score-and-sort methods fail to capture combinatorial dependencies, Generative Reranking offers a superior paradigm by directly modeling the permutation probability. However, deploying Generative Reranking in such a high-stakes environment faces a fundamental dual dilemma: 1) the structural trade-off where Autoregressive (AR) models offer superior Sequential modeling but suffer from prohibitive latency, versus Non-Autoregressive (NAR) models that enable efficiency but lack dependency capturing; 2) the optimization gap where Supervised Learning faces challenges in directly optimizing whole-page utility, while Reinforcement Learning (RL) struggles with instability in high-throughput data streams. To resolve this, we propose Dual-Rerank, a unified framework designed for industrial reranking that bridges the structural gap via Sequential Knowledge Distillation and addresses the optimization gap using List-wise Decoupled Reranking Optimization (LDRO) for stable online RL. Extensive A/B testing on production traffic demonstrates that Dual-Rerank achieves State-of-the-Art performance, significantly improving User satisfaction and Watch Time while drastically reducing inference latency compared to AR baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：双路重排：融合因果性与效用的工业级生成式重排框架
快手平台日活跃用户超4亿，每日需处理数亿次搜索查询，其内容库包含数百亿短视频。作为最终决策层，重排阶段通过优化整页效用决定用户体验。传统评分排序方法难以捕捉组合依赖关系，而生成式重排通过直接建模排列概率提供了更优范式。然而，在此高要求场景部署生成式重排面临双重困境：1）结构权衡——自回归模型具备优异序列建模能力但延迟过高，非自回归模型虽高效却缺乏依赖捕获能力；2）优化鸿沟——监督学习难以直接优化整页效用，而强化学习在高吞吐数据流中存在稳定性挑战。为此，我们提出Dual-Rerank统一框架，通过序列知识蒸馏弥合结构鸿沟，并采用列表解耦重排优化实现稳定的在线强化学习。生产流量A/B测试表明，Dual-Rerank取得业界最优性能，在显著提升用户满意度与观看时长的同时，较自回归基线大幅降低推理延迟。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the dual challenges of structural trade-offs and optimization gaps in deploying generative reranking for large-scale industrial systems like Kuaishou's video search, where traditional methods fail to capture combinatorial dependencies. The method introduces Dual-Rerank, a unified framework that bridges the structural gap via Sequential Knowledge Distillation to combine the efficiency of non-autoregressive models with the dependency modeling of autoregressive ones, and addresses the optimization gap using List-wise Decoupled Reranking Optimization for stable online reinforcement learning. Main experimental results from extensive A/B testing on production traffic show that Dual-Rerank achieves state-of-the-art performance, significantly improving user satisfaction and watch time while drastically reducing inference latency compared to autoregressive baselines.
本研究的动机是解决在快手等大规模工业系统中部署生成式重排时面临的结构性权衡和优化差距的双重挑战，传统方法在此类视频搜索场景中难以捕捉组合依赖性。方法上提出了Dual-Rerank统一框架，通过序列知识蒸馏来融合非自回归模型的高效性和自回归模型的依赖性建模能力，以弥合结构差距，并采用列表解耦重排优化实现稳定的在线强化学习来应对优化差距。主要实验结果表明，在生产流量上的广泛A/B测试中，Dual-Rerank实现了最先进的性能，与自回归基线相比，显著提升了用户满意度和观看时长，同时大幅降低了推理延迟。
Multi-Turn Reasoning LLMs for Task Offloading in Mobile Edge Computing
Authors: Ning Yang, Chuangxin Cheng, Haijun Zhang
First: 2026-04-08T14:38:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T14:38:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Emerging computation-intensive applications impose stringent latency requirements on resource-constrained mobile devices. Mobile Edge Computing (MEC) addresses this challenge through task offloading. However, designing effective policies remains difficult due to dynamic task arrivals, time-varying channels, and the spatio-temporal coupling of server queues. Conventional heuristics lack adaptability, while Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) suffers from limited generalization and architectural rigidity, requiring retraining when network topology changes. Although Large Language Models (LLMs) offer semantic reasoning capabilities, standard Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) yields myopic policies that greedily minimize immediate latency without accounting for long-term system evolution. To address these limitations, we propose COMLLM, a generative framework that enables foresighted decision-making in MEC systems. COMLLM integrates Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with a Look-Ahead Collaborative Simulation (LACS) mechanism, which performs multi-step Monte Carlo rollouts while jointly modeling server queue dynamics. By incorporating these rollouts into the reward design, the framework captures the long-term impact of current decisions on future system states. Experimental results demonstrate that COMLLM achieves near-optimal latency and improved load-balancing fairness. Notably, it exhibits zero-shot topological scalability, allowing a model trained on small-scale networks to generalize to larger, unseen topologies without retraining, outperforming SFT, DRL, and heuristic baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向移动边缘计算任务卸载的多轮推理大语言模型
新兴计算密集型应用对资源受限的移动设备提出了严格的延迟要求。移动边缘计算（MEC）通过任务卸载应对这一挑战，但由于动态任务到达、时变信道及服务器队列的时空耦合，设计高效策略仍面临困难。传统启发式方法缺乏适应性，而深度强化学习（DRL）存在泛化能力有限和架构僵化问题，需在网络拓扑变化时重新训练。尽管大语言模型（LLMs）具备语义推理能力，但标准监督微调（SFT）会产生短视策略，仅贪婪地最小化即时延迟，未考虑长期系统演化。为突破这些局限，我们提出COMLLM——一个支持MEC系统前瞻性决策的生成框架。该框架将组相对策略优化（GRPO）与前瞻协作模拟（LACS）机制结合，通过多步蒙特卡洛推演联合建模服务器队列动态，并将推演结果融入奖励设计，从而捕捉当前决策对未来系统状态的长期影响。实验表明，COMLLM实现了接近最优的延迟和更优的负载均衡公平性。其具备零样本拓扑可扩展性，允许基于小规模网络训练的模型无需重训练即可泛化至更大未知拓扑，性能超越SFT、DRL及启发式基线方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of designing adaptive task offloading policies in Mobile Edge Computing (MEC), where dynamic conditions and long-term system effects render conventional heuristics and Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) approaches inadequate. The authors propose COMLLM, a framework that equips a Large Language Model (LLM) with foresight by integrating Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with a Look-Ahead Collaborative Simulation (LACS) mechanism, which performs multi-step Monte Carlo rollouts to model future queue dynamics and inform reward design. Experimental results show that COMLLM achieves near-optimal latency and improved load balancing, and uniquely demonstrates zero-shot generalization to larger, unseen network topologies without retraining, outperforming SFT, DRL, and heuristic baselines.
本文针对移动边缘计算（MEC）中设计自适应任务卸载策略的挑战展开研究，传统启发式方法和深度强化学习（DRL）因动态环境及长期系统效应而存在不足。作者提出了COMLLM框架，通过将组相对策略优化（GRPO）与前瞻协作模拟（LACS）机制相结合，使大型语言模型（LLM）具备预见能力；LACS执行多步蒙特卡洛推演以建模未来队列动态并指导奖励设计。实验结果表明，COMLLM实现了接近最优的延迟和更好的负载均衡公平性，并显著展现出零样本拓扑可扩展性，即在小规模网络上训练的模型无需重新训练即可泛化到更大、未见过的拓扑结构，其性能超越了监督微调、DRL及启发式基线方法。
Energy Saving for Cell-Free Massive MIMO Networks: A Multi-Agent Deep Reinforcement Learning Approach
Authors: Qichen Wang, Keyu Li, Ozan Alp Topal, Özlem Tugfe Demir, Mustafa Ozger, Cicek Cavdar
First: 2026-04-08T14:27:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T14:27:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper focuses on energy savings in downlink operation of cell-free massive MIMO (CF mMIMO) networks under dynamic traffic conditions. We propose a multi-agent deep reinforcement learning (MADRL) algorithm that enables each access point (AP) to autonomously control antenna re-configuration and advanced sleep mode (ASM) selection. After the training process, the proposed framework operates in a fully distributed manner, eliminating the need for centralized control and allowing each AP to dynamically adjust to real-time traffic fluctuations. Simulation results show that the proposed algorithm reduces power consumption (PC) by 56.23% compared to systems without any energy-saving scheme and by 30.12% relative to a non-learning mechanism that only utilizes the lightest sleep mode, with only a slight increase in drop ratio. Moreover, compared to the widely used deep Q-network (DQN) algorithm, it achieves a similar PC level but with a significantly lower drop ratio.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无蜂窝大规模MIMO网络节能：一种多智能体深度强化学习方法
本文聚焦于动态流量条件下无蜂窝大规模MIMO（CF mMIMO）网络下行链路的节能问题。我们提出了一种多智能体深度强化学习（MADRL）算法，使每个接入点（AP）能够自主控制天线重配置和高级休眠模式（ASM）选择。训练完成后，所提框架以完全分布式方式运行，无需集中控制，允许每个AP动态适应实时流量波动。仿真结果表明，与无节能方案的系统相比，该算法降低了56.23%的功耗（PC）；相较于仅使用最浅休眠模式的非学习机制，功耗降低了30.12%，且掉线率仅轻微上升。此外，与广泛使用的深度Q网络（DQN）算法相比，它在达到相近功耗水平的同时，实现了显著更低的掉线率。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to reduce energy consumption in cell-free massive MIMO networks under dynamic traffic. The method employs a multi-agent deep reinforcement learning framework where each access point autonomously learns to control antenna configuration and select advanced sleep modes, operating in a fully distributed manner after training. The main experimental results demonstrate that the proposed algorithm reduces power consumption by 56.23% compared to a baseline with no energy-saving scheme and by 30.12% relative to a non-learning mechanism using only the lightest sleep mode, while maintaining a similar power consumption level to a deep Q-network approach but with a significantly lower connection drop ratio.
本文旨在降低动态流量下无蜂窝大规模MIMO网络的能耗。方法上采用多智能体深度强化学习框架，使每个接入点在训练后能自主控制天线配置并选择高级睡眠模式，实现完全分布式运行。主要实验结果表明，所提算法相比无节能方案的基线系统降低了56.23%的功耗，相比仅使用最浅睡眠模式的非学习机制降低了30.12%的功耗，且与广泛使用的深度Q网络算法相比，在保持相似功耗水平的同时显著降低了连接丢弃率。
Bayesian Optimization for Mixed-Variable Problems in the Natural Sciences
Authors: Yuhao Zhang, Ti John, Matthias Stosiek, Patrick Rinke
First: 2026-04-08T13:55:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T13:55:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Optimizing expensive black-box objectives over mixed search spaces is a common challenge across the natural sciences. Bayesian optimization (BO) offers sample-efficient strategies through probabilistic surrogate models and acquisition functions. However, its effectiveness diminishes in mixed or high-cardinality discrete spaces, where gradients are unavailable and optimizing the acquisition function becomes computationally demanding. In this work, we generalize the probabilistic reparameterization (PR) approach of Daulton et al. to handle non-equidistant discrete variables, enabling gradient-based optimization in fully mixed-variable settings with Gaussian process (GP) surrogates. With real-world scientific optimization tasks in mind, we conduct systematic benchmarks on synthetic and experimental objectives to obtain an optimized kernel formulations and demonstrate the robustness of our generalized PR method. We additionally show that, when combined with a modified BO workflow, our approach can efficiently optimize highly discontinuous and discretized objective landscapes. This work establishes a practical BO framework for addressing fully mixed optimization problems in the natural sciences, and is particularly well suited to autonomous laboratory settings where noise, discretization, and limited data are inherent.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向自然科学中混合变量问题的贝叶斯优化方法
在混合搜索空间上优化昂贵黑箱目标函数是自然科学领域的常见挑战。贝叶斯优化通过概率代理模型和采集函数提供样本高效策略，但在混合或高基数离散空间中，其有效性会因梯度缺失和采集函数优化计算成本高昂而降低。本研究推广Daulton等人的概率重参数化方法，以处理非等距离散变量，从而在采用高斯过程代理的完全混合变量场景中实现基于梯度的优化。针对实际科学优化任务，我们在合成与实验目标上进行了系统基准测试，获得了优化的核函数形式，并证明了广义PR方法的鲁棒性。进一步研究表明，结合改进的贝叶斯优化流程，本方法能高效优化高度不连续且离散化的目标函数景观。这项工作为处理自然科学中的完全混合优化问题建立了实用框架，尤其适用于噪声、离散化和数据受限的自主实验室环境。
Summary / 总结
This work addresses the challenge of optimizing expensive black-box functions over mixed-variable search spaces, a common problem in the natural sciences where Bayesian optimization (BO) often struggles with high-cardinality or non-equidistant discrete variables. The method generalizes the probabilistic reparameterization (PR) technique to handle such mixed spaces, enabling gradient-based optimization with Gaussian process surrogates. Experimental results from systematic benchmarks on synthetic and real-world tasks demonstrate the robustness of the approach and its effectiveness in optimizing highly discontinuous, discretized landscapes, establishing a practical BO framework suited for noisy, data-limited autonomous laboratory environments.

STRIDE-ED: A Strategy-Grounded Stepwise Reasoning Framework for Empathetic Dialogue Systems
Authors: Hongru Ji, Yuyin Fan, Meng Zhao, Xianghua Li, Lianwei Wu, Chao Gao
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-08T13:53:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T13:53:27+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Empathetic dialogue requires not only recognizing a user's emotional state but also making strategy-aware, context-sensitive decisions throughout response generation. However, the lack of a comprehensive empathy strategy framework, explicit task-aligned multi-stage reasoning, and high-quality strategy-aware data fundamentally limits existing approaches, preventing them from effectively modeling empathetic dialogue as a complex, multi-stage cognitive and decision-making process. To address these challenges, we propose STRIDE-ED, a STRategy-grounded, Interpretable, and DEep reasoning framework that models Empathetic Dialogue through structured, strategy-conditioned reasoning. To support effective learning, we develop a strategy-aware data refinement pipeline integrating LLM-based annotation, multi-model consistency-weighted evaluation, and dynamic sampling to construct high-quality training data aligned with empathetic strategies. Furthermore, we adopt a two-stage training paradigm that combines supervised fine-tuning with multi-objective reinforcement learning to better align model behaviors with target emotions, empathetic strategies, and response formats. Extensive experiments demonstrate that STRIDE-ED generalizes across diverse open-source LLMs and consistently outperforms existing methods on both automatic metrics and human evaluations.

标题：STRIDE-ED：基于策略的渐进式推理框架用于共情对话系统
共情对话不仅需要识别用户情绪状态，更需在响应生成过程中进行策略感知、情境敏感的决策。然而，现有方法因缺乏完整的共情策略框架、明确任务对齐的多阶段推理机制及高质量策略感知数据，难以将共情对话有效建模为复杂的多阶段认知决策过程。为此，我们提出STRIDE-ED——一个基于策略、可解释的深度推理框架，通过结构化策略条件推理建模共情对话。为支持有效学习，我们开发了策略感知数据精炼流程，集成基于大语言模型的标注、多模型一致性加权评估和动态采样，构建与共情策略对齐的高质量训练数据。此外，采用监督微调与多目标强化学习相结合的两阶段训练范式，使模型行为更好地对齐目标情绪、共情策略及响应格式。大量实验表明，STRIDE-ED能泛化至多种开源大语言模型，在自动指标和人工评估中均持续优于现有方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing empathetic dialogue systems in lacking a comprehensive strategy framework and explicit multi-stage reasoning, this paper proposes STRIDE-ED, a strategy-grounded and interpretable reasoning framework that models empathetic dialogue through structured, strategy-conditioned reasoning. The method involves constructing high-quality strategy-aware training data via an LLM-based annotation and evaluation pipeline, followed by a two-stage training paradigm combining supervised fine-tuning with multi-objective reinforcement learning. Experimental results show that STRIDE-ED generalizes across various LLMs and outperforms existing methods on both automatic metrics and human evaluations.

Epistemic Robust Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Abhilash Reddy Chenreddy, Erick Delage
First: 2026-04-08T13:26:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T13:26:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning learns policies from fixed datasets without further environment interaction. A key challenge in this setting is epistemic uncertainty, arising from limited or biased data coverage, particularly when the behavior policy systematically avoids certain actions. This can lead to inaccurate value estimates and unreliable generalization. Ensemble-based methods like SAC-N mitigate this by conservatively estimating Q-values using the ensemble minimum, but they require large ensembles and often conflate epistemic with aleatoric uncertainty. To address these limitations, we propose a unified and generalizable framework that replaces discrete ensembles with compact uncertainty sets over Q-values. %We further introduce an Epinet based model that directly shapes the uncertainty sets to optimize the cumulative reward under the robust Bellman objective without relying on ensembles. We also introduce a benchmark for evaluating offline RL algorithms under risk-sensitive behavior policies, and demonstrate that our method achieves improved robustness and generalization over ensemble-based baselines across both tabular and continuous state domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：认知鲁棒离线强化学习
离线强化学习从固定数据集中学习策略，无需与环境进一步交互。该场景下的核心挑战是认知不确定性，源于有限或有偏的数据覆盖，尤其当行为策略系统性地规避某些动作时，这可能导致价值估计不准确与泛化不可靠。基于集成的方法（如SAC-N）通过集成最小值保守估计Q值来缓解此问题，但需要大规模集成且常混淆认知不确定性与偶然不确定性。为突破这些局限，我们提出一个统一且可泛化的框架，用紧凑的Q值不确定性集合替代离散集成。我们进一步引入基于Epinet的模型，直接构建不确定性集合以在鲁棒贝尔曼目标下优化累积奖励，无需依赖集成。同时，我们建立了评估风险敏感行为策略下离线强化学习算法的基准测试，并证明该方法在表格与连续状态域中均比基于集成的基线具有更强的鲁棒性与泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of epistemic uncertainty in offline reinforcement learning, which arises from limited or biased data coverage and can lead to inaccurate value estimates. The authors propose a unified framework that replaces traditional ensemble methods with compact uncertainty sets over Q-values, aiming to directly optimize the robust Bellman objective without relying on large ensembles. Experimental results on a new benchmark for risk-sensitive behavior policies show that the method achieves improved robustness and generalization over ensemble-based baselines in both tabular and continuous domains.
本文针对离线强化学习中因数据覆盖有限或偏差导致的认知不确定性挑战，该问题可能引发价值估计不准确。作者提出一个统一框架，用紧凑的Q值不确定性集合替代传统集成方法，旨在直接优化鲁棒贝尔曼目标而无需依赖大型集成。在针对风险敏感行为策略的新基准测试中，实验结果表明该方法在表格和连续状态域上均比基于集成的基线实现了更好的鲁棒性和泛化能力。
Apple: Toward General Active Perception via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tim Schneider, Cristiana de Farias, Roberto Calandra, Liming Chen, Jan Peters
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-05-09T16:49:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T13:14:26+00:00
Comments: 27 pages; 21 figures; accepted at the Fourteenth International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Active perception is a fundamental skill that enables us humans to deal with uncertainty in our inherently partially observable environment. For senses such as touch, where the information is sparse and local, active perception becomes crucial. In recent years, active perception has emerged as an important research domain in robotics. However, current methods are often bound to specific tasks or make strong assumptions, which limit their generality. To address this gap, this work introduces APPLE (Active Perception Policy Learning) - a novel framework that leverages reinforcement learning (RL) to address a range of different active perception problems. APPLE jointly trains a transformer-based perception module and decision-making policy with a unified optimization objective, learning how to actively gather information. By design, APPLE is not limited to a specific task and can, in principle, be applied to a wide range of active perception problems. We evaluate two variants of APPLE across different tasks, including tactile exploration problems from the Tactile MNIST benchmark. Experiments demonstrate the efficacy of APPLE, achieving high accuracies on both regression and classification tasks. These findings underscore the potential of APPLE as a versatile and general framework for advancing active perception in robotics. Project page: https://timschneider42.github.io/apple

Motivated by the need for general active perception methods in robotics, which are often task-specific or rely on strong assumptions, this paper introduces APPLE, a reinforcement learning framework that jointly trains a transformer-based perception module and a decision-making policy to actively gather information. The method is designed to be task-agnostic and is evaluated on various tasks, including tactile exploration from the Tactile MNIST benchmark. Experimental results show that APPLE achieves high accuracy on both regression and classification tasks, demonstrating its potential as a versatile framework for active perception.

Production-Ready Automated ECU Calibration using Residual Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Andreas Kampmeier, Kevin Badalian, Lucas Koch, Sung-Yong Lee, Jakob Andert
First: 2026-04-08T13:10:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T13:10:20+00:00
Comments: This manuscript has been submitted to SAE as a conference paper for the 2026 Stuttgart International Symposium on Automotive and Powertrain Technology
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Electronic Control Units (ECUs) have played a pivotal role in transforming motorcars of yore into the modern vehicles we see on our roads today. They actively regulate the actuation of individual components and thus determine the characteristics of the whole system. In this, the behavior of the control functions heavily depends on their calibration parameters which engineers traditionally design by hand. This is taking place in an environment of rising customer expectations and steadily shorter product development cycles. At the same time, legislative requirements are increasing while emission standards are getting stricter. Considering the number of vehicle variants on top of all that, the conventional method is losing its practical and financial viability. Prior work has already demonstrated that optimal control functions can be automatically developed with reinforcement learning (RL); since the resulting functions are represented by artificial neural networks, they lack explainability, a circumstance which renders them challenging to employ in production vehicles. In this article, we present an explainable approach to automating the calibration process using residual RL which follows established automotive development principles. Its applicability is demonstrated by means of a map-based air path controller in a series control unit using a hardware-in-the-loop (HiL) platform. Starting with a sub-optimal map, the proposed methodology quickly converges to a calibration which closely resembles the reference in the series ECU. The results prove that the approach is suitable for the industry where it leads to better calibrations in significantly less time and requires virtually no human intervention
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于残差强化学习的量产级自动ECU标定方法
电子控制单元（ECU）在将传统汽车转变为现代车辆的过程中发挥着关键作用。它通过主动调节各部件执行机构，决定整个系统的运行特性。其中控制函数的行为高度依赖标定参数，传统上这些参数由工程师手动设计。当前客户期望持续提升、产品开发周期不断缩短，同时法规要求日益严格、排放标准不断提高，加之车型变体数量激增，传统方法在实践可行性和经济性方面面临挑战。已有研究表明强化学习（RL）可自动生成最优控制函数，但由于其采用人工神经网络实现，缺乏可解释性，难以应用于量产车辆。本文提出一种基于残差强化学习的可解释自动标定方法，遵循成熟的汽车开发原则。通过硬件在环（HiL）平台对系列控制单元中的基于脉谱图的气路控制器进行验证，该方法能从次优初始脉谱图快速收敛至接近量产ECU参考值的标定结果。实验证明该方案适用于工业应用，能在显著缩短时间内获得更优标定，且几乎无需人工干预。

The method applies residual RL to optimize calibration parameters, starting from a sub-optimal baseline, and is validated on a hardware-in-the-loop platform with a map-based air path controller in a series ECU. Experimental results show the approach quickly converges to a calibration closely matching the reference, demonstrating its industrial viability for achieving better calibrations in significantly less time with minimal human intervention.
针对现代汽车中电子控制单元（ECU）手动标定日益复杂且耗时的问题，本文提出了一种可解释的自动化方法，采用残差强化学习（RL）以遵循汽车开发标准。该方法应用残差RL从次优基线开始优化标定参数，并在硬件在环平台上使用系列ECU中的基于图谱的空气路径控制器进行了验证。实验结果表明，该方法能快速收敛到与参考标定高度接近的结果，证明了其在工业应用中的可行性，能够以更少时间和几乎无需人工干预获得更优标定。
SubSearch: Intermediate Rewards for Unsupervised Guided Reasoning in Complex Retrieval
Authors: Roxana Petcu, Evangelos Kanoulas, Maarten de Rijke
First: 2026-04-08T13:09:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T13:09:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are probabilistic in nature and perform more reliably when augmented with external information. As complex queries often require multi-step reasoning over the retrieved information, with no clear or predetermined reasoning path, they remain challenging. Recent approaches train models using reinforcement learning on the model's outcome, showing promise in improving how models handle complex information. We introduce SubSearch, a specialized framework that shifts from outcome-only supervision to intermediate reward signals that incentivize planning high-quality reasoning. Unlike previous work on process reward modeling, which focuses on training a separate reward model with annotated trajectories by either human annotators or large LLM judges, SubSearch directly optimizes the generator using intrinsic process rewards, which we define as internally-derived rewards, eliminating the need for external supervision, and moving towards autonomous information-intensive reasoning. Experiments on seven benchmarks show that rewarding intermediate reasoning steps with intrinsic rewards leads to more robust reasoning traces in both QA and multi-hop QA datasets over using only outcome rewards. SubSearch can help in building reasoning traces that allow agents to better integrate search engines for complex query answering, while offering a data-efficient alternative to supervised process modeling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SubSearch：复杂检索中无监督引导推理的中间奖励机制
大语言模型本质具有概率性，在结合外部信息时表现更可靠。复杂查询常需对检索信息进行多步推理，且缺乏明确或预设的推理路径，这使其仍具挑战性。近期研究通过基于模型结果的强化学习训练模型，在提升复杂信息处理能力方面展现出潜力。本文提出SubSearch框架，将监督从仅关注结果转向通过中间奖励信号激励高质量推理规划。与以往依赖人工标注或大模型评判轨迹来训练独立奖励模型的方法不同，SubSearch直接利用内在过程奖励优化生成器——即通过内部衍生的奖励机制，无需外部监督，推动自主信息密集型推理发展。在七个基准测试上的实验表明，在问答和多跳问答数据集中，通过内在奖励激励中间推理步骤，比仅使用结果奖励能产生更稳健的推理轨迹。SubSearch有助于构建推理轨迹，使智能体能更有效地整合搜索引擎处理复杂查询，同时为监督式过程建模提供了数据高效的替代方案。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of enabling large language models to perform reliable multi-step reasoning for complex queries, where no predetermined reasoning path exists. It introduces SubSearch, a framework that shifts from outcome-only reinforcement learning to using intrinsic intermediate rewards to guide the reasoning process, eliminating the need for external supervision from human annotators or separate reward models. Experimental results on seven benchmarks demonstrate that this approach yields more robust reasoning traces in QA and multi-hop QA tasks compared to methods relying solely on outcome rewards, facilitating better integration with search engines for complex query answering.
本文针对大型语言模型在处理复杂查询时缺乏明确推理路径的挑战，提出了一种名为SubSearch的框架，旨在通过内在的中间奖励而非仅依赖结果奖励来引导多步推理过程，从而无需外部监督或单独奖励模型。该方法在七个基准测试上的实验表明，相较于仅使用结果奖励，引入中间推理步骤的奖励能在问答和多跳问答数据集中产生更稳健的推理轨迹，有助于智能体更好地结合搜索引擎回答复杂查询，同时为监督式过程建模提供了数据高效的替代方案。
Strategic Persuasion with Trait-Conditioned Multi-Agent Systems for Iterative Legal Argumentation
Authors: Philipp D. Siedler
First: 2026-04-08T12:46:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T12:46:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Strategic interaction in adversarial domains such as law, diplomacy, and negotiation is mediated by language, yet most game-theoretic models abstract away the mechanisms of persuasion that operate through discourse. We present the Strategic Courtroom Framework, a multi-agent simulation environment in which prosecution and defense teams composed of trait-conditioned Large Language Model (LLM) agents engage in iterative, round-based legal argumentation. Agents are instantiated using nine interpretable traits organized into four archetypes, enabling systematic control over rhetorical style and strategic orientation. We evaluate the framework across 10 synthetic legal cases and 84 three-trait team configurations, totaling over 7{,}000 simulated trials using DeepSeek-R1 and Gemini~2.5~Pro. Our results show that heterogeneous teams with complementary traits consistently outperform homogeneous configurations, that moderate interaction depth yields more stable verdicts, and that certain traits (notably quantitative and charismatic) contribute disproportionately to persuasive success. We further introduce a reinforcement-learning-based Trait Orchestrator that dynamically generates defense traits conditioned on the case and opposing team, discovering strategies that outperform static, human-designed trait combinations. Together, these findings demonstrate how language can be treated as a first-class strategic action space and provide a foundation for building autonomous agents capable of adaptive persuasion in multi-agent environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于特质条件多智能体系统的迭代法律论证策略性说服研究
在法律、外交和谈判等对抗性领域中，策略性互动通过语言媒介实现，然而多数博弈论模型忽略了通过话语运作的说服机制。本文提出战略法庭框架——一个多智能体仿真环境，其中由特质条件大语言模型智能体组成的控辩双方团队进行迭代式、回合制法律论证。智能体通过九个可解释特质（归为四种原型）实例化，实现对修辞风格与策略取向的系统控制。 我们在10个合成法律案例和84种三特质团队配置中评估该框架，使用DeepSeek-R1与Gemini~2.5~Pro模型累计模拟超过7,000场庭审。结果表明：具有互补特质的异构团队持续优于同质配置；适中的交互深度产生更稳定的判决；特定特质（尤其是量化型与魅力型）对说服成功贡献显著。我们进一步提出基于强化学习的特质编排器，能根据案件与对手团队动态生成辩护特质，其发现的策略优于静态人工设计的特质组合。 这些发现共同论证了如何将语言视为一级策略行动空间，并为构建能在多智能体环境中实现自适应说服的自主智能体奠定基础。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the gap between game-theoretic models and the linguistic mechanisms of persuasion in adversarial domains like law, this paper introduces the Strategic Courtroom Framework, a multi-agent simulation where prosecution and defense teams of trait-conditioned LLM agents engage in iterative legal argumentation. The method involves instantiating agents with nine interpretable traits organized into four archetypes to control rhetorical style and strategy, and evaluating the framework across 10 synthetic cases and 84 team configurations using models like DeepSeek-R1 and Gemini 2.5 Pro. Experimental results show that heterogeneous teams with complementary traits outperform homogeneous ones, moderate interaction depth leads to more stable verdicts, and traits like quantitative and charismatic significantly boost persuasive success; additionally, a reinforcement-learning-based Trait Orchestrator dynamically generates defense traits that surpass static human-designed combinations.
本文的动机在于弥补博弈论模型与法律等对抗性领域中语言说服机制之间的差距，提出了战略法庭框架，这是一个多智能体模拟环境，其中由特质条件化大语言模型智能体组成的控辩双方团队进行迭代式法律论证。方法上，通过九个可解释特质组织成四种原型来实例化智能体，以控制修辞风格和策略，并使用DeepSeek-R1和Gemini 2.5 Pro等模型，在10个合成案例和84种团队配置中评估该框架。实验结果表明，具有互补特质的异质团队表现优于同质团队，适中的交互深度能产生更稳定的判决，且定量和魅力等特质对说服成功贡献显著；此外，基于强化学习的特质编排器能动态生成针对案件和对手团队的防御特质，其策略优于静态人工设计的组合。
Predictive Representations for Skill Transfer in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ruben Vereecken, Luke Dickens, Alessandra Russo
First: 2026-04-08T12:35:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T12:35:24+00:00
Comments: esearch conducted: September 2018 to June 2021. This manuscript represents the work as of June 2021
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A key challenge in scaling up Reinforcement Learning is generalizing learned behaviour. Without the ability to carry forward acquired knowledge an agent is doomed to learn each task from scratch. In this paper we develop a new formalism for transfer by virtue of state abstraction. Based on task-independent, compact observations (outcomes) of the environment, we introduce Outcome-Predictive State Representations (OPSRs), agent-centered and task-independent abstractions that are made up of predictions of outcomes. We show formally and empirically that they have the potential for optimal but limited transfer, then overcome this trade-off by introducing OPSR-based skills, i.e. abstract actions (based on options) that can be reused between tasks as a result of state abstraction. In a series of empirical studies, we learn OPSR-based skills from demonstrations and show how they speed up learning considerably in entirely new and unseen tasks without any pre-processing. We believe that the framework introduced in this work is a promising step towards transfer in RL in general, and towards transfer through combining state and action abstraction specifically.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中基于预测表征的技能迁移方法
强化学习规模化应用的核心挑战在于学习行为的泛化能力。若智能体无法传承已获知识，则每项任务都需从零学起。本文通过状态抽象提出一种新的迁移学习形式化框架：基于环境任务无关的紧凑观测（结果），我们引入结果预测状态表征（OPSRs）——这种以智能体为中心、任务无关的抽象表征由结果预测构成。我们通过理论证明与实验验证，表明OPSRs具备有限但最优的迁移潜力，进而通过引入基于OPSR的技能（即基于选项的抽象动作）突破此限制。这些技能因状态抽象而能在任务间复用。在一系列实证研究中，我们通过演示学习获得基于OPSR的技能，并证明其能在未经预处理的全新任务中显著加速学习进程。本研究提出的框架为强化学习迁移领域，特别是结合状态与动作抽象的迁移路径，迈出了关键一步。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of knowledge transfer in reinforcement learning, where agents typically learn tasks from scratch. The authors propose Outcome-Predictive State Representations (OPSRs), which are task-independent abstractions based on predicting environmental outcomes, to enable limited optimal transfer. To overcome transfer limitations, they introduce OPSR-based skills as abstract actions derived from options, allowing reuse across tasks. Experimental results demonstrate that skills learned from demonstrations significantly accelerate learning in novel, unseen tasks without preprocessing, highlighting the framework's potential for combining state and action abstraction to improve transfer.
本文针对强化学习中知识迁移的挑战，即智能体通常需从零开始学习任务。作者提出了结果预测状态表示（OPSRs），这是一种基于环境结果预测的、与任务无关的抽象表示，以实现有限的最优迁移。为克服迁移限制，他们引入了基于OPSR的技能作为从选项中衍生的抽象动作，允许在任务间重用。实验结果表明，通过演示学习的技能能在无需预处理的情况下，显著加速在全新未见任务中的学习，凸显了该框架通过结合状态和动作抽象来改进迁移的潜力。
QNAS: A Neural Architecture Search Framework for Accurate and Efficient Quantum Neural Networks
Authors: Kooshan Maleki, Alberto Marchisio, Muhammad Shafique
First: 2026-04-08T12:34:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T12:34:01+00:00
Comments: To appear at the IEEE International Joint Conference on Neural Networks (IJCNN), Maastricht, The Netherlands, June 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing quantum neural networks (QNNs) that are both accurate and deployable on NISQ hardware is challenging. Handcrafted ansatze must balance expressivity, trainability, and resource use, while limited qubits often necessitate circuit cutting. Existing quantum architecture search methods primarily optimize accuracy while only heuristically controlling quantum and mostly ignore the exponential overhead of circuit cutting. We introduce QNAS, a neural architecture search framework that unifies hardware aware evaluation, multi objective optimization, and cutting overhead awareness for hybrid quantum classical neural networks (HQNNs). QNAS trains a shared parameter SuperCircuit and uses NSGA-II to optimize three objectives jointly: (i) validation error, (ii) a runtime cost proxy measuring wall clock evaluation time, and (iii) the estimated number of subcircuits under a target qubit budget. QNAS evaluates candidate HQNNs under a few epochs of training and discovers clear Pareto fronts that reveal tradeoffs between accuracy, efficiency, and cutting overhead. Across MNIST, Fashion-MNIST, and Iris benchmarks, we observe that embedding type and CNOT mode selection significantly impact both accuracy and efficiency, with angle-y embedding and sparse entangling patterns outperforming other configurations on image datasets, and amplitude embedding excelling on tabular data (Iris). On MNIST, the best architecture achieves 97.16% test accuracy with a compact 8 qubit, 2 layer circuit; on the more challenging Fashion-MNIST, 87.38% with a 5 qubit, 2 layer circuit; and on Iris, 100% validation accuracy with a 4 qubit, 2 layer circuit. QNAS surfaces these design insights automatically during search, guiding practitioners toward architectures that balance accuracy, resource efficiency, and practical deployability on current hardware.
中文标题/摘要
标题：QNAS：面向精确高效量子神经网络的神经架构搜索框架
设计兼具精确性且可部署于NISQ硬件的量子神经网络（QNN）具有挑战性。手工设计的拟设需平衡表达能力、可训练性与资源消耗，而有限量子比特常需电路切割。现有量子架构搜索方法主要优化精度，仅启发性控制量子资源，且大多忽略电路切割的指数级开销。我们提出QNAS——一种融合硬件感知评估、多目标优化与切割开销感知的神经架构搜索框架，适用于混合量子经典神经网络（HQNN）。QNAS训练共享参数的超级电路，采用NSGA-II联合优化三个目标：（i）验证误差；（ii）衡量实际评估时间的运行时成本代理；（iii）目标量子比特预算下的预估子电路数量。QNAS通过少量训练轮次评估候选HQNN，发现清晰的帕累托前沿，揭示精度、效率与切割开销间的权衡。在MNIST、Fashion-MNIST和Iris基准测试中，嵌入类型与CNOT模式选择显著影响精度与效率：角度-y嵌入与稀疏纠缠模式在图像数据集上表现优异，振幅嵌入在表格数据（Iris）中表现突出。在MNIST上，最佳架构以紧凑的8量子比特2层电路实现97.16%测试精度；在更具挑战的Fashion-MNIST上，以5量子比特2层电路实现87.38%精度；在Iris上以4量子比特2层电路达到100%验证精度。QNAS在搜索过程中自动揭示这些设计洞见，指导实践者构建平衡精度、资源效率与当前硬件实际可部署性的架构。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of designing quantum neural networks (QNNs) that are both accurate and deployable on noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) hardware, where handcrafted designs struggle to balance expressivity, trainability, and resource constraints, this paper introduces QNAS, a neural architecture search framework. The method unifies hardware-aware evaluation and multi-objective optimization by training a shared-parameter SuperCircuit and using NSGA-II to jointly optimize validation error, a runtime cost proxy, and the estimated number of subcircuits under a qubit budget, thereby explicitly accounting for the overhead of circuit cutting. Experimental results on MNIST, Fashion-MNIST, and Iris benchmarks reveal clear Pareto fronts, demonstrating trade-offs between accuracy, efficiency, and cutting overhead; specifically, the best architectures achieve 97.16% test accuracy on MNIST with an 8-qubit 2-layer circuit, 87.38% on Fashion-MNIST with a 5-qubit 2-layer circuit, and 100% validation accuracy on Iris with a 4-qubit 2-layer circuit, while automatically surfacing design insights such as the superiority of angle-y embedding for image data and amplitude embedding for tabular data.

EmoMAS: Emotion-Aware Multi-Agent System for High-Stakes Edge-Deployable Negotiation with Bayesian Orchestration
Authors: Yunbo Long, Yunhan Liu, Liming Xu
First: 2026-04-08T12:20:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T12:20:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) has been widely used for automated negotiation, but their high computational cost and privacy risks limit deployment in privacy-sensitive, on-device settings such as mobile assistants or rescue robots. Small language models (SLMs) offer a viable alternative, yet struggle with the complex emotional dynamics of high-stakes negotiation. We introduces EmoMAS, a Bayesian multi-agent framework that transforms emotional decision-making from reactive to strategic. EmoMAS leverages a Bayesian orchestrator to coordinate three specialized agents: game-theoretic, reinforcement learning, and psychological coherence models. The system fuses their real-time insights to optimize emotional state transitions while continuously updating agent reliability based on negotiation feedback. This mixture-of-agents architecture enables online strategy learning without pre-training. We further introduce four high-stakes, edge-deployable negotiation benchmarks across debt, healthcare, emergency response, and educational domains. Through extensive agent-to-agent simulations across all benchmarks, both SLMs and LLMs equipped with EmoMAS consistently surpass all baseline models in negotiation performance while balancing ethical behavior. These results show that strategic emotional intelligence is also the key driver of negotiation success. By treating emotional expression as a strategic variable within a Bayesian multi-agent optimization framework, EmoMAS establishes a new paradigm for effective, private, and adaptive negotiation AI suitable for high-stakes edge deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EmoMAS：面向高风险边缘可部署谈判的贝叶斯编排情感感知多智能体系统
大语言模型（LLMs）已广泛用于自动谈判，但其高计算成本和隐私风险限制了在移动助手或救援机器人等隐私敏感的端侧部署。小语言模型（SLMs）提供了可行替代方案，但难以应对高风险谈判中复杂的情感动态。本文提出EmoMAS，一种贝叶斯多智能体框架，将情感决策从被动反应转变为战略行为。EmoMAS利用贝叶斯编排器协调三个专业智能体：博弈论模型、强化学习模型和心理一致性模型。该系统融合其实时洞察以优化情感状态转换，同时根据谈判反馈持续更新智能体可靠性。这种混合智能体架构支持无需预训练的在线策略学习。我们进一步引入了债务、医疗、应急响应和教育领域的四个高风险边缘可部署谈判基准。通过跨所有基准的广泛智能体间模拟，搭载EmoMAS的SLMs和LLMs在平衡伦理行为的同时，谈判性能持续超越所有基线模型。结果表明战略情感智能同样是谈判成功的关键驱动因素。通过将情感表达作为贝叶斯多智能体优化框架中的战略变量，EmoMAS为适用于高风险边缘部署的高效、隐私安全且自适应的谈判AI建立了新范式。

The method employs a Bayesian orchestrator to coordinate three specialized agents—game-theoretic, reinforcement learning, and psychological coherence models—fusing their real-time insights to optimize emotional state transitions and update agent reliability online without pre-training. Reinforcement Learning with Reward Machines for Sleep Control in Mobile Networks
Authors: Kristina Levina, Nikolaos Pappas, Athanasios Karapantelakis, Aneta Vulgarakis Feljan, Jendrik Seipp
First: 2026-04-08T12:17:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T12:17:43+00:00
Comments: Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Energy efficiency in mobile networks is crucial for sustainable telecommunications infrastructure, particularly as network densification continues to increase power consumption. Sleep mechanisms for the components in mobile networks can reduce energy use, but deciding which components to put to sleep, when, and for how long while preserving quality of service (QoS) remains a difficult optimisation problem. In this paper, we utilise reinforcement learning with reward machines (RMs) to make sleep-control decisions that balance immediate energy savings and long-term QoS impact, i.e. time-averaged packet drop rates for deadline-constrained traffic and time-averaged minimum-throughput guarantees for constant-rate users. A challenge is that time-averaged constraints depend on cumulative performance over time rather than immediate performance. As a result, the effective reward is non-Markovian, and optimal actions depend on operational history rather than the instantaneous system state. RMs account for the history dependence by maintaining an abstract state that explicitly tracks the QoS constraint violations over time. Our framework provides a principled, scalable approach to energy management for next-generation mobile networks under diverse traffic patterns and QoS requirements.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于奖励机的强化学习在移动网络休眠控制中的应用
移动网络的能效对可持续电信基础设施至关重要，尤其在网络密集化持续推高能耗的背景下。网络组件的休眠机制可降低能耗，但如何在保障服务质量（QoS）的前提下，确定休眠组件、时机及时长仍属复杂优化问题。本文采用奖励机（RM）增强的强化学习方法，制定兼顾即时节能与长期QoS影响的休眠控制决策——具体针对时限敏感业务的时均丢包率与恒定速率用户的时均最低吞吐量保障。核心挑战在于时均约束依赖于长期累积性能而非即时表现，导致有效奖励呈非马尔可夫性，最优动作需依据运行历史而非瞬时系统状态。奖励机通过维护抽象状态显式追踪QoS约束的历时违反情况，以处理历史依赖性。本框架为多样化业务模式与QoS要求下的新一代移动网络，提供了原则性、可扩展的能源管理方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of optimizing energy efficiency in mobile networks through sleep control mechanisms, motivated by the need to reduce power consumption while maintaining quality of service (QoS) under diverse traffic patterns. The method employs reinforcement learning with reward machines (RMs) to handle non-Markovian rewards arising from time-averaged QoS constraints, such as packet drop rates and throughput guarantees, by using an abstract state to track historical constraint violations. Experimental results demonstrate that this framework effectively balances immediate energy savings with long-term QoS impact, offering a scalable solution for energy management in next-generation networks.
本文针对移动网络中通过休眠控制优化能源效率的挑战，动机是在多样化流量模式下降低功耗的同时保持服务质量（QoS）。方法采用奖励机增强的强化学习，通过抽象状态跟踪历史约束违规，以处理由时间平均QoS约束（如丢包率和吞吐量保证）引起的非马尔可夫奖励。实验结果表明，该框架能有效平衡即时节能与长期QoS影响，为下一代网络的能源管理提供了可扩展的解决方案。
Exploring Natural Language-Based Strategies for Efficient Number Learning in Children through Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tirthankar Mittra
First: 2024-10-10T19:49:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T11:56:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we build a reinforcement learning framework to study how children compose numbers using base-ten blocks. Studying numerical cognition in toddlers offers a powerful window into the learning process itself, because numbers sit at the intersection of language, logic, perception, and culture. Specifically, we utilize state of the art (SOTA) reinforcement learning algorithms and neural network architectures to understand how variations in linguistic instructions can affect the learning process. Our results also show that instructions providing explicit action guidance are a more effective learning signal for RL agents to construct numbers. Furthermore, we identify an effective curriculum for ordering numerical-composition examples during training, resulting in faster convergence and improved generalization to unseen data. These findings highlight the role of language and multi-modal signals in numerical cognition and provide hypotheses for designing effective instructional strategies for early childhood education.
中文标题/摘要
标题：探索基于自然语言的强化学习策略促进儿童高效数字学习
本文构建了一个强化学习框架，研究儿童如何利用十进制积木组合数字。研究幼儿的数字认知为理解学习过程本身提供了重要窗口，因为数字处于语言、逻辑、感知与文化的交汇点。具体而言，我们采用最先进的强化学习算法与神经网络架构，探究语言指令的差异如何影响学习过程。结果表明，提供明确行动指导的指令能更有效地引导强化学习智能体构建数字。此外，我们设计了一种有效的课程安排方法，用于在训练过程中排序数字组合示例，从而加速模型收敛并提升对未见数据的泛化能力。这些发现凸显了语言与多模态信号在数字认知中的作用，并为设计有效的早期教育指导策略提供了理论依据。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to understand how children learn numerical concepts through language and multi-modal interaction, this paper develops a reinforcement learning framework that simulates number composition using base-ten blocks. The method employs state-of-the-art reinforcement learning algorithms and neural networks to analyze how different linguistic instructions influence learning efficiency. Experimental results demonstrate that explicit action guidance in instructions serves as a more effective learning signal, and an optimized curriculum for ordering examples accelerates convergence and enhances generalization to unseen data, offering insights for designing educational strategies in early childhood.
本研究旨在探索儿童如何通过语言和多模态交互学习数字概念，为此构建了一个强化学习框架，模拟使用十进制积木进行数字组合的过程。方法采用先进的强化学习算法和神经网络架构，分析不同语言指令对学习效率的影响。实验结果表明，提供明确行动指导的指令能更有效地促进强化学习代理的数字构建能力，同时通过优化训练中数字组合示例的顺序课程，实现了更快的收敛速度和更好的泛化性能，为早期教育中的教学策略设计提供了理论依据。
Block-Bench: A Framework for Controllable and Transparent Discrete Optimization Benchmarking
Authors: Furong Ye, Frank Neumann, Thomas Bäck, Niki van Stein
First: 2026-04-08T11:44:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T11:44:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a novel approach for constructing discrete optimization benchmarks that enables fine-grained control over problem properties, and such benchmarks can facilitate analyzing discrete algorithm behaviors. We build benchmark problems based on a set of block functions, where each block function maps a subset of variables to a real value. Problems are instantiated through a set of block functions, weight factors, and an adjacency graph representing the dependency among the block functions. Through analyzing intermediate block values, our framework allows to analyze algorithm behavior not only in the objective space but also at the level of variable representations in the obtained solutions. This capacity is particularly useful for analyzing discrete heuristics in large-scale multi-modal problems, thereby enhancing the practical relevance of benchmark studies. We demonstrate how the proposed approach can inspire the related work in self-adaptation and diversity control in evolutionary algorithms. Moreover, we explain that the proposed benchmark design enables explicit control over problem properties, supporting research in broader domains such as dynamic algorithm configuration and multi-objective optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Block-Bench：一种可控且透明的离散优化基准测试框架
我们提出了一种构建离散优化基准的新方法，能够对问题属性进行细粒度控制，此类基准有助于分析离散算法的行为。我们基于一组块函数构建基准问题，每个块函数将变量子集映射为实数值。问题通过一组块函数、权重因子以及表示块函数间依赖关系的邻接图来实例化。通过分析中间块值，我们的框架不仅能在目标空间分析算法行为，还能在所得解的变量表示层面进行分析。这种能力对于分析大规模多模态问题中的离散启发式算法尤为有用，从而增强了基准研究的实际相关性。我们展示了所提方法如何启发进化算法中自适应和多样性控制的相关研究。此外，我们解释了所提出的基准设计能够显式控制问题属性，支持更广泛领域的研究，如动态算法配置和多目标优化。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Block-Bench, a framework designed to create transparent and controllable benchmarks for discrete optimization, motivated by the need to better analyze algorithm behaviors through fine-grained control over problem properties. The method constructs benchmark problems using block functions that map subsets of variables to real values, combined with weight factors and an adjacency graph to define dependencies, allowing detailed analysis of both objective space and variable-level solution representations. Experimental results demonstrate its utility in analyzing discrete heuristics for large-scale multi-modal problems, inspiring applications in self-adaptation, diversity control in evolutionary algorithms, and broader domains like dynamic algorithm configuration and multi-objective optimization.
