LongWriter-Zero: Mastering Ultra-Long Text Generation via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yuhao Wu, Yushi Bai, Zhiqiang Hu, Roy Ka-Wei Lee, Juanzi Li
Venue: ICLR 2026 Oral
First: 2025-06-23T16:59:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T11:33:52+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026 Oral
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Ultra-long generation by large language models (LLMs) is a widely demanded scenario, yet it remains a significant challenge due to their maximum generation length limit and overall quality degradation as sequence length increases. Previous approaches, exemplified by LongWriter, typically rely on ''teaching'', which involves supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on synthetic long-form outputs. However, this strategy heavily depends on synthetic SFT data, which is difficult and costly to construct, often lacks coherence and consistency, and tends to be overly artificial and structurally monotonous. In this work, we propose an incentivization-based approach that, starting entirely from scratch and without relying on any annotated or synthetic data, leverages reinforcement learning (RL) to foster the emergence of ultra-long, high-quality text generation capabilities in LLMs. We perform RL training starting from a base model, similar to R1-Zero, guiding it to engage in reasoning that facilitates planning and refinement during the writing process. To support this, we employ specialized reward models that steer the LLM towards improved length control, writing quality, and structural formatting. Experimental evaluations show that our LongWriter-Zero model, trained from Qwen2.5-32B, consistently outperforms traditional SFT methods on long-form writing tasks, achieving state-of-the-art results across all metrics on WritingBench and Arena-Write, and even surpassing 100B+ models such as DeepSeek R1 and Qwen3-235B. We open-source our data and model checkpoints under https://huggingface.co/THU-KEG/LongWriter-Zero-32B
中文标题/摘要
标题：LongWriter-Zero：通过强化学习掌握超长文本生成
大语言模型（LLMs）的超长文本生成是广泛需求的场景，但由于其最大生成长度限制以及随着序列长度增加导致的整体质量下降，这仍然是一个重大挑战。先前以LongWriter为代表的方法通常依赖“教学”策略，即在合成的长文本输出上进行监督微调（SFT）。然而，该策略严重依赖合成的SFT数据，这类数据构建困难且成本高昂，往往缺乏连贯性和一致性，并容易显得过于人工化、结构单调。本研究提出一种基于激励的方法，完全从零开始、不依赖任何标注或合成数据，利用强化学习（RL）在LLMs中培育超长高质量文本生成能力。我们从基础模型出发进行RL训练（类似R1-Zero），引导模型在写作过程中进行促进规划与优化的推理。为此，我们采用专门设计的奖励模型，引导LLM在长度控制、写作质量和结构格式方面持续改进。实验评估表明，基于Qwen2.5-32B训练的LongWriter-Zero模型在长文本写作任务上持续超越传统SFT方法，在WritingBench和Arena-Write的所有指标上均达到最先进水平，甚至超越DeepSeek R1、Qwen3-235B等百亿参数模型。我们已在https://huggingface.co/THU-KEG/LongWriter-Zero-32B开源数据与模型检查点。

A First Guess is Rarely the Final Answer: Learning to Search in the Travelling Salesperson Problem
Authors: Andoni Irazusta Garmendia
First: 2026-04-08T11:04:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T11:04:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Most neural solvers for the Traveling Salesperson Problem (TSP) are trained to output a single solution, even though practitioners rarely stop there: at test time, they routinely spend extra compute on sampling or post-hoc search. This raises a natural question: can the search procedure itself be learned? Neural improvement methods take this perspective by learning a policy that applies local modifications to a candidate solution, accumulating gains over an improvement trajectory. Yet learned improvement for TSP remains comparatively immature, with existing methods still falling short of robust, scalable performance. We argue that a key reason is design mismatch: many approaches reuse state representations, architectural choices, and training recipes inherited from single-solution methods, rather than being built around the mechanics of local search. This mismatch motivates NICO-TSP (Neural Improvement for Combinatorial Optimization): a 2-opt improvement framework for TSP. NICO-TSP represents the current tour with exactly $n$ edge tokens aligned with the neighborhood operator, scores 2-opt moves directly without tour positional encodings, and trains via a two-stage procedure: imitation learning to short-horizon optimal trajectories, followed by critic-free group-based reinforcement learning over longer rollouts. Under compute-matched evaluations that measure improvement as a function of both search steps and wall-clock time, NICO-TSP delivers consistently stronger and markedly more step-efficient improvement than prior learned and heuristic search baselines, generalizes far more reliably to larger out-of-distribution instances, and serves both as a competitive replacement for classical local search and as a powerful test-time refinement module for constructive solvers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：首次猜测鲜为最终答案：学习在旅行商问题中进行搜索
大多数针对旅行商问题（TSP）的神经求解器被训练为输出单一解，然而实践者很少止步于此：在测试阶段，他们通常会投入额外计算资源进行采样或事后搜索。这引出一个自然问题：搜索过程本身能否被学习？神经改进方法正是基于这一视角，通过学习一个对候选解施加局部修改的策略，在改进轨迹中累积收益。但针对TSP的学习式改进方法仍相对不成熟，现有方法在鲁棒性和可扩展性能方面仍有不足。我们认为关键原因在于设计错配：许多方法沿用了单解方法的状态表示、架构选择和训练方案，而非围绕局部搜索机制构建。这种错配催生了NICO-TSP（组合优化神经改进框架）：一种针对TSP的2-opt改进框架。NICO-TSP通过精确对齐邻域算子的n个边令牌表示当前路径，无需路径位置编码直接评估2-opt操作，并采用两阶段训练：先通过模仿学习获得短视界最优轨迹，再通过无评论员的分组强化学习进行长序列推演。在衡量搜索步数与实际耗时函数的计算匹配评估中，NICO-TSP相比先前学习式和启发式搜索基线，展现出持续更强且显著更高效的改进性能，对更大规模分布外实例具有更可靠的泛化能力，既可替代经典局部搜索作为竞争性方案，也能作为构造性求解器的高效测试时优化模块。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the observation that neural solvers for the Traveling Salesperson Problem (TSP) typically output a single solution while practitioners often perform additional search, this paper investigates whether the search process itself can be learned. The method introduces NICO-TSP, a neural improvement framework designed specifically for local search mechanics, which represents tours with edge tokens aligned to the 2-opt neighborhood operator, scores moves directly, and employs a two-stage training procedure combining imitation learning and group-based reinforcement learning. Experimental results show that NICO-TSP achieves stronger, more step-efficient improvement than prior learned and heuristic baselines, generalizes better to larger out-of-distribution instances, and effectively serves as both a standalone local search method and a refinement module for constructive solvers.

Not All Tokens See Equally: Perception-Grounded Policy Optimization for Large Vision-Language Models
Authors: Zekai Ye, Qiming Li, Xiaocheng Feng, Ruihan Chen, Ziming Li, Haoyu Ren, Kun Chen, Dandan Tu, Bing Qin
First: 2026-04-02T09:53:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T10:48:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has advanced reasoning in Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs), prevailing frameworks suffer from a foundational methodological flaw: by distributing identical advantages across all generated tokens, these methods inherently dilute the learning signals essential for optimizing the critical, visually-grounded steps of multimodal reasoning. To bridge this gap, we formulate \textit{Token Visual Dependency}, quantifying the causal information gain of visual inputs via the Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence between visual-conditioned and text-only predictive distributions. Revealing that this dependency is highly sparse and semantically pivotal, we introduce Perception-Grounded Policy Optimization (PGPO), which is a novel fine-grained credit assignment framework that dynamically reshapes advantages at the token level. Through a threshold-gated, mass-conserving mechanism, PGPO actively amplifies learning signals for visually-dependent tokens while suppressing gradient noise from linguistic priors. Extensive experiments based on the Qwen2.5-VL series across seven challenging multimodal reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PGPO boosts models by 18.7% on average. Both theoretical and empirical analyses confirm that PGPO effectively reduces gradient variance, prevents training collapse, and acts as a potent regularizer for robust, perception-grounded multimodal reasoning. Code will be released on https://github.com/Yzk1114/PGPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：非等视之符：面向大型视觉语言模型的感知驱动策略优化
尽管可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）推动了大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）的推理能力，现有框架仍存在根本性方法缺陷：通过在所有生成词符上分配相同的优势值，这些方法本质上稀释了优化多模态推理关键视觉基础步骤所需的学习信号。为弥合此差距，我们提出\textit{词符视觉依赖度}，通过视觉条件预测分布与纯文本预测分布间的KL散度量化视觉输入的因果信息增益。研究发现该依赖度具有高度稀疏性和语义关键性，据此提出感知驱动策略优化（PGPO）——一种新颖的细粒度信用分配框架，能在词符层面动态重塑优势值。通过阈值门控的质量守恒机制，PGPO主动增强视觉依赖词符的学习信号，同时抑制语言先验的梯度噪声。基于Qwen2.5-VL系列模型在七个挑战性多模态推理基准上的大量实验表明，PGPO平均提升模型性能18.7%。理论与实证分析共同证实，PGPO能有效降低梯度方差、防止训练崩溃，并作为鲁棒的感知驱动多模态推理的强效正则化器。代码将在https://github.com/Yzk1114/PGPO发布。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses a flaw in existing Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods for Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs), where uniformly distributing learning signals across all tokens dilutes the optimization of visually-grounded reasoning steps. The authors propose a novel method, Perception-Grounded Policy Optimization (PGPO), which introduces Token Visual Dependency to quantify the causal information gain from visual inputs using KL divergence, revealing its sparse and pivotal nature. PGPO dynamically reshapes token-level advantages via a threshold-gated mechanism, amplifying signals for visually-dependent tokens while suppressing noise from linguistic priors. Experimental results on the Qwen2.5-VL series across seven benchmarks show an average performance boost of 18.7%, with analyses confirming that PGPO reduces gradient variance, prevents training collapse, and acts as a robust regularizer for perception-grounded reasoning.
本文针对大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）中基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法的一个缺陷展开研究，即现有方法对所有生成令牌均匀分配学习信号，从而稀释了对视觉基础推理关键步骤的优化。作者提出了一种新方法——感知基础策略优化（PGPO），该方法通过引入令牌视觉依赖性，利用KL散度量化视觉输入的因果信息增益，揭示了其稀疏性和关键性。PGPO通过一个阈值门控机制动态重塑令牌级优势，放大视觉依赖令牌的学习信号，同时抑制来自语言先验的梯度噪声。在Qwen2.5-VL系列模型上对七个具有挑战性的多模态推理基准进行的实验表明，PGPO平均提升了18.7%的性能，分析证实该方法能有效降低梯度方差、防止训练崩溃，并作为感知基础多模态推理的强正则化器。
FP4 Explore, BF16 Train: Diffusion Reinforcement Learning via Efficient Rollout Scaling
Authors: Yitong Li, Junsong Chen, Shuchen Xue, Pengcuo Zeren, Siyuan Fu, Dinghao Yang, Yangyang Tang, Junjie Bai, Ping Luo, Song Han, Enze Xie
First: 2026-04-08T10:14:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T10:14:47+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement-Learning-based post-training has recently emerged as a promising paradigm for aligning text-to-image diffusion models with human preferences. In recent studies, increasing the rollout group size yields pronounced performance improvements, indicating substantial room for further alignment gains. However, scaling rollouts on large-scale foundational diffusion models (e.g., FLUX.1-12B) imposes a heavy computational burden. To alleviate this bottleneck, we explore the integration of FP4 quantization into Diffusion RL rollouts. Yet, we identify that naive quantized pipelines inherently introduce risks of performance degradation. To overcome this dilemma between efficiency and training integrity, we propose Sol-RL (Speed-of-light RL), a novel FP4-empowered Two-stage Reinforcement Learning framework. First, we utilize high-throughput NVFP4 rollouts to generate a massive candidate pool and extract a highly contrastive subset. Second, we regenerate these selected samples in BF16 precision and optimize the policy exclusively on them. By decoupling candidate exploration from policy optimization, Sol-RL integrates the algorithmic mechanisms of rollout scaling with the system-level throughput gains of NVFP4. This synergistic algorithm-hardware design effectively accelerates the rollout phase while reserving high-fidelity samples for optimization. We empirically demonstrate that our framework maintains the training integrity of BF16 precision pipeline while fully exploiting the throughput gains enabled by FP4 arithmetic. Extensive experiments across SANA, FLUX.1, and SD3.5-L substantiate that our approach delivers superior alignment performance across multiple metrics while accelerating training convergence by up to $4.64\times$, unlocking the power of massive rollout scaling at a fraction of the cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FP4探索、BF16训练：基于高效推演扩展的扩散强化学习
基于强化学习的后训练已成为将文生图扩散模型与人类偏好对齐的重要范式。近期研究表明，扩大推演组规模能显著提升性能，表明对齐效果仍有巨大提升空间。然而，在大型基础扩散模型（如FLUX.1-12B）上扩展推演会带来沉重计算负担。为缓解这一瓶颈，我们探索将FP4量化技术整合到扩散强化学习推演中，但发现原始量化流程会引入性能退化风险。为解决效率与训练完整性之间的矛盾，我们提出Sol-RL（光速强化学习）——一种创新的FP4增强型两阶段强化学习框架：第一阶段利用高吞吐量NVFP4推演生成海量候选池并提取高对比度子集；第二阶段以BF16精度重新生成选定样本并仅基于这些样本优化策略。通过解耦候选探索与策略优化，Sol-RL将推演扩展的算法机制与NVFP4的系统级吞吐增益相结合。这种算法-硬件协同设计在加速推演阶段的同时，为优化保留了高保真样本。实验证明，该框架在保持BF16精度训练完整性的同时，充分发挥了FP4运算的吞吐优势。在SANA、FLUX.1和SD3.5-L上的大量实验表明，本方法在多项指标上均实现更优的对齐性能，训练收敛速度最高提升4.64倍，以极低成本释放了大规模推演扩展的潜力。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the high computational cost of scaling reinforcement learning rollouts for aligning large text-to-image diffusion models with human preferences, which is necessary for performance gains but burdensome with models like FLUX.1-12B. The method proposed, Sol-RL, is a two-stage framework that first uses efficient FP4 quantization for high-throughput rollout exploration to generate a large candidate pool and extract a contrastive subset, then regenerates selected samples in BF16 precision for policy optimization, decoupling exploration from optimization to integrate algorithmic scaling with hardware throughput gains. The main experimental results show that this approach maintains training integrity comparable to BF16 pipelines while accelerating training convergence by up to 4.64 times and delivering superior alignment performance across multiple metrics on models such as SANA, FLUX.1, and SD3.5-L, enabling massive rollout scaling at reduced cost.
本研究的动机是解决在将大型文本到图像扩散模型与人类偏好对齐时，强化学习rollout扩展带来的高计算成本问题，这对于性能提升至关重要，但在FLUX.1-12B等模型上计算负担沉重。提出的方法Sol-RL是一个两阶段框架：首先利用高效的FP4量化进行高吞吐量rollout探索，生成大量候选样本并提取高对比度子集；然后在BF16精度下重新生成选定样本进行策略优化，将探索与优化解耦，以整合算法扩展与硬件吞吐增益。主要实验结果表明，该方法在保持与BF16流程相当的训练完整性的同时，将训练收敛速度提升高达4.64倍，并在SANA、FLUX.1和SD3.5-L等模型上实现了多指标对齐性能的优越表现，从而以较低成本实现了大规模rollout扩展。
Equivariant Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning for Multimodal Vehicle-to-Infrastructure Systems
Authors: Charbel Bou Chaaya, Mehdi Bennis
First: 2026-04-08T10:13:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T10:13:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we study a vehicle-to-infrastructure (V2I) system where distributed base stations (BSs) acting as road-side units (RSUs) collect multimodal (wireless and visual) data from moving vehicles. We consider a decentralized rate maximization problem, where each RSU relies on its local observations to optimize its resources, while all RSUs must collaborate to guarantee favorable network performance. We recast this problem as a distributed multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) problem, by incorporating rotation symmetries in terms of vehicles' locations. To exploit these symmetries, we propose a novel self-supervised learning framework where each BS agent aligns the latent features of its multimodal observation to extract the positions of the vehicles in its local region. Equipped with this sensing data at each RSU, we train an equivariant policy network using a graph neural network (GNN) with message passing layers, such that each agent computes its policy locally, while all agents coordinate their policies via a signaling scheme that overcomes partial observability and guarantees the equivariance of the global policy. We present numerical results carried out in a simulation environment, where ray-tracing and computer graphics are used to collect wireless and visual data. Results show the generalizability of our self-supervised and multimodal sensing approach, achieving more than two-fold accuracy gains over baselines, and the efficiency of our equivariant MARL training, attaining more than 50% performance gains over standard approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向多模态车路协同系统的等变多智能体强化学习
本文研究一种车路协同系统，其中分布式基站作为路侧单元从移动车辆收集无线与视觉多模态数据。我们考虑一个去中心化的速率最大化问题：每个路侧单元依赖本地观测优化资源分配，同时所有单元需协作保障网络性能。通过引入车辆位置的旋转对称性，我们将该问题重构为分布式多智能体强化学习问题。为利用对称性，提出一种新型自监督学习框架，使每个基站智能体对齐多模态观测的隐特征以提取局部区域内车辆位置。基于各单元感知数据，采用带消息传递层的图神经网络训练等变策略网络，使各智能体本地计算策略，并通过信号传递方案协调策略以克服部分可观测性并保证全局策略的等变性。在仿真环境中进行的数值实验结合射线追踪与计算机图形技术采集无线和视觉数据，结果表明：自监督多模态感知方法较基线实现两倍以上精度提升，等变多智能体强化学习训练较标准方法获得超50%的性能增益。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the decentralized resource optimization problem in vehicle-to-infrastructure (V2I) systems, where base stations (RSUs) must coordinate using multimodal data to maximize network rates despite partial observability. The method introduces a self-supervised learning framework for aligning multimodal features to extract vehicle positions, combined with an equivariant multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) approach using graph neural networks (GNNs) and message passing to ensure policy symmetry with respect to vehicle location rotations. Experimental simulations with ray-tracing and computer graphics demonstrate that the proposed approach generalizes effectively, yielding over two-fold accuracy improvements in sensing and more than 50% performance gains in MARL compared to baseline methods.

Self-Distilled RLVR
Authors: Chenxu Yang, Chuanyu Qin, Qingyi Si, Minghui Chen, Naibin Gu, Dingyu Yao, Zheng Lin, Weiping Wang, Jiaqi Wang, Nan Duan
First: 2026-04-03T15:50:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T08:22:36+00:00
Comments: Work in progress
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
On-policy distillation (OPD) has become a popular training paradigm in the LLM community. This paradigm selects a larger model as the teacher to provide dense, fine-grained signals for each sampled trajectory, in contrast to reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), which only obtains sparse signals from verifiable outcomes in the environment. Recently, the community has explored on-policy self-distillation (OPSD), where the same model serves as both teacher and student, with the teacher receiving additional privileged information such as reference answers to enable self-evolution. This paper demonstrates that learning signals solely derived from the privileged teacher result in severe information leakage and unstable long-term training. Accordingly, we identify the optimal niche for self-distillation and propose \textbf{RLSD} (\textbf{RL}VR with \textbf{S}elf-\textbf{D}istillation). Specifically, we leverage self-distillation to obtain token-level policy differences for determining fine-grained update magnitudes, while continuing to use RLVR to derive reliable update directions from environmental feedback (e.g., response correctness). This enables RLSD to simultaneously harness the strengths of both RLVR and OPSD, achieving a higher convergence ceiling and superior training stability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自蒸馏RLVR
在策略蒸馏已成为大语言模型领域流行的训练范式。该范式选取较大模型作为教师，为每个采样轨迹提供密集细粒度信号；而可验证奖励强化学习仅能从环境中的可验证结果获取稀疏信号。近期学界探索了在策略自蒸馏范式，即同一模型同时担任教师与学生角色，教师端通过获取参考答案等特权信息实现自我演进。本文论证仅从特权教师端获取的学习信号会导致严重信息泄露与长期训练不稳定。据此，我们界定了自蒸馏的最佳适用场景，提出\textbf{RLSD}（\textbf{可验证奖励强化学习}结合\textbf{自}我\textbf{蒸}馏）。具体而言，我们利用自蒸馏获取词元级策略差异以确定细粒度更新幅度，同时持续采用可验证奖励强化学习从环境反馈（如响应正确性）推导可靠更新方向。这使得RLSD能同时融合可验证奖励强化学习与在策略自蒸馏的优势，实现更高的收敛上限与卓越的训练稳定性。
Summary / 总结
This work addresses limitations in on-policy self-distillation (OPSD) for language models, where using a teacher model with privileged information leads to information leakage and unstable training. The proposed method, RLSD, integrates self-distillation with reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) by using self-distillation to calculate token-level update magnitudes while relying on RLVR's sparse environmental feedback, such as answer correctness, to determine reliable update directions. Experimental results demonstrate that this hybrid approach achieves higher convergence performance and superior training stability compared to using either technique alone.
本研究针对语言模型在策略自蒸馏中因教师模型使用特权信息导致信息泄露和训练不稳定的问题，提出了RLSD方法。该方法将自蒸馏与基于可验证奖励的强化学习相结合，利用自蒸馏计算细粒度的令牌级更新幅度，同时依赖强化学习从环境反馈（如答案正确性）中获得可靠的更新方向。实验结果表明，这种混合方法相比单独使用任一技术，能实现更高的收敛性能和更优的训练稳定性。
REVEAL: Reasoning-Enhanced Forensic Evidence Analysis for Explainable AI-Generated Image Detection
Authors: Huangsen Cao, Qin Mei, Zhiheng Li, Yuxi Li, Zhan Meng, Ying Zhang, Chen Li, Zhimeng Zhang, Xin Ding, Yongwei Wang, Jing Lyu, Fei Wu
First: 2025-11-28T13:11:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T07:23:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid progress of visual generative models has made AI-generated images increasingly difficult to distinguish from authentic ones, posing growing risks to social trust and information integrity. This motivates detectors that are not only accurate but also forensically explainable. While recent multimodal approaches improve interpretability, many rely on post-hoc rationalizations or coarse visual cues, without constructing verifiable chains of evidence, thus often leading to poor generalization. We introduce REVEAL-Bench, a reasoning-enhanced multimodal benchmark for AI-generated image forensics, structured around explicit chains of forensic evidence derived from lightweight expert models and consolidated into step-by-step chain-of-evidence traces. Based on this benchmark, we propose REVEAL (\underline{R}easoning-\underline{e}nhanced Forensic E\underline{v}id\underline{e}nce \underline{A}na\underline{l}ysis), an explainable forensic framework trained with expert-grounded reinforcement learning. Our reward design jointly promotes detection accuracy, evidence-grounded reasoning stability, and explanation faithfulness. Extensive experiments demonstrate significantly improved cross-domain generalization and more faithful explanations to baseline detectors. All data and codes will be released.
中文标题/摘要
标题：REVEAL：面向可解释AI生成图像检测的推理增强式法证证据分析
视觉生成模型的快速发展使得AI生成图像与真实图像越来越难以区分，对社会信任和信息完整性构成日益增长的风险。这促使检测器不仅需要高精度，还需具备法证可解释性。尽管近期多模态方法提升了可解释性，但许多方法依赖事后合理化或粗略视觉线索，未能构建可验证的证据链，导致泛化能力普遍不足。我们提出了REVEAL-Bench——一个面向AI生成图像法证分析的推理增强多模态基准，其围绕轻量级专家模型提取的显式法证证据链构建，并整合为逐步递进的证据链追踪框架。基于此基准，我们提出REVEAL（推理增强式法证证据分析），这是一个通过专家引导强化学习训练的可解释法证框架。我们的奖励机制协同提升检测精度、证据驱动推理稳定性与解释忠实度。大量实验表明，该方法显著提升了跨域泛化能力，并为基线检测器提供了更可信的解释。所有数据与代码将公开。

Motivated by the increasing difficulty of distinguishing AI-generated images from authentic ones and the need for forensically explainable detectors, this paper introduces REVEAL, a reasoning-enhanced forensic evidence analysis framework. The method constructs a benchmark with explicit chains of forensic evidence from expert models and trains REVEAL using expert-grounded reinforcement learning to jointly optimize detection accuracy, reasoning stability, and explanation faithfulness. Experimental results show that REVEAL achieves significantly improved cross-domain generalization and produces more faithful explanations compared to baseline detectors.

JoyAI-LLM Flash: Advancing Mid-Scale LLMs with Token Efficiency
Authors: Aichen Cai, Anmeng Zhang, Anyu Li, Bo Zhang, Bohua Cai, Chang Li, Changjian Jiang, Changkai Lu, Chao Xue, Chaocai Liang, Cheng Zhang, Dongkai Liu, Fei Wang, Guoqiang Huang, Haijian Ke, Han Lin, Hao Wang, Ji Miao, Jiacheng Zhang, Jialong Shi, Jifeng Zhu, Jingjing Qian, Junhui Luo, Junwu Xiong, Lam So, Liang Huang, Ming Ke, Mingyang Li, Panfeng Shi, Peng Hao, Qi Wang, Qian Lai, Qiaoqiao Yuan, Qingyu Yin, Qiong Cao, Qixiang Wang, Rongcheng Bian, Rongduo Han, Shaoqiang Zheng, Shi Hu, Shi Suo, Shijie Ren, Shijin Zhang, Shiying Fan, Shuai Xie, Tianyi Zhang, Wei Liu, Wentao Tan, Xianghan Meng, Xiaodong He, Xing Pan, Xiran Wang, Xuyang Peng, Ya Zhang, Yang Liu, Yangyang Duan, Yanxu Chen, Yicheng Gong, Yidan Huang, Yifei Liu, Yinhao Bai, Yongqiang Liu, Yuesong Zhang, Yuqi Zhang, Zerui Xie, Zhenfang Wang, Zhennan Shen, Zheyuan Liu, Zhuwei Zeng
First: 2026-04-03T13:52:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T07:22:54+00:00
Comments: Xiaodong He is the corresponding author
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce JoyAI-LLM Flash, an efficient Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) language model designed to redefine the trade-off between strong performance and token efficiency in the sub-50B parameter regime. JoyAI-LLM Flash is pretrained on a massive corpus of 20 trillion tokens and further optimized through a rigorous post-training pipeline, including supervised fine-tuning (SFT), Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), and large-scale reinforcement learning (RL) across diverse environments. To improve token efficiency, JoyAI-LLM Flash strategically balances \emph{thinking} and \emph{non-thinking} cognitive modes and introduces FiberPO, a novel RL algorithm inspired by fibration theory that decomposes trust-region maintenance into global and local components, providing unified multi-scale stability control for LLM policy optimization. To enhance architectural sparsity, the model comprises 48B total parameters while activating only 2.7B parameters per forward pass, achieving a substantially higher sparsity ratio than contemporary industry leading models of comparable scale. To further improve inference throughput, we adopt a joint training-inference co-design that incorporates dense Multi-Token Prediction (MTP) and Quantization-Aware Training (QAT). We release the checkpoints for both JoyAI-LLM-48B-A3B Base and its post-trained variants on Hugging Face to support the open-source community.
中文标题/摘要
标题：JoyAI-LLM Flash：通过令牌效率推进中等规模大语言模型发展
我们推出JoyAI-LLM Flash，这是一款高效的专家混合语言模型，旨在重新定义50B参数规模以下模型中强大性能与令牌效率之间的权衡。该模型基于20万亿令牌的大规模语料库进行预训练，并通过严格的训练后流程进一步优化，包括监督微调、直接偏好优化以及跨多样化环境的大规模强化学习。为提升令牌效率，JoyAI-LLM Flash策略性地平衡“思考”与“非思考”认知模式，并引入受纤维化理论启发的新型强化学习算法FiberPO——该算法将信任域维护分解为全局与局部组件，为大语言模型策略优化提供统一的多尺度稳定性控制。为增强架构稀疏性，模型包含480亿总参数而每前向传播仅激活27亿参数，实现了远高于同规模当代行业领先模型的稀疏比。为进一步提升推理吞吐量，我们采用联合训练-推理协同设计，融合了密集多令牌预测与量化感知训练。我们在Hugging Face平台开源JoyAI-LLM-48B-A3B基础模型及其训练后变体的检查点，以支持开源社区。

The paper introduces JoyAI-LLM Flash, a Mixture-of-Experts model designed to enhance performance and token efficiency for mid-scale language models under 50B parameters. The method involves pretraining on 20 trillion tokens followed by a post-training pipeline including SFT, DPO, and a novel RL algorithm called FiberPO for stable optimization, alongside architectural sparsity to activate only 2.7B parameters per inference and techniques like multi-token prediction for throughput. Experimental results show the model achieves high sparsity ratios and improved inference efficiency compared to industry-leading models of similar scale, with checkpoints released openly.

Adaptive Replay Buffer for Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chihyeon Song, Jaewoo Lee, Jinkyoo Park
First: 2025-12-11T10:30:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T06:04:45+00:00
Comments: AISTATS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning (O2O RL) faces a critical dilemma in balancing the use of a fixed offline dataset with newly collected online experiences. Standard methods, often relying on a fixed data-mixing ratio, struggle to manage the trade-off between early learning stability and asymptotic performance. To overcome this, we introduce the Adaptive Replay Buffer (ARB), a novel approach that dynamically prioritizes data sampling based on a lightweight metric we call 'on-policyness'. Unlike prior methods that rely on complex learning procedures or fixed ratios, ARB is designed to be learning-free and simple to implement, seamlessly integrating into existing O2O RL algorithms. It assesses how closely collected trajectories align with the current policy's behavior and assigns a proportional sampling weight to each transition within that trajectory. This strategy effectively leverages offline data for initial stability while progressively focusing learning on the most relevant, high-rewarding online experiences. Our extensive experiments on D4RL benchmarks demonstrate that ARB consistently mitigates early performance degradation and significantly improves the final performance of various O2O RL algorithms, highlighting the importance of an adaptive, behavior-aware replay buffer design. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/song970407/ARB.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离线到在线强化学习的自适应回放缓冲区
离线到在线强化学习（O2O RL）面临一个关键困境：如何在利用固定离线数据集与新收集的在线经验之间取得平衡。标准方法通常依赖固定的数据混合比例，难以在早期学习稳定性与渐进性能之间进行权衡。为此，我们提出了自适应回放缓冲区（ARB），这是一种基于轻量级指标“策略一致性”动态优先数据采样的新方法。与依赖复杂学习过程或固定比例的先前方法不同，ARB无需额外学习且易于实现，可无缝集成到现有O2O RL算法中。它评估收集的轨迹与当前策略行为的匹配程度，并为轨迹中的每个转移分配相应的采样权重。该策略有效利用离线数据确保初始稳定性，同时逐步将学习聚焦于最相关、高回报的在线经验。我们在D4RL基准测试上的大量实验表明，ARB能持续缓解早期性能下降，并显著提升多种O2O RL算法的最终性能，凸显了自适应、行为感知的回放缓冲区设计的重要性。代码已公开于https://github.com/song970407/ARB。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge in Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning (O2O RL) of balancing a fixed offline dataset with new online experiences, where standard fixed-ratio methods fail to optimize both early stability and final performance. The authors propose the Adaptive Replay Buffer (ARB), a simple, learning-free method that dynamically prioritizes data sampling using a lightweight 'on-policyness' metric, which measures how closely trajectories align with the current policy's behavior to assign sampling weights. Experimental results on D4RL benchmarks show that ARB consistently reduces early performance drops and significantly enhances the final performance of various O2O RL algorithms, underscoring the value of an adaptive, behavior-aware buffer design.
本文针对离线到在线强化学习（O2O RL）中平衡固定离线数据集与新在线经验的难题，指出标准固定混合比率方法难以兼顾早期学习稳定性和最终性能。作者提出了自适应回放缓冲区（ARB），这是一种简单、无需额外学习的轻量级方法，它通过“策略一致性”指标动态调整数据采样优先级，该指标评估轨迹与当前策略行为的匹配程度以分配采样权重。在D4RL基准测试上的实验结果表明，ARB能有效缓解早期性能下降，并显著提升多种O2O RL算法的最终性能，证明了自适应、行为感知缓冲区设计的重要性。
GIFT: Group-Relative Implicit Fine-Tuning Integrates GRPO with DPO and UNA
Authors: Zhichao Wang
First: 2025-10-27T21:18:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T05:55:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper proposes \textit{Group-relative Implicit Fine-Tuning (GIFT)}, a reinforcement learning framework for aligning large language models (LLMs) that unifies on-policy optimization with implicit preference learning. GIFT combines three key elements: (1) group-based sampling and normalization from GRPO, (2) the implicit reward formulation of DPO, and (3) the training principle underlying UNA. The central idea is to transform reward maximization into a \textit{group-wise reward matching problem}. By jointly normalizing implicit and explicit rewards within each sampled group, GIFT eliminates the intractable normalization constant associated with implicit rewards and reduces sensitivity to the KL-regularization coefficient through normalization. This yields a simple mean squared error (MSE) objective between normalized implicit and explicit reward functions, providing a stable and analytically tractable training signal. Unlike offline approaches such as DPO and UNA, GIFT retains on-policy exploration through on-policy response sampling. Compared to GRPO, it replaces high-variance reward maximization with structured reward matching, simplifying optimization and reducing sensitivity to hyperparameters. GIFT is evaluated across both RLHF and RLVR settings on models ranging from 7B to 32B parameters. Results show that GIFT converges faster, generalizes better with reduced overfitting, and outperforms GRPO on mathematical reasoning benchmarks (GSM8K, MATH, AIME) as well as generation tasks' evaluations (AlpacaEval and Arena-Hard).
中文标题/摘要
标题：GIFT：基于组相对隐式微调整合GRPO、DPO与UNA
本文提出\textit{组相对隐式微调（GIFT）}，一种用于对齐大语言模型（LLM）的强化学习框架，它将同策略优化与隐式偏好学习相统一。GIFT融合了三个关键要素：（1）GRPO的基于组采样与归一化，（2）DPO的隐式奖励构建，（3）UNA的训练原理。其核心思想是将奖励最大化转化为\textit{组间奖励匹配问题}。通过对每个采样组内的隐式与显式奖励进行联合归一化，GIFT消除了隐式奖励中难以处理的归一化常数，并通过归一化降低了对KL正则化系数的敏感性。这产生了一个简单的归一化隐式与显式奖励函数之间的均方误差（MSE）目标，提供了稳定且可解析处理的训练信号。与DPO、UNA等离线方法不同，GIFT通过同策略响应采样保留了同策略探索能力。相较于GRPO，它以结构化奖励匹配替代了高方差的奖励最大化，从而简化了优化过程并降低了对超参数的敏感性。GIFT在RLHF和RLVR两种设置下，对7B至32B参数规模的模型进行了评估。结果表明，GIFT收敛更快、泛化能力更强且过拟合减少，在数学推理基准（GSM8K、MATH、AIME）以及生成任务评估（AlpacaEval和Arena-Hard）上均优于GRPO。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces GIFT, a reinforcement learning framework designed to unify on-policy optimization with implicit preference learning for aligning large language models, motivated by the need to combine the strengths of existing methods like GRPO, DPO, and UNA while addressing their limitations. The method transforms reward maximization into a group-wise reward matching problem by jointly normalizing implicit and explicit rewards within sampled groups, which eliminates intractable normalization constants and reduces sensitivity to hyperparameters, resulting in a stable mean squared error objective. Experimental results on models from 7B to 32B parameters in RLHF and RLVR settings demonstrate that GIFT converges faster, generalizes better with less overfitting, and outperforms GRPO on mathematical reasoning benchmarks such as GSM8K, MATH, and AIME, as well as on generation tasks like AlpacaEval and Arena-Hard.
本文提出了GIFT，一种强化学习框架，旨在统一策略优化与隐式偏好学习以对齐大语言模型，其动机在于结合GRPO、DPO和UNA等现有方法的优势并克服其局限性。该方法通过将奖励最大化转化为组间奖励匹配问题，在采样组内联合归一化隐式和显式奖励，从而消除了难以处理的归一化常数并降低了对超参数的敏感性，形成了一个稳定的均方误差目标。在7B至32B参数模型的RLHF和RLVR设置中的实验结果表明，GIFT收敛更快、泛化能力更强且过拟合减少，在数学推理基准（如GSM8K、MATH和AIME）以及生成任务评估（如AlpacaEval和Arena-Hard）上均优于GRPO。
KD-MARL: Resource-Aware Knowledge Distillation in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Monirul Islam Pavel, Siyi Hu, Muhammad Anwar Masum, Mahardhika Pratama, Ryszard Kowalczyk, Zehong Jimmy Cao
First: 2026-04-08T05:12:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T05:12:40+00:00
Comments: Accepted in IJCNN 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Real world deployment of multi agent reinforcement learning MARL systems is fundamentally constrained by limited compute memory and inference time. While expert policies achieve high performance they rely on costly decision cycles and large scale models that are impractical for edge devices or embedded platforms. Knowledge distillation KD offers a promising path toward resource aware execution but existing KD methods in MARL focus narrowly on action imitation often neglecting coordination structure and assuming uniform agent capabilities. We propose resource aware Knowledge Distillation for Multi Agent Reinforcement Learning KD MARL a two stage framework that transfers coordinated behavior from a centralized expert to lightweight decentralized student agents. The student policies are trained without a critic relying instead on distilled advantage signals and structured policy supervision to preserve coordination under heterogeneous and limited observations. Our approach transfers both action level behavior and structural coordination patterns from expert policies while supporting heterogeneous student architectures allowing each agent model capacity to match its observation complexity which is crucial for efficient execution under partial or limited observability and limited onboard resources. Extensive experiments on SMAC and MPE benchmarks demonstrate that KD MARL achieves high performance retention while substantially reducing computational cost. Across standard multi agent benchmarks KD MARL retains over 90 percent of expert performance while reducing computational cost by up to 28.6 times FLOPs. The proposed approach achieves expert level coordination and preserves it through structured distillation enabling practical MARL deployment across resource constrained onboard platforms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KD-MARL：多智能体强化学习中的资源感知知识蒸馏
多智能体强化学习（MARL）系统的实际部署从根本上受限于有限的计算内存和推理时间。专家策略虽能实现高性能，但依赖昂贵的决策周期和大规模模型，难以在边缘设备或嵌入式平台上实用。知识蒸馏（KD）为资源感知执行提供了可行路径，但现有MARL中的KD方法多局限于动作模仿，常忽略协调结构并假设智能体能力同质。本文提出面向多智能体强化学习的资源感知知识蒸馏框架（KD-MARL），通过两阶段框架将集中式专家的协调行为迁移至轻量级分散式学生智能体。学生策略无需评论家网络，而是依赖蒸馏的优势信号与结构化策略监督，在异构且受限的观测条件下保持协调能力。该方法同时迁移专家策略的动作级行为与结构协调模式，支持异构学生架构，使各智能体模型容量与其观测复杂度相匹配——这对部分可观测、资源受限场景的高效执行至关重要。在SMAC和MPE基准上的大量实验表明，KD-MARL在显著降低计算成本的同时保持了高性能。在标准多智能体基准中，KD-MARL保留超过90%的专家性能，计算成本最高降低28.6倍（FLOPs）。所提方法实现了专家级协调能力，并通过结构化蒸馏保持该能力，为资源受限的嵌入式平台部署实用MARL系统提供了可能。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the practical constraints of deploying multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) systems on resource-limited edge devices, where expert policies are computationally expensive. The method introduces KD-MARL, a two-stage knowledge distillation framework that transfers coordinated behavior from a centralized expert to decentralized, lightweight student agents by using distilled advantage signals and structured policy supervision, without relying on a critic, and supports heterogeneous student architectures tailored to observation complexity. Experimental results on SMAC and MPE benchmarks show that KD-MARL retains over 90% of expert performance while reducing computational cost by up to 28.6 times in FLOPs, enabling efficient deployment on resource-constrained platforms.
本文的动机源于在资源受限的边缘设备上部署多智能体强化学习（MARL）系统的实际约束，其中专家策略计算成本高昂。方法提出了KD-MARL，一个两阶段的知识蒸馏框架，通过使用蒸馏的优势信号和结构化策略监督，将集中式专家的协调行为迁移到去中心化的轻量级学生智能体，且不依赖评论家，并支持根据观测复杂性定制的异构学生架构。在SMAC和MPE基准测试上的实验结果表明，KD-MARL保持了超过90%的专家性能，同时将计算成本降低高达28.6倍（以FLOPs计），从而实现了在资源受限平台上的高效部署。
DROP: Distributional and Regular Optimism and Pessimism for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Taisuke Kobayashi
First: 2024-10-22T23:14:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T04:40:56+00:00
Comments: 51 pages, 15 figures (accepted in Neural Computation)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In reinforcement learning (RL), temporal difference (TD) error is known to be related to the firing rate of dopamine neurons. It has been observed that each dopamine neuron does not behave uniformly, but each responds to the TD error in an optimistic or pessimistic manner, interpreted as a kind of distributional RL. To explain such a biological data, a heuristic model has also been introduced with learning rates asymmetric for the positive and negative TD errors. However, this heuristic model is not theoretically-grounded and unknown whether it can work as a RL algorithm. This paper therefore introduces a novel theoretically-grounded model with optimism and pessimism, which is derived from control as inference. In combination with ensemble learning, a distributional value function as a critic is estimated from regularly introduced optimism and pessimism. Based on its central value, a policy in an actor is improved. This proposed algorithm, so-called DROP (distributional and regular optimism and pessimism), is compared on dynamic tasks. Although the heuristic model showed poor learning performance, DROP demonstrated excellent performance in all tasks with high generality. In addition, DROP achieved learning performance comparable to the state-of-the-art algorithms. In other words, it was suggested that DROP is a new model that can elicit the potential contributions of optimism and pessimism.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DROP：强化学习中的分布性与规则性乐观悲观机制
在强化学习（RL）中，时序差分（TD）误差已知与多巴胺神经元的放电频率相关。研究发现，多巴胺神经元并非统一响应，而是各自以乐观或悲观的方式对TD误差作出反应，这被解释为一种分布性强化学习。为解释此类生物学数据，已有研究引入启发式模型，该模型对正负TD误差采用不对称的学习率。然而，该启发式模型缺乏理论依据，且其能否作为强化学习算法尚不明确。为此，本文基于“推断即控制”框架，提出一种具有理论基础的乐观悲观新模型。结合集成学习方法，通过规则性引入的乐观与悲观机制估计作为评论家的分布性价值函数，并基于其中心值改进执行器中的策略。所提出的算法称为DROP（分布性与规则性乐观悲观机制），在动态任务中进行了性能比较。结果显示，启发式模型学习性能较差，而DROP在所有任务中均表现出优异的泛化性能，且达到与前沿算法相当的学习效果。这表明DROP是一种能充分发挥乐观与悲观机制潜在贡献的新模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by biological observations that dopamine neurons exhibit optimistic or pessimistic responses to temporal difference errors, this paper addresses the lack of a theoretically-grounded reinforcement learning model capturing such distributional properties. The method introduces DROP, a novel algorithm derived from control as inference, which combines ensemble learning to estimate a distributional value function through regularly introduced optimism and pessimism, and uses its central value to improve the actor's policy. Experimental results on dynamic tasks show that DROP outperforms a heuristic baseline, achieves high generality across tasks, and performs comparably to state-of-the-art algorithms, demonstrating its potential to effectively leverage optimism and pessimism in reinforcement learning.
本文受生物学观察启发，即多巴胺神经元对时序差分误差表现出乐观或悲观的响应，旨在解决现有启发式模型缺乏理论基础的不足。方法上提出了DROP算法，该算法基于控制即推断理论推导，结合集成学习通过定期引入乐观和悲观来估计分布式的价值函数，并利用其中心值优化行动者策略。实验结果表明，在动态任务中，DROP相比启发式模型表现出更优的学习性能，具有较高的通用性，且与最先进算法性能相当，表明其能有效挖掘乐观与悲观在强化学习中的潜力。
Rethinking Generalization in Reasoning SFT: A Conditional Analysis on Optimization, Data, and Model Capability
Authors: Qihan Ren, Peng Wang, Ruikun Cai, Shuai Shao, Dadi Guo, Yuejin Xie, Yafu Li, Quanshi Zhang, Xia Hu, Jing Shao, Dongrui Liu
First: 2026-04-08T03:11:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T03:11:16+00:00
Comments: Preprint. Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A prevailing narrative in LLM post-training holds that supervised finetuning (SFT) memorizes while reinforcement learning (RL) generalizes. We revisit this claim for reasoning SFT with long chain-of-thought (CoT) supervision and find that cross-domain generalization is not absent but conditional, jointly shaped by optimization dynamics, training data, and base-model capability. Some reported failures are under-optimization artifacts: cross-domain performance first degrades before recovering and improving with extended training (a dip-and-recovery pattern), so shorttraining checkpoints can underestimate generalization. Data quality and structure both matter: low-quality solutions broadly hurt generalization,while verified long-CoT traces yield consistent cross-domain gains. Model capability is essential: stronger models internalize transferable procedural patterns (e.g., backtracking) even from a toy arithmetic game, while weaker ones imitate surface verbosity. This generalization is asymmetric, however: reasoning improves while safety degrades, reframing the question from whether reasoning SFT generalizes to under what conditions and at what cost.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重新审视推理监督微调中的泛化问题：基于优化、数据与模型能力的条件性分析
当前大语言模型后训练的主流观点认为：监督微调（SFT）导致记忆，而强化学习（RL）促进泛化。本研究针对带有长思维链（CoT）监督的推理SFT重新检验这一论断，发现跨领域泛化并非缺失，而是具有条件性——其表现由优化动态、训练数据和基座模型能力共同塑造。部分已报道的失败案例实为欠优化假象：跨领域性能在训练初期下降，随后随训练延长恢复并提升（呈现“先降后升”模式），因此短期训练检查点可能低估泛化能力。数据质量与结构均至关重要：低质量解决方案普遍损害泛化，而经过验证的长思维链轨迹能带来稳定的跨领域增益。模型能力具有决定性：强模型即使从简单算术游戏中也能内化可迁移的程序性模式（如回溯策略），而弱模型仅模仿表面冗余表达。需注意的是，这种泛化具有不对称性：推理能力提升的同时安全性可能下降，这促使我们重新思考问题——不应再问“推理SFT是否泛化”，而应探究“在何种条件下、以何种代价实现泛化”。
Summary / 总结
This paper challenges the prevailing view that supervised fine-tuning (SFT) merely memorizes while reinforcement learning (RL) generalizes, specifically in the context of reasoning tasks with long chain-of-thought supervision. The authors demonstrate that cross-domain generalization in reasoning SFT is conditional, influenced jointly by optimization dynamics, training data quality, and base-model capability. Key experimental findings reveal that insufficient training can create artifacts where generalization initially dips before recovering with extended training, that high-quality verified reasoning traces consistently improve cross-domain performance, and that stronger base models learn transferable procedural patterns rather than superficial features. However, this generalization is asymmetric, often improving reasoning at the cost of degrading safety, shifting the research question to understanding the specific conditions and trade-offs involved.
本文挑战了当前主流观点，即监督微调（SFT）仅导致记忆而强化学习（RL）促进泛化，特别是在具有长思维链监督的推理任务背景下。研究表明，推理SFT的跨领域泛化是有条件的，共同受优化动态、训练数据质量和基础模型能力的影响。主要实验结果发现，训练不足会导致泛化性能先下降后恢复的假象，高质量验证过的推理轨迹能持续提升跨领域表现，且更强的基础模型能学习可迁移的程序性模式而非表面特征。然而，这种泛化是不对称的，常在提升推理能力的同时损害安全性，从而将研究问题转向理解具体条件与代价。
RLBoost: Harvesting Preemptible Resources for Cost-Efficient Reinforcement Learning on LLMs
Authors: Yongji Wu, Xueshen Liu, Haizhong Zheng, Juncheng Gu, Beidi Chen, Z. Morley Mao, Arvind Krishnamurthy, Ion Stoica
First: 2025-10-22T04:19:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T03:04:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become essential for unlocking advanced reasoning capabilities in large language models (LLMs). RL workflows involve interleaving rollout and training stages with fundamentally different resource requirements. Rollout typically dominates overall execution time, yet scales efficiently through multiple independent instances. In contrast, training requires tightly-coupled GPUs with full-mesh communication. Existing RL frameworks fall into two categories: co-located and disaggregated architectures. Co-located frameworks fail to address this resource tension by forcing both stages to share the same GPUs. Disaggregated architectures, without modifications of well-established RL algorithms, suffer from resource under-utilization. Meanwhile, preemptible GPU resources, i.e., spot instances on public clouds and spare capacity in production clusters, present significant cost-saving opportunities for accelerating RL workflows, if efficiently harvested for rollout. In this paper, we present RLBoost, a framework for cost-efficient RL training that harvests preemptible GPU resources. Our key insight is that rollout's stateless and embarrassingly parallel nature aligns perfectly with preemptible and often fragmented resources. To efficiently utilize these resources despite frequent and unpredictable availability changes, RLBoost adopts a hybrid architecture with three key techniques: (1) adaptive rollout offload to dynamically adjust workloads on the reserved (on-demand) cluster, (2) pull-based weight transfer that quickly provisions newly available instances, and (3) token-level response collection and migration for efficient preemption handling and continuous load balancing. Extensive experiments show RLBoost increases training throughput by 1.51x-1.97x while improving cost efficiency by 28%-49% compared to using only on-demand GPU resources.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLBoost：利用抢占式资源实现大语言模型强化学习的成本效益优化
强化学习已成为解锁大语言模型高级推理能力的关键技术。其工作流程包含资源需求迥异的两个阶段：耗时占主导但可通过多独立实例高效扩展的轨迹生成阶段，以及需要全互联通信的紧耦合GPU训练阶段。现有RL框架分为两类：同构架构强制两阶段共享GPU资源，无法解决资源冲突；异构架构虽分离资源，但未优化经典算法时易导致资源利用率不足。与此同时，抢占式GPU资源（如公有云竞价实例与生产集群闲置资源）为加速RL工作流提供了显著的成本节约潜力。本文提出RLBoost框架，通过高效利用抢占式GPU资源实现成本效益优化的RL训练。其核心洞见在于：轨迹生成阶段的无状态性与高度并行性，与抢占式资源的高度动态性天然契合。为应对资源可用性的频繁波动，RLBoost采用混合架构并集成三项关键技术：（1）自适应轨迹卸载动态调整预留集群负载；（2）基于拉取的权重快速部署新可用实例；（3）令牌级响应收集与迁移机制，实现高效抢占处理与持续负载均衡。实验表明，相较于仅使用按需GPU资源，RLBoost将训练吞吐量提升1.51-1.97倍，同时提高成本效益28%-49%。

The paper is motivated by the high cost and resource inefficiency of reinforcement learning (RL) workflows for large language models, which involve distinct rollout and training stages with conflicting resource demands, and by the opportunity to leverage low-cost preemptible GPU resources. The method introduces RLBoost, a framework that harvests preemptible resources for the parallelizable rollout stage through a hybrid architecture featuring adaptive rollout offload, pull-based weight transfer, and token-level response collection and migration to handle resource volatility. Experimental results demonstrate that RLBoost increases training throughput by 1.51x to 1.97x and improves cost efficiency by 28% to 49% compared to using only on-demand GPU resources.
本文的动机在于大型语言模型的强化学习工作流程成本高昂且资源效率低下，其包含资源需求冲突的并行化rollout和集中式训练阶段，同时存在利用低成本可抢占GPU资源的机会。方法上提出了RLBoost框架，通过混合架构来为可并行rollout阶段收割可抢占资源，其关键技术包括自适应rollout卸载、基于拉取的权重转移以及令牌级响应收集与迁移，以应对资源波动。实验结果表明，与仅使用按需GPU资源相比，RLBoost将训练吞吐量提高了1.51倍至1.97倍，并将成本效率提升了28%至49%。
The Theorems of Dr. David Blackwell and Their Contributions to Artificial Intelligence
Authors: Napoleon Paxton
First: 2026-04-08T03:01:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T03:01:58+00:00
Comments: Survey article, 19 pages, 1 figure, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Dr. David Blackwell was a mathematician and statistician of the first rank, whose contributions to statistical theory, game theory, and decision theory predated many of the algorithmic breakthroughs that define modern artificial intelligence. This survey examines three of his most consequential theoretical results the Rao Blackwell theorem, the Blackwell Approachability theorem, and the Blackwell Informativeness theorem (comparison of experiments) and traces their direct influence on contemporary AI and machine learning. We show that these results, developed primarily in the 1940s and 1950s, remain technically live across modern subfields including Markov Chain Monte Carlo inference, autonomous mobile robot navigation (SLAM), generative model training, no-regret online learning, reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), large language model alignment, and information design. NVIDIAs 2024 decision to name their flagship GPU architecture (Blackwell) provides vivid testament to his enduring relevance. We also document an emerging frontier: explicit Rao Blackwellized variance reduction in LLM RLHF pipelines, recently proposed but not yet standard practice. Together, Blackwell theorems form a unified framework addressing information compression, sequential decision making under uncertainty, and the comparison of information sources precisely the problems at the core of modern AI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大卫·布莱克威尔博士的定理及其对人工智能的贡献
大卫·布莱克威尔博士是一位顶尖的数学家和统计学家，他在统计理论、博弈论和决策论方面的贡献早于许多定义现代人工智能的算法突破。本文综述了他三项最具影响力的理论成果——拉奥-布莱克威尔定理、布莱克威尔可逼近性定理和布莱克威尔信息量定理（实验比较），并追溯了它们对当代人工智能和机器学习的直接影响。研究表明，这些主要形成于1940-1950年代的成果，至今仍在马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛推断、自主移动机器人导航（SLAM）、生成模型训练、无悔在线学习、人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）、大语言模型对齐和信息设计等现代子领域保持技术活力。英伟达2024年将其旗舰GPU架构命名为“布莱克威尔”，生动印证了其持久影响力。本文还记录了一个新兴前沿：LLM RLHF流程中显式的拉奥-布莱克威尔化方差缩减方法，该方案近期被提出但尚未成为标准实践。总体而言，布莱克威尔定理构成了一个统一框架，专门解决信息压缩、不确定性下的序列决策以及信源比较——这些正是现代人工智能核心问题。
Summary / 总结
This survey article is motivated by the need to highlight the foundational yet often overlooked theoretical contributions of Dr. David Blackwell to modern artificial intelligence. The method involves examining three of his key theorems—the Rao-Blackwell theorem, the Blackwell Approachability theorem, and the Blackwell Informativeness theorem—and tracing their direct influence. The main experimental results, as documented, show these theorems remain technically vital across contemporary AI subfields, including Markov Chain Monte Carlo inference, reinforcement learning from human feedback, and large language model alignment, with emerging applications like variance reduction in RLHF pipelines further demonstrating their enduring relevance.
本综述文章的动机在于强调大卫·布莱克威尔博士对现代人工智能的基础性但常被忽视的理论贡献。方法涉及审视他的三个关键定理——拉奥-布莱克威尔定理、布莱克威尔可逼近性定理和布莱克威尔信息性定理——并追溯其直接影响。主要实验结果，如文献所载，表明这些定理在当代人工智能子领域，包括马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛推断、基于人类反馈的强化学习和大型语言模型对齐中，仍具有技术上的关键作用，而像在RLHF流程中方差减少等新兴应用进一步证明了其持久的现实意义。
TwinLoop: Simulation-in-the-Loop Digital Twins for Online Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Nan Zhang, Zishuo Wang, Shuyu Huang, Georgios Diamantopoulos, Nikos Tziritas, Panagiotis Oikonomou, Georgios Theodoropoulos
First: 2026-04-08T02:43:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-08T02:43:04+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decentralised online learning enables runtime adaptation in cyber-physical multi-agent systems, but when operating conditions change, learned policies often require substantial trial-and-error interaction before recovering performance. To address this, we propose TwinLoop, a simulation-in-the-loop digital twin framework for online multi-agent reinforcement learning. When a context shift occurs, the digital twin is triggered to reconstruct the current system state, initialise from the latest agent policies, and perform accelerated policy improvement with simulation what-if analysis before synchronising updated parameters back to the agents in the physical system. We evaluate TwinLoop in a vehicular edge computing task-offloading scenario with changing workload and infrastructure conditions. The results suggest that digital twins can improve post-shift adaptation efficiency and reduce reliance on costly online trial-and-error.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TwinLoop：面向在线多智能体强化学习的仿真在环数字孪生框架
去中心化在线学习支持信息物理多智能体系统的运行时自适应，但当运行条件变化时，习得策略往往需要大量试错交互才能恢复性能。为此，我们提出TwinLoop——一种面向在线多智能体强化学习的仿真在环数字孪生框架。当发生情境偏移时，数字孪生被触发以重构当前系统状态，基于最新智能体策略初始化，并通过仿真假设分析进行加速策略改进，再将更新后的参数同步回物理系统中的智能体。我们在工作负载与基础设施条件动态变化的车载边缘计算任务卸载场景中评估TwinLoop。结果表明，数字孪生能提升偏移后的自适应效率，并减少对高成本在线试错的依赖。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge that decentralized online multi-agent reinforcement learning systems often require extensive trial-and-error to recover performance after operational context shifts, which is costly in cyber-physical settings. To address this, the authors propose TwinLoop, a framework that integrates a simulation-in-the-loop digital twin; when a shift is detected, the twin reconstructs the system state, initializes with current agent policies, and accelerates policy improvement through simulated what-if analysis before synchronizing updates back to the physical agents. Experimental evaluation in a vehicular edge computing task-offloading scenario with dynamic workload and infrastructure conditions shows that TwinLoop enhances adaptation efficiency after shifts and reduces reliance on expensive online trial-and-error interactions.
本文的动机在于解决去中心化在线多智能体强化学习系统在运行条件变化后，通常需要大量试错交互才能恢复性能的问题，这在网络物理系统中成本高昂。为此，作者提出了TwinLoop框架，它集成了一个仿真在环的数字孪生；当检测到环境变化时，该数字孪生会重建系统状态，基于最新智能体策略初始化，并通过仿真假设分析加速策略改进，然后将更新后的参数同步回物理系统中的智能体。在车辆边缘计算任务卸载场景中，针对工作负载和基础设施条件变化的实验结果表明，TwinLoop能提高环境变化后的适应效率，并减少对昂贵在线试错交互的依赖。
Soft-Quantum Algorithms
Authors: Basil Kyriacou, Mo Kordzanganeh, Maniraman Periyasamy, Alexey Melnikov
First: 2026-04-07T23:30:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T23:30:40+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 6 figures, 0 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Quantum operations on pure states can be fully represented by unitary matrices. Variational quantum circuits, also known as quantum neural networks, embed data and trainable parameters into gate-based operations and optimize the parameters via gradient descent. The high cost of training and low fidelity of current quantum devices, however, restricts much of quantum machine learning to classical simulation. For few-qubit problems with large datasets, training the matrix elements directly, as is done with weight matrices in classical neural networks, can be faster than decomposing data and parameters into gates. We propose a method that trains matrices directly while maintaining unitarity through a single regularization term added to the loss function. A second training step, circuit alignment, then recovers a gate-based architecture from the resulting soft-unitary. On a five-qubit supervised classification task with 1000 datapoints, this two-step process produces a trained variational circuit in under four minutes, compared to over two hours for direct circuit training, while achieving lower binary cross-entropy loss. In a second experiment, soft-unitaries are embedded in a hybrid quantum-classical network for a reinforcement learning cartpole task, where the hybrid agent outperforms a purely classical baseline of comparable size.
中文标题/摘要
标题：软量子算法
纯态上的量子操作可由酉矩阵完全表示。变分量子电路（亦称量子神经网络）将数据和可训练参数嵌入基于门的操作中，并通过梯度下降优化参数。然而，当前量子设备的高训练成本和低保真度限制了量子机器学习多依赖于经典模拟。对于具有大数据集的少量子比特问题，直接训练矩阵元素（类似经典神经网络中的权重矩阵）可能比将数据和参数分解为门操作更快。我们提出一种方法，通过在损失函数中添加单一正则化项，在直接训练矩阵的同时保持酉性。随后通过电路对齐的第二步训练，从所得软酉矩阵恢复出基于门的架构。在包含1000个数据点的五量子比特监督分类任务中，这一两步流程在四分钟内完成变分电路训练，而直接电路训练需两小时以上，且实现了更低的二元交叉熵损失。在第二个实验中，软酉矩阵被嵌入混合量子-经典网络，用于强化学习小车倒立摆任务，该混合智能体在可比规模下超越了纯经典基线。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high training costs and low fidelity of current quantum hardware, which limit quantum machine learning to classical simulation, this paper proposes a method called soft-quantum algorithms that directly trains matrices while ensuring unitarity via a regularization term in the loss function, followed by a circuit alignment step to recover a gate-based architecture. The main experimental results show that on a five-qubit classification task with 1000 datapoints, this two-step process trains a variational circuit in under four minutes, significantly faster than the over two hours required for direct circuit training, while achieving lower binary cross-entropy loss, and in a reinforcement learning cartpole task, a hybrid network embedding soft-unitaries outperforms a comparable classical baseline.
针对当前量子硬件训练成本高、保真度低，导致量子机器学习多限于经典模拟的问题，本文提出了一种称为软量子算法的方法，该方法通过在损失函数中添加正则化项直接训练矩阵并保持酉性，随后通过电路对齐步骤恢复基于门的架构。主要实验结果表明，在一个包含1000个数据点的五量子比特分类任务中，这一两步过程在四分钟内训练出变分电路，远快于直接电路训练所需的两个多小时，且实现了更低的二元交叉熵损失；在强化学习倒立摆任务中，嵌入软酉矩阵的混合网络性能优于规模相当的纯经典基线。
Discrete Flow Matching Policy Optimization
Authors: Maojiang Su, Po-Chung Hsieh, Weimin Wu, Mingcheng Lu, Jiunhau Chen, Jerry Yao-Chieh Hu, Han Liu
First: 2026-04-07T21:49:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T21:49:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Discrete flow Matching policy Optimization (DoMinO), a unified framework for Reinforcement Learning (RL) fine-tuning Discrete Flow Matching (DFM) models under a broad class of policy gradient methods. Our key idea is to view the DFM sampling procedure as a multi-step Markov Decision Process. This perspective provides a simple and transparent reformulation of fine-tuning reward maximization as a robust RL objective. Consequently, it not only preserves the original DFM samplers but also avoids biased auxiliary estimators and likelihood surrogates used by many prior RL fine-tuning methods. To prevent policy collapse, we also introduce new total-variation regularizers to keep the fine-tuned distribution close to the pretrained one. Theoretically, we establish an upper bound on the discretization error of DoMinO and tractable upper bounds for the regularizers. Experimentally, we evaluate DoMinO on regulatory DNA sequence design. DoMinO achieves stronger predicted enhancer activity and better sequence naturalness than the previous best reward-driven baselines. The regularization further improves alignment with the natural sequence distribution while preserving strong functional performance. These results establish DoMinO as an useful framework for controllable discrete sequence generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：离散流匹配策略优化
我们提出了离散流匹配策略优化（DoMinO），这是一个在广泛策略梯度方法下对离散流匹配（DFM）模型进行强化学习（RL）微调的统一框架。核心思想是将DFM采样过程视为多步马尔可夫决策过程，从而将奖励最大化的微调目标简洁透明地重构为稳健的RL目标。该方法不仅保留了原始DFM采样器，还避免了先前许多RL微调方法中使用的有偏辅助估计器和似然替代。为防止策略崩溃，我们引入了新的全变差正则化器，使微调后的分布接近预训练分布。理论上，我们建立了DoMinO离散化误差的上界以及正则化器的可处理上界。实验部分，我们在调控DNA序列设计任务上评估DoMinO，其预测增强子活性和序列自然度均优于先前最佳的奖励驱动基线。正则化进一步提升了与自然序列分布的对齐性，同时保持了强大的功能性能。这些结果表明DoMinO是可控离散序列生成的有效框架。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Discrete Flow Matching Policy Optimization (DoMinO), motivated by the need to fine-tune Discrete Flow Matching (DFM) models for reinforcement learning tasks, particularly in controllable discrete sequence generation. The method reframes DFM sampling as a multi-step Markov Decision Process, enabling a straightforward RL objective that avoids biased estimators and likelihood surrogates while preserving original DFM samplers, and incorporates total-variation regularizers to prevent policy collapse by keeping the fine-tuned distribution close to the pretrained one. Experimental results on regulatory DNA sequence design show that DoMinO outperforms prior reward-driven baselines in predicted enhancer activity and sequence naturalness, with regularization further improving alignment to natural distributions without compromising functional performance.
本文提出了离散流匹配策略优化（DoMinO），其动机在于需要对离散流匹配（DFM）模型进行强化学习微调，特别是在可控离散序列生成任务中。该方法将DFM采样重新构建为多步马尔可夫决策过程，从而形成一个直接的强化学习目标，避免了有偏估计器和似然替代物，同时保留了原始DFM采样器，并引入了总变差正则化器以防止策略崩溃，使微调后的分布接近预训练分布。在调控DNA序列设计上的实验结果表明，DoMinO在预测增强子活性和序列自然性方面优于先前的奖励驱动基线，正则化进一步提高了与自然序列分布的对齐性，且未损害功能性能。
Non-Expansive Mappings in Two-Time-Scale Stochastic Approximation: Finite-Time Analysis
Authors: Siddharth Chandak
First: 2025-01-18T16:00:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-07T21:37:47+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication to SIAM Journal on Control and Optimization
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Two-time-scale stochastic approximation algorithms are iterative methods used in applications such as optimization, reinforcement learning, and control. Finite-time analysis of these algorithms has primarily focused on fixed point iterations where both time-scales have contractive mappings. In this work, we broaden the scope of such analyses by considering settings where the slower time-scale has a non-expansive mapping. For such algorithms, the slower time-scale can be viewed as a stochastic inexact Krasnoselskii-Mann iteration. We also study a variant where the faster time-scale has a projection step which leads to non-expansiveness in the slower time-scale. We show that the last-iterate mean square residual error for such algorithms decays at a rate $O(1/k^{1/4-ε})$, where $ε>0$ is arbitrarily small. We further establish almost sure convergence of iterates to the set of fixed points. We demonstrate the applicability of our framework by applying our results to minimax optimization, linear stochastic approximation, and Lagrangian optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：双时间尺度随机逼近中的非扩张映射：有限时间分析
双时间尺度随机逼近算法是用于优化、强化学习和控制等领域的迭代方法。现有有限时间分析主要针对两个时间尺度均具有压缩映射的不动点迭代。本研究通过考虑较慢时间尺度具有非扩张映射的情形，拓展了此类分析的范围。此类算法中，较慢时间尺度可视为随机非精确Krasnoselskii-Mann迭代。我们还研究了较快时间尺度包含投影步骤导致较慢时间尺度非扩张的变体。证明此类算法的末次迭代均方残差以$O(1/k^{1/4-ε})$速率衰减（$ε>0$任意小），并建立迭代几乎必然收敛至不动点集的结论。通过将结果应用于极小极大优化、线性随机逼近和拉格朗日优化，展示了本框架的适用性。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to extend finite-time analysis of two-time-scale stochastic approximation algorithms beyond the restrictive assumption of contractive mappings, focusing instead on scenarios where the slower time-scale employs a non-expansive mapping. The method involves modeling the slower time-scale as a stochastic inexact Krasnoselskii-Mann iteration and also examines a variant incorporating a projection step in the faster time-scale that induces non-expansiveness. Experimentally, the authors prove that the last-iterate mean square residual error decays at a rate of O(1/k^{1/4-ε}) for arbitrarily small ε>0 and establish almost sure convergence of iterates to the fixed point set, with applications demonstrated in minimax optimization, linear stochastic approximation, and Lagrangian optimization.
本文的动机在于将双时间尺度随机逼近算法的有限时间分析从压缩映射的限制性假设扩展到更一般的情形，重点关注慢时间尺度采用非扩张映射的场景。方法上，将慢时间尺度建模为随机不精确的Krasnoselskii-Mann迭代，并研究了一种在快时间尺度引入投影步骤从而诱导非扩张性的变体。实验结果表明，算法最后迭代的均方残差误差以O(1/k^{1/4-ε})的速率衰减（其中ε>0可任意小），并证明了迭代几乎必然收敛到不动点集，其框架在极小极大优化、线性随机逼近和拉格朗日优化等应用中得到了验证。
